Step 1: GPU Monitoring eBPF Program
bpf/gpu.bpf.c
c -108 lines

// SPDX-License-Identifier: GPL-2.0
// GPU monitoring with eBPF
#include "core.bpf.h"
char LICENSE[] SEC("license") = "GPL";
// GPU event types
enum gpu_event_type {
    GPU_MEMORY_ALLOC = 1,
    GPU_MEMORY_FREE = 2,
    GPU_KERNEL_LAUNCH = 3,
    GPU_MEMCPY_H2D = 4,    // Host to Device
    GPU_MEMCPY_D2H = 5,    // Device to Host
    GPU_MEMCPY_D2D = 6,    // Device to Device
    GPU_SYNC = 7,
};
// GPU event structure
struct gpu_event {
    struct event_header hdr;
    u8 gpu_event_type;
    u32 device_id;
    u64 address;
    u64 size;
    u32 duration_us;
    // Kernel launch specific
    u32 grid_x;
    u32 grid_y;
    u32 grid_z;
    u32 block_x;
    u32 block_y;
    u32 block_z;
    u32 shared_memory;
    char kernel_name[64];
};
// GPU stats per process
struct gpu_stats {
    u64 memory_allocated;
    u64 memory_freed;
    u64 memory_current;
    u64 memory_peak;
    u64 kernel_launches;
    u64 memcpy_h2d_bytes;
    u64 memcpy_d2h_bytes;
    u64 total_kernel_time_us;
    u32 active_kernels;
};
// Per-device stats
struct device_stats {
    u64 total_memory_used;
    u64 total_kernel_launches;
    u32 active_processes;
};
// Maps
struct {
    __uint(type, BPF_MAP_TYPE_RINGBUF);
    __uint(max_entries, 512 * 1024);
} gpu_events SEC(".maps");
struct {
    __uint(type, BPF_MAP_TYPE_HASH);
    __uint(max_entries, 1024);
    __type(key, u32);  // PID
    __type(value, struct gpu_stats);
} process_gpu_stats SEC(".maps");
struct {
    __uint(type, BPF_MAP_TYPE_ARRAY);
    __uint(max_entries, 16);  // Support up to 16 GPUs
    __type(key, u32);         // Device ID
    __type(value, struct device_stats);
} device_gpu_stats SEC(".maps");
// Track kernel launch timing
struct {
    __uint(type, BPF_MAP_TYPE_HASH);
    __uint(max_entries, MAX_ENTRIES);
    __type(key, u64);  // Unique kernel ID
    __type(value, u64); // Start timestamp
} kernel_start_time SEC(".maps");
// Helper to update GPU stats
static __always_inline void update_gpu_stats(u32 pid, s64 memory_delta)
{
    struct gpu_stats *stats = bpf_map_lookup_elem(&process_gpu_stats, &pid);
    if (!stats) {
        struct gpu_stats new_stats = {};
        if (memory_delta > 0) {
            new_stats.memory_allocated = memory_delta;
            new_stats.memory_current = memory_delta;
            new_stats.memory_peak = memory_delta;
        }
        bpf_map_update_elem(&process_gpu_stats, &pid, &new_stats, BPF_ANY);
    } else {
        if (memory_delta > 0) {
            __sync_fetch_and_add(&stats->memory_allocated, memory_delta);
            __sync_fetch_and_add(&stats->memory_current, memory_delta);
            if (stats->memory_current > stats->memory_peak) {
                stats->memory_peak = stats->memory_current;
            }
        } else {
            __sync_fetch_and_add(&stats->memory_freed, -memory_delta);
            __sync_fetch_and_add(&stats->memory_current, memory_delta);
        }
    }
}
static __always_inline void emit_gpu_event(struct gpu_event *event)
{
    struct gpu_event *e;
    e = bpf_ringbuf_reserve(&gpu_events, sizeof(*e), 0);
    if (!e)
        return;
    __builtin_memcpy(e, event, sizeof(*event));
    bpf_ringbuf_submit(e, 0);
}




Step 2: CUDA API Tracing
bpf/cuda.bpf.c
c -242 lines

// SPDX-License-Identifier: GPL-2.0
// CUDA API tracing with eBPF
#include "core.bpf.h"
#include "gpu.bpf.c"  // Include GPU events
char LICENSE[] SEC("license") = "GPL";
// Track cudaMalloc
SEC("uprobe/libcudart.so:cudaMalloc")
int BPF_UPROBE(trace_cuda_malloc_enter, void **devPtr, size_t size)
{
    if (!should_trace_process())
        return 0;
    u64 id = bpf_get_current_pid_tgid();
    bpf_map_update_elem(&kernel_start_time, &id, &size, BPF_ANY);
    return 0;
}
SEC("uretprobe/libcudart.so:cudaMalloc")
int BPF_URETPROBE(trace_cuda_malloc_exit, int ret, void **devPtr)
{
    if (!should_trace_process())
        return 0;
    u64 id = bpf_get_current_pid_tgid();
    u32 pid = id >> 32;
    u64 *size_ptr = bpf_map_lookup_elem(&kernel_start_time, &id);
    if (!size_ptr)
        return 0;
    u64 size = *size_ptr;
    bpf_map_delete_elem(&kernel_start_time, &id);
    // Only track successful allocations
    if (ret != 0)
        return 0;
    // Create event
    struct gpu_event event = {};
    fill_event_header(&event.hdr, EVENT_MEMORY_ALLOC);
    event.gpu_event_type = GPU_MEMORY_ALLOC;
    event.size = size;
    // Read device pointer
    void *ptr;
    bpf_probe_read_user(&ptr, sizeof(ptr), devPtr);
    event.address = (u64)ptr;
    emit_gpu_event(&event);
    // Update stats
    update_gpu_stats(pid, size);
    return 0;
}
// Track cudaFree
SEC("uprobe/libcudart.so:cudaFree")
int BPF_UPROBE(trace_cuda_free, void *devPtr)
{
    if (!should_trace_process())
        return 0;
    u32 pid = bpf_get_current_pid_tgid() >> 32;
    struct gpu_event event = {};
    fill_event_header(&event.hdr, EVENT_MEMORY_FREE);
    event.gpu_event_type = GPU_MEMORY_FREE;
    event.address = (u64)devPtr;
    emit_gpu_event(&event);
    return 0;
}
// Track cudaMemcpy
SEC("uprobe/libcudart.so:cudaMemcpy")
int BPF_UPROBE(trace_cuda_memcpy_enter, 
               void *dst, const void *src, size_t count, int kind)
{
    if (!should_trace_process())
        return 0;
    u64 id = bpf_get_current_pid_tgid();
    u64 ts = bpf_ktime_get_ns();
    // Store start time and size
    struct {
        u64 ts;
        u64 size;
        u32 kind;
    } info = {
        .ts = ts,
        .size = count,
        .kind = kind,
    };
    bpf_map_update_elem(&kernel_start_time, &id, &info, BPF_ANY);
    return 0;
}
SEC("uretprobe/libcudart.so:cudaMemcpy")
int BPF_URETPROBE(trace_cuda_memcpy_exit, int ret)
{
    if (!should_trace_process() || ret != 0)
        return 0;
    u64 id = bpf_get_current_pid_tgid();
    u32 pid = id >> 32;
    void *info_ptr = bpf_map_lookup_elem(&kernel_start_time, &id);
    if (!info_ptr)
        return 0;
    struct {
        u64 ts;
        u64 size;
        u32 kind;
    } info;
    bpf_probe_read(&info, sizeof(info), info_ptr);
    bpf_map_delete_elem(&kernel_start_time, &id);
    u64 duration_ns = bpf_ktime_get_ns() - info.ts;
    struct gpu_event event = {};
    fill_event_header(&event.hdr, EVENT_MEMORY_ALLOC);
    event.size = info.size;
    event.duration_us = duration_ns / 1000;
    // cudaMemcpyKind: 1=H2D, 2=D2H, 3=D2D
    switch (info.kind) {
    case 1:
        event.gpu_event_type = GPU_MEMCPY_H2D;
        break;
    case 2:
        event.gpu_event_type = GPU_MEMCPY_D2H;
        break;
    case 3:
        event.gpu_event_type = GPU_MEMCPY_D2D;
        break;
    }
    emit_gpu_event(&event);
    // Update stats
    struct gpu_stats *stats = bpf_map_lookup_elem(&process_gpu_stats, &pid);
    if (stats) {
        if (info.kind == 1) {
            __sync_fetch_and_add(&stats->memcpy_h2d_bytes, info.size);
        } else if (info.kind == 2) {
            __sync_fetch_and_add(&stats->memcpy_d2h_bytes, info.size);
        }
    }
    return 0;
}
// Track CUDA kernel launches
SEC("uprobe/libcudart.so:cudaLaunchKernel")
int BPF_UPROBE(trace_cuda_launch_enter,
               const void *func,
               u32 gridDimX, u32 gridDimY, u32 gridDimZ,
               u32 blockDimX, u32 blockDimY, u32 blockDimZ,
               u32 sharedMem,
               void *stream,
               void **args,
               void **extra)
{
    if (!should_trace_process())
        return 0;
    u64 id = bpf_get_current_pid_tgid();
    u64 ts = bpf_ktime_get_ns();
    bpf_map_update_elem(&kernel_start_time, &id, &ts, BPF_ANY);
    // Store kernel info for exit probe
    struct {
        u64 func_addr;
        u32 grid[3];
        u32 block[3];
        u32 shared_mem;
    } kernel_info = {
        .func_addr = (u64)func,
        .grid = {gridDimX, gridDimY, gridDimZ},
        .block = {blockDimX, blockDimY, blockDimZ},
        .shared_mem = sharedMem,
    };
    // Use a different map key to avoid collision
    u64 info_key = id | (1ULL << 63);
    bpf_map_update_elem(&kernel_start_time, &info_key, &kernel_info, BPF_ANY);
    return 0;
}
SEC("uretprobe/libcudart.so:cudaLaunchKernel")
int BPF_URETPROBE(trace_cuda_launch_exit, int ret)
{
    if (!should_trace_process() || ret != 0)
        return 0;
    u64 id = bpf_get_current_pid_tgid();
    u32 pid = id >> 32;
    u64 *start_ts = bpf_map_lookup_elem(&kernel_start_time, &id);
    if (!start_ts)
        return 0;
    u64 duration_ns = bpf_ktime_get_ns() - *start_ts;
    bpf_map_delete_elem(&kernel_start_time, &id);
    struct gpu_event event = {};
    fill_event_header(&event.hdr, EVENT_MEMORY_ALLOC);
    event.gpu_event_type = GPU_KERNEL_LAUNCH;
    event.duration_us = duration_ns / 1000;
    // Retrieve kernel info
    u64 info_key = id | (1ULL << 63);
    void *info_ptr = bpf_map_lookup_elem(&kernel_start_time, &info_key);
    if (info_ptr) {
        struct {
            u64 func_addr;
            u32 grid[3];
            u32 block[3];
            u32 shared_mem;
        } kernel_info;
        bpf_probe_read(&kernel_info, sizeof(kernel_info), info_ptr);
        bpf_map_delete_elem(&kernel_start_time, &info_key);
        event.address = kernel_info.func_addr;
        event.grid_x = kernel_info.grid[0];
        event.grid_y = kernel_info.grid[1];
        event.grid_z = kernel_info.grid[2];
        event.block_x = kernel_info.block[0];
        event.block_y = kernel_info.block[1];
        event.block_z = kernel_info.block[2];
        event.shared_memory = kernel_info.shared_mem;
    }
    emit_gpu_event(&event);
    // Update stats
    struct gpu_stats *stats = bpf_map_lookup_elem(&process_gpu_stats, &pid);
    if (!stats) {
        struct gpu_stats new_stats = {
            .kernel_launches = 1,
            .total_kernel_time_us = duration_ns / 1000,
            .active_kernels = 1,
        };
        bpf_map_update_elem(&process_gpu_stats, &pid, &new_stats, BPF_ANY);
    } else {
        __sync_fetch_and_add(&stats->kernel_launches, 1);
        __sync_fetch_and_add(&stats->total_kernel_time_us, duration_ns / 1000);
        __sync_fetch_and_add(&stats->active_kernels, 1);
    }
    return 0;
}
// Track cudaDeviceSynchronize
SEC("uprobe/libcudart.so:cudaDeviceSynchronize")
int BPF_UPROBE(trace_cuda_sync_enter)
{
    if (!should_trace_process())
        return 0;
    u64 id = bpf_get_current_pid_tgid();
    u64 ts = bpf_ktime_get_ns();
    bpf_map_update_elem(&kernel_start_time, &id, &ts, BPF_ANY);
    return 0;
}
SEC("uretprobe/libcudart.so:cudaDeviceSynchronize")
int BPF_URETPROBE(trace_cuda_sync_exit, int ret)
{
    if (!should_trace_process())
        return 0;
    u64 id = bpf_get_current_pid_tgid();
    u64 *start_ts = bpf_map_lookup_elem(&kernel_start_time, &id);
    if (!start_ts)
        return 0;
    u64 duration_ns = bpf_ktime_get_ns() - *start_ts;
    bpf_map_delete_elem(&kernel_start_time, &id);
    struct gpu_event event = {};
    fill_event_header(&event.hdr, EVENT_MEMORY_ALLOC);
    event.gpu_event_type = GPU_SYNC;
    event.duration_us = duration_ns / 1000;
    emit_gpu_event(&event);
    return 0;
}




Step 3: PyTorch Integration
bpf/pytorch.bpf.c
c -172 lines

// SPDX-License-Identifier: GPL-2.0
// PyTorch framework monitoring
#include "core.bpf.h"
char LICENSE[] SEC("license") = "GPL";
// PyTorch event types
enum pytorch_event_type {
    PYTORCH_FORWARD = 1,
    PYTORCH_BACKWARD = 2,
    PYTORCH_OPTIMIZER_STEP = 3,
    PYTORCH_MODEL_LOAD = 4,
    PYTORCH_MODEL_SAVE = 5,
};
// PyTorch event structure
struct pytorch_event {
    struct event_header hdr;
    u8 pytorch_event_type;
    char model_name[128];
    u32 batch_size;
    u32 duration_us;
    u64 tensor_size;
    u32 num_parameters;
};
// PyTorch stats per model
struct model_stats {
    u64 forward_passes;
    u64 backward_passes;
    u64 optimizer_steps;
    u64 total_forward_time_us;
    u64 total_backward_time_us;
    u64 total_samples_processed;
    u32 current_batch_size;
};
// Maps
struct {
    __uint(type, BPF_MAP_TYPE_RINGBUF);
    __uint(max_entries, 256 * 1024);
} pytorch_events SEC(".maps");
struct {
    __uint(type, BPF_MAP_TYPE_HASH);
    __uint(max_entries, 256);
    __type(key, u32);  // Model hash or PID
    __type(value, struct model_stats);
} model_stats_map SEC(".maps");
// Track timing
struct {
    __uint(type, BPF_MAP_TYPE_HASH);
    __uint(max_entries, MAX_ENTRIES);
    __type(key, u64);
    __type(value, u64);
} pytorch_timing SEC(".maps");
// Track PyTorch forward pass
// Note: Symbol names may vary by PyTorch version
SEC("uprobe/libtorch_python.so:_ZN5torch8autograd6Engine12execute_implEv")
int BPF_UPROBE(trace_pytorch_forward_enter)
{
    if (!should_trace_process())
        return 0;
    u64 id = bpf_get_current_pid_tgid();
    u64 ts = bpf_ktime_get_ns();
    bpf_map_update_elem(&pytorch_timing, &id, &ts, BPF_ANY);
    return 0;
}
SEC("uretprobe/libtorch_python.so:_ZN5torch8autograd6Engine12execute_implEv")
int BPF_URETPROBE(trace_pytorch_forward_exit)
{
    if (!should_trace_process())
        return 0;
    u64 id = bpf_get_current_pid_tgid();
    u32 pid = id >> 32;
    u64 *start_ts = bpf_map_lookup_elem(&pytorch_timing, &id);
    if (!start_ts)
        return 0;
    u64 duration_ns = bpf_ktime_get_ns() - *start_ts;
    bpf_map_delete_elem(&pytorch_timing, &id);
    struct pytorch_event event = {};
    fill_event_header(&event.hdr, EVENT_MEMORY_ALLOC);
    event.pytorch_event_type = PYTORCH_FORWARD;
    event.duration_us = duration_ns / 1000;
    struct pytorch_event *e;
    e = bpf_ringbuf_reserve(&pytorch_events, sizeof(*e), 0);
    if (e) {
        __builtin_memcpy(e, &event, sizeof(event));
        bpf_ringbuf_submit(e, 0);
    }
    // Update stats
    struct model_stats *stats = bpf_map_lookup_elem(&model_stats_map, &pid);
    if (!stats) {
        struct model_stats new_stats = {
            .forward_passes = 1,
            .total_forward_time_us = duration_ns / 1000,
        };
        bpf_map_update_elem(&model_stats_map, &pid, &new_stats, BPF_ANY);
    } else {
        __sync_fetch_and_add(&stats->forward_passes, 1);
        __sync_fetch_and_add(&stats->total_forward_time_us, duration_ns / 1000);
    }
    return 0;
}
// Track backward pass
SEC("uprobe/libtorch_python.so:_ZN5torch8autograd8backward")
int BPF_UPROBE(trace_pytorch_backward_enter)
{
    if (!should_trace_process())
        return 0;
    u64 id = bpf_get_current_pid_tgid();
    u64 ts = bpf_ktime_get_ns();
    u64 key = id | (1ULL << 62);  // Different key for backward
    bpf_map_update_elem(&pytorch_timing, &key, &ts, BPF_ANY);
    return 0;
}
SEC("uretprobe/libtorch_python.so:_ZN5torch8autograd8backward")

{
    if (!should_trace_process())
        return 0;
    u64 id = bpf_get_current_pid_tgid();
    u32 pid = id >> 32;
    u64 key = id | (1ULL << 62);
    u64 *start_ts = bpf_map_lookup_elem(&pytorch_timing, &key);
    if (!start_ts)
        return 0;
    u64 duration_ns = bpf_ktime_get_ns() - *start_ts;
    bpf_map_delete_elem(&pytorch_timing, &key);
    struct pytorch_event event = {};
    fill_event_header(&event.hdr, EVENT_MEMORY_ALLOC);
    event.pytorch_event_type = PYTORCH_BACKWARD;
    event.duration_us = duration_ns / 1000;
    struct pytorch_event *e;
    e = bpf_ringbuf_reserve(&pytorch_events, sizeof(*e), 0);
    if (e) {
        __builtin_memcpy(e, &event, sizeof(event));
        bpf_ringbuf_submit(e, 0);
    }
    // Update stats
    struct model_stats *stats = bpf_map_lookup_elem(&model_stats_map, &pid);
    if (stats) {
        __sync_fetch_and_add(&stats->backward_passes, 1);
        __sync_fetch_and_add(&stats->total_backward_time_us, duration_ns / 1000);
    }
    return 0;
}

        return 0;

    }
    return 0;

package types

// GPU event types
type GPUEventType uint8
const (
    GPUMemoryAlloc GPUEventType = iota + 1
    GPUMemoryFree
    GPUKernelLaunch

    GPUMemcpyD2H
    GPUMemcpyD2D

)

type GPUEvent struct {

    GPUEventType  GPUEventType
    DeviceID      uint32
    Address       uint64
    Size          uint64
    DurationUs    uint32
    // Kernel launch specific
    GridDim       [3]uint32
    BlockDim      [3]uint32
    SharedMemory  uint32

}

    MemoryAllocated    uint64
    MemoryFreed        uint64
    MemoryCurrent      uint64
    MemoryPeak         uint64

    MemcpyD2HBytes     uint64

}

    PyTorchOptimizerStep
    PyTorchModelLoad
    PyTorchModelSave
)

}

    TotalBackwardTimeUs    uint64

Step 5: GPU Detection and Utilities
pkg/gpu/detector.go
go -122 lines

package gpu
import (
    "fmt"
    "os"
    "path/filepath"
)
type GPUVendor string
const (
    NVIDIA GPUVendor = "nvidia"
    AMD    GPUVendor = "amd"
    Intel  GPUVendor = "intel"
    Unknown GPUVendor = "unknown"
)
type GPUInfo struct {
    Vendor     GPUVendor
    DeviceID   int
    Name       string
    Memory     uint64
    PCIBusID   string
    Driver     string
}
type GPUDetector struct {
    gpus []GPUInfo
}
func NewGPUDetector() *GPUDetector {
    return &GPUDetector{
        gpus: make([]GPUInfo, 0),
    }
}
func (d *GPUDetector) Detect() ([]GPUInfo, error) {
    // Try NVIDIA first
    nvidiaGPUs, err := d.detectNVIDIA()
    if err == nil && len(nvidiaGPUs) > 0 {
        d.gpus = append(d.gpus, nvidiaGPUs...)
    }
    // Try AMD
    amdGPUs, err := d.detectAMD()
    if err == nil && len(amdGPUs) > 0 {
        d.gpus = append(d.gpus, amdGPUs...)
    }
    if len(d.gpus) == 0 {
        return nil, fmt.Errorf("no GPUs detected")
    }
    return d.gpus, nil
}
func (d *GPUDetector) detectNVIDIA() ([]GPUInfo, error) {
    // Check if NVIDIA driver is loaded
    if _, err := os.Stat("/proc/driver/nvidia/version"); os.IsNotExist(err) {
        return nil, fmt.Errorf("NVIDIA driver not found")
    }
    // Check for nvidia-smi
    if _, err := os.Stat("/usr/bin/nvidia-smi"); os.IsNotExist(err) {
        return nil, fmt.Errorf("nvidia-smi not found")
    }
    // Use NVML library for detection
    gpus, err := detectNVIDIAWithNVML()
    if err != nil {
        return nil, err
    }
    return gpus, nil
}
func (d *GPUDetector) detectAMD() ([]GPUInfo, error) {
    // Check for AMD GPU sysfs entries
    sysfsPath := "/sys/class/drm"
    entries, err := os.ReadDir(sysfsPath)
    if err != nil {
        return nil, err
    }
    gpus := make([]GPUInfo, 0)
    for _, entry := range entries {
        if !entry.IsDir() {
            continue
        }
        // Check if it's an AMD GPU (renderD* devices)
        devicePath := filepath.Join(sysfsPath, entry.Name(), "device")
        vendorPath := filepath.Join(devicePath, "vendor")
        vendorData, err := os.ReadFile(vendorPath)
        if err != nil {
            continue
        }
        // AMD vendor ID is 0x1002
        if string(vendorData) == "0x1002\n" {
            gpu := GPUInfo{
                Vendor: AMD,
                Name:   "AMD GPU",
            }
            gpus = append(gpus, gpu)
        }
    }
    return gpus, nil
}
func (d *GPUDetector) GetLibraryPath(vendor GPUVendor) (string, error) {
    switch vendor {
    case NVIDIA:
        // Try common CUDA runtime library paths
        paths := []string{
            "/usr/local/cuda/lib64/libcudart.so",
            "/usr/lib/x86_64-linux-gnu/libcudart.so",
            "/usr/lib64/libcudart.so",
        }
        for _, path := range paths {
            if _, err := os.Stat(path); err == nil {
                return path, nil
            }
        }
        return "", fmt.Errorf("CUDA runtime library not found")
    case AMD:
        // ROCm library
        paths := []string{
            "/opt/rocm/lib/libamdhip64.so",
            "/usr/lib/x86_64-linux-gnu/libamdhip64.so",
        }
        for _, path := range paths {
            if _, err := os.Stat(path); err == nil {
                return path, nil
            }
        }
        return "", fmt.Errorf("ROCm library not found")
    default:
        return "", fmt.Errorf("unsupported GPU vendor: %s", vendor)
    }
}




pkg/gpu/nvidia.go
go -80 lines

package gpu
import (
    "fmt"
    "github.com/NVIDIA/go-nvml/pkg/nvml"
)
func detectNVIDIAWithNVML() ([]GPUInfo, error) {
    ret := nvml.Init()
    if ret != nvml.SUCCESS {
        return nil, fmt.Errorf("failed to initialize NVML: %v", nvml.ErrorString(ret))
    }
    defer nvml.Shutdown()
    count, ret := nvml.DeviceGetCount()
    if ret != nvml.SUCCESS {
        return nil, fmt.Errorf("failed to get device count: %v", nvml.ErrorString(ret))
    }
    gpus := make([]GPUInfo, 0, count)
    for i := 0; i < count; i++ {
        device, ret := nvml.DeviceGetHandleByIndex(i)
        if ret != nvml.SUCCESS {
            continue
        }
        name, ret := device.GetName()
        if ret != nvml.SUCCESS {
            name = "Unknown NVIDIA GPU"
        }
        memory, ret := device.GetMemoryInfo()
        var totalMemory uint64
        if ret == nvml.SUCCESS {
            totalMemory = memory.Total
        }
        pciInfo, ret := device.GetPciInfo()
        var busID string
        if ret == nvml.SUCCESS {
            busID = fmt.Sprintf("%08x:%02x:%02x.%x",
                pciInfo.Domain, pciInfo.Bus, pciInfo.Device, pciInfo.Function)
        }
        gpu := GPUInfo{
            Vendor:   NVIDIA,
            DeviceID: i,
            Name:     name,
            Memory:   totalMemory,
            PCIBusID: busID,
            Driver:   "nvidia",
        }
        gpus = append(gpus, gpu)
    }
    return gpus, nil
}
func GetNVIDIAUtilization(deviceID int) (uint32, error) {
    ret := nvml.Init()
    if ret != nvml.SUCCESS {
        return 0, fmt.Errorf("failed to initialize NVML: %v", nvml.ErrorString(ret))
    }
    defer nvml.Shutdown()
    device, ret := nvml.DeviceGetHandleByIndex(deviceID)
    if ret != nvml.SUCCESS {
        return 0, fmt.Errorf("failed to get device: %v", nvml.ErrorString(ret))
    }
    utilization, ret := device.GetUtilizationRates()
    if ret != nvml.SUCCESS {
        return 0, fmt.Errorf("failed to get utilization: %v", nvml.ErrorString(ret))
    }
    return utilization.Gpu, nil
}
func GetNVIDIAMemoryInfo(deviceID int) (used, total uint64, err error) {
    ret := nvml.Init()
    if ret != nvml.SUCCESS {
        return 0, 0, fmt.Errorf("failed to initialize NVML: %v", nvml.ErrorString(ret))
    }
    defer nvml.Shutdown()
    device, ret := nvml.DeviceGetHandleByIndex(deviceID)
    if ret != nvml.SUCCESS {
        return 0, 0, fmt.Errorf("failed to get device: %v", nvml.ErrorString(ret))
    }
    memory, ret := device.GetMemoryInfo()
    if ret != nvml.SUCCESS {
        return 0, 0, fmt.Errorf("failed to get memory info: %v", nvml.ErrorString(ret))
    }
    return memory.Used, memory.Total, nil
}




Step 6: GPU Agent Handler
pkg/agent/gpu.go
go -279 lines

package agent
import (
    "bytes"
    "encoding/binary"
    "fmt"
    "log"
    "time"
    "github.com/cilium/ebpf/ringbuf"
    "github.com/yourorg/neurontrace/pkg/gpu"
    "github.com/yourorg/neurontrace/pkg/types"
)
// GPU event from eBPF (must match C struct)
type gpuEventRaw struct {
    Header       eventHeaderRaw
    GPUEventType uint8
    DeviceID     uint32
    Address      uint64
    Size         uint64
    DurationUs   uint32
    GridX        uint32
    GridY        uint32
    GridZ        uint32
    BlockX       uint32
    BlockY       uint32
    BlockZ       uint32
    SharedMemory uint32
    KernelName   [64]byte
}
func (a *Agent) startGPUMonitoring() error {
    // Detect GPUs
    detector := gpu.NewGPUDetector()
    gpus, err := detector.Detect()
    if err != nil {
        log.Printf("⚠ No GPUs detected: %v", err)
        return nil  // Not an error, just skip GPU monitoring
    }
    log.Printf("✓ Detected %d GPU(s)", len(gpus))
    for _, g := range gpus {
        log.Printf("  - %s: %s (%d MB)", g.Vendor, g.Name, g.Memory/(1024*1024))
    }
    // Load GPU eBPF programs
    if err := a.loadGPUPrograms(gpus); err != nil {
        return fmt.Errorf("failed to load GPU programs: %w", err)
    }
    // Start event processing
    rb, ok := a.objs.Maps["gpu_events"]
    if !ok {
        return fmt.Errorf("gpu_events map not found")
    }
    reader, err := ringbuf.NewReader(rb)
    if err != nil {
        return fmt.Errorf("failed to create GPU reader: %w", err)
    }
    a.readers = append(a.readers, reader)
    go a.processGPUEvents(reader)
    // Start GPU stats collector
    go a.collectGPUStats(gpus)
    log.Println("✓ GPU monitoring started")
    return nil
}
func (a *Agent) loadGPUPrograms(gpus []gpu.GPUInfo) error {
    // For each GPU vendor, attach appropriate probes
    for _, g := range gpus {
        switch g.Vendor {
        case gpu.NVIDIA:
            if err := a.attachCUDAProbes(); err != nil {
                return fmt.Errorf("failed to attach CUDA probes: %w", err)
            }
        case gpu.AMD:
            if err := a.attachROCmProbes(); err != nil {
                log.Printf("⚠ Failed to attach ROCm probes: %v", err)
                // Continue anyway
            }
        }
    }
    return nil
}
func (a *Agent) attachCUDAProbes() error {
    detector := gpu.NewGPUDetector()
    cudaLibPath, err := detector.GetLibraryPath(gpu.NVIDIA)
    if err != nil {
        return err
    }
    log.Printf("Attaching CUDA probes to: %s", cudaLibPath)
    // Attach cudaMalloc probes
    if err := a.attachUprobe(cudaLibPath, "cudaMalloc", "trace_cuda_malloc_enter"); err != nil {
        return fmt.Errorf("failed to attach cudaMalloc enter: %w", err)
    }
    if err := a.attachUretprobe(cudaLibPath, "cudaMalloc", "trace_cuda_malloc_exit"); err != nil {
        return fmt.Errorf("failed to attach cudaMalloc exit: %w", err)
    }
    // Attach cudaFree probe
    if err := a.attachUprobe(cudaLibPath, "cudaFree", "trace_cuda_free"); err != nil {
        log.Printf("⚠ Failed to attach cudaFree: %v", err)
    }
    // Attach cudaMemcpy probes
    if err := a.attachUprobe(cudaLibPath, "cudaMemcpy", "trace_cuda_memcpy_enter"); err != nil {
        log.Printf("⚠ Failed to attach cudaMemcpy enter: %v", err)
    }
    if err := a.attachUretprobe(cudaLibPath, "cudaMemcpy", "trace_cuda_memcpy_exit"); err != nil {
        log.Printf("⚠ Failed to attach cudaMemcpy exit: %v", err)
    }
    // Attach cudaLaunchKernel probes
    if err := a.attachUprobe(cudaLibPath, "cudaLaunchKernel", "trace_cuda_launch_enter"); err != nil {
        log.Printf("⚠ Failed to attach cudaLaunchKernel enter: %v", err)
    }
    if err := a.attachUretprobe(cudaLibPath, "cudaLaunchKernel", "trace_cuda_launch_exit"); err != nil {
        log.Printf("⚠ Failed to attach cudaLaunchKernel exit: %v", err)
    }
    // Attach cudaDeviceSynchronize probes
    if err := a.attachUprobe(cudaLibPath, "cudaDeviceSynchronize", "trace_cuda_sync_enter"); err != nil {
        log.Printf("⚠ Failed to attach cudaDeviceSynchronize enter: %v", err)
    }
    if err := a.attachUretprobe(cudaLibPath, "cudaDeviceSynchronize", "trace_cuda_sync_exit"); err != nil {
        log.Printf("⚠ Failed to attach cudaDeviceSynchronize exit: %v", err)
    }
    log.Println("✓ CUDA probes attached")
    return nil
}
func (a *Agent) attachROCmProbes() error {
    // Similar to CUDA but for AMD ROCm
    // Implementation would be similar but with ROCm API functions
    return fmt.Errorf("ROCm monitoring not yet implemented")
}
func (a *Agent) processGPUEvents(reader *ringbuf.Reader) {
    log.Println("GPU event processing loop started")
    for {
        select {
        case <-a.ctx.Done():
            return
        default:
            record, err := reader.Read()
            if err != nil {
                continue
            }
            var raw gpuEventRaw
            if err := binary.Read(
                bytes.NewReader(record.RawSample),
                binary.LittleEndian,
                &raw,
            ); err != nil {
                log.Printf("Failed to parse GPU event: %v\n", err)
                continue
            }
            event := a.parseGPUEvent(&raw)
            a.handleGPUEvent(event)
            a.metrics.EventsProcessed.Inc()
        }
    }
}
func (a *Agent) parseGPUEvent(raw *gpuEventRaw) *types.GPUEvent {
    event := &types.GPUEvent{
        EventHeader:  parseEventHeader(&raw.Header),
        GPUEventType: types.GPUEventType(raw.GPUEventType),
        DeviceID:     raw.DeviceID,
        Address:      raw.Address,
        Size:         raw.Size,
        DurationUs:   raw.DurationUs,
        GridDim:      [3]uint32{raw.GridX, raw.GridY, raw.GridZ},
        BlockDim:     [3]uint32{raw.BlockX, raw.BlockY, raw.BlockZ},
        SharedMemory: raw.SharedMemory,
        KernelName:   string(bytes.TrimRight(raw.KernelName[:], "\x00")),
    }
    return event
}
func (a *Agent) handleGPUEvent(event *types.GPUEvent) {
    comm := event.Comm
    deviceID := fmt.Sprintf("%d", event.DeviceID)
    switch event.GPUEventType {
    case types.GPUMemoryAlloc:
        a.metrics.GPUMemoryAllocated.WithLabelValues(
            comm,
            deviceID,
        ).Add(float64(event.Size))
        if a.config.LogLevel == "debug" {
            log.Printf("GPU Alloc: %s allocated %d bytes on device %d",
                comm, event.Size, event.DeviceID)
        }
    case types.GPUMemoryFree:
        a.metrics.GPUMemoryFreed.WithLabelValues(
            comm,
            deviceID,
        ).Inc()
    case types.GPUKernelLaunch:
        a.metrics.GPUKernelLaunches.WithLabelValues(
            comm,
            deviceID,
            event.KernelName,
        ).Inc()
        a.metrics.GPUKernelDuration.WithLabelValues(
            comm,
            deviceID,
        ).Observe(float64(event.DurationUs) / 1000000.0)  // Convert to seconds
        if a.config.LogLevel == "debug" {
            log.Printf("GPU Kernel: %s launched %s (grid:%v block:%v) took %dus",
                comm, event.KernelName, event.GridDim, event.BlockDim, event.DurationUs)
        }
    case types.GPUMemcpyH2D:
        a.metrics.GPUMemcpyBytes.WithLabelValues(
            comm,
            deviceID,
            "H2D",
        ).Add(float64(event.Size))
    case types.GPUMemcpyD2H:
        a.metrics.GPUMemcpyBytes.WithLabelValues(
            comm,
            deviceID,
            "D2H",
        ).Add(float64(event.Size))
    case types.GPUSync:
        a.metrics.GPUSyncDuration.WithLabelValues(
            comm,
            deviceID,
        ).Observe(float64(event.DurationUs) / 1000000.0)
    }
}
func (a *Agent) collectGPUStats(gpus []gpu.GPUInfo) {
    ticker := time.NewTicker(5 * time.Second)
    defer ticker.Stop()
    for {
        select {
        case <-a.ctx.Done():
            return
        case <-ticker.C:
            for _, g := range gpus {
                if g.Vendor != gpu.NVIDIA {
                    continue
                }
                // Get GPU utilization
                util, err := gpu.GetNVIDIAUtilization(g.DeviceID)
                if err == nil {
                    a.metrics.GPUUtilization.WithLabelValues(
                        fmt.Sprintf("%d", g.DeviceID),
                        g.Name,
                    ).Set(float64(util))
                }
                // Get memory info
                used, total, err := gpu.GetNVIDIAMemoryInfo(g.DeviceID)
                if err == nil {
                    a.metrics.GPUMemoryUsed.WithLabelValues(
                        fmt.Sprintf("%d", g.DeviceID),
                        g.Name,
                    ).Set(float64(used))
                    a.metrics.GPUMemoryTotal.WithLabelValues(
                        fmt.Sprintf("%d", g.DeviceID),
                        g.Name,
                    ).Set(float64(total))
                }
            }
            // Read stats from eBPF maps
            a.updateGPUMapStats()
        }
    }
}
func (a *Agent) updateGPUMapStats() {
    statsMap, ok := a.objs.Maps["process_gpu_stats"]
    if !ok {
        return
    }
    var pid uint32
    var stats struct {
        MemoryAllocated   uint64
        MemoryFreed       uint64
        MemoryCurrent     uint64
        MemoryPeak        uint64
        KernelLaunches    uint64
        MemcpyH2DBytes    uint64
        MemcpyD2HBytes    uint64
        TotalKernelTimeUs uint64
        ActiveKernels     uint32
    }
    iter := statsMap.Iterate()
    for iter.Next(&pid, &stats) {
        pidStr := fmt.Sprintf("%d", pid)
        // Update per-process GPU metrics
        a.metrics.ProcessGPUMemory.WithLabelValues(pidStr).Set(float64(stats.MemoryCurrent))
        a.metrics.ProcessGPUKernels.WithLabelValues(pidStr).Set(float64(stats.KernelLaunches))
    }
}




Step 7: Enhanced Metrics for GPU/AI
pkg/agent/metrics.go (Add GPU metrics)
go -198 lines

// Add to existing Metrics struct
// GPU metrics

Step 8: Test PyTorch Script
scripts/test-pytorch.py
python -152 lines

#!/usr/bin/env python3
"""
Test PyTorch workload for NeuronTrace
Generates various GPU operations for monitoring
"""
import torch
import torch.nn as nn
import torch.optim as optim
import time
import argparse
class SimpleModel(nn.Module):
    def __init__(self, input_size=1024, hidden_size=512, output_size=10):
        super(SimpleModel, self).__init__()
        self.fc1 = nn.Linear(input_size, hidden_size)
        self.relu = nn.ReLU()
        self.fc2 = nn.Linear(hidden_size, hidden_size)
        self.fc3 = nn.Linear(hidden_size, output_size)
    def forward(self, x):
        x = self.fc1(x)
        x = self.relu(x)
        x = self.fc2(x)
        x = self.relu(x)
        x = self.fc3(x)
        return x
def train_step(model, optimizer, criterion, batch_size=32):
    """Single training step"""
    # Generate random data
    inputs = torch.randn(batch_size, 1024).cuda()
    targets = torch.randint(0, 10, (batch_size,)).cuda()
    # Forward pass
    optimizer.zero_grad()
    outputs = model(inputs)
    loss = criterion(outputs, targets)
    # Backward pass
    loss.backward()
    # Optimizer step
    optimizer.step()
    return loss.item()
def inference(model, batch_size=32):
    """Single inference pass"""
    with torch.no_grad():
        inputs = torch.randn(batch_size, 1024).cuda()
        outputs = model(inputs)
    return outputs
def test_memory_allocation():
    """Test various memory allocation patterns"""
    print("Testing memory allocation...")
    # Allocate various sizes
    tensors = []
    sizes = [1024, 2048, 4096, 8192, 16384]
    for size in sizes:
        t = torch.randn(size, size).cuda()
        tensors.append(t)
        time.sleep(0.1)
    # Free memory
    del tensors
    torch.cuda.empty_cache()
    print("✓ Memory allocation test complete")
def test_kernel_launches():
    """Test various CUDA kernel operations"""
    print("Testing kernel launches...")
    a = torch.randn(1000, 1000).cuda()
    b = torch.randn(1000, 1000).cuda()
    # Matrix operations
    c = torch.matmul(a, b)
    d = torch.add(a, b)
    e = torch.mul(a, b)
    f = torch.div(a, b)
    # Reductions
    sum_a = torch.sum(a)
    mean_a = torch.mean(a)
    max_a = torch.max(a)
    torch.cuda.synchronize()
    print("✓ Kernel launch test complete")
def test_training(num_steps=100, batch_size=32):
    """Test training loop"""
    print(f"Testing training loop ({num_steps} steps, batch_size={batch_size})...")
    model = SimpleModel().cuda()
    optimizer = optim.Adam(model.parameters(), lr=0.001)
    criterion = nn.CrossEntropyLoss()
    start_time = time.time()
    for step in range(num_steps):
        loss = train_step(model, optimizer, criterion, batch_size)
        if (step + 1) % 10 == 0:
            elapsed = time.time() - start_time
            throughput = (step + 1) * batch_size / elapsed
            print(f"  Step {step+1}/{num_steps} - Loss: {loss:.4f} - "
                  f"Throughput: {throughput:.2f} samples/sec")
    total_time = time.time() - start_time
    total_samples = num_steps * batch_size
    avg_throughput = total_samples / total_time
    print(f"✓ Training test complete")
    print(f"  Total time: {total_time:.2f}s")
    print(f"  Average throughput: {avg_throughput:.2f} samples/sec")
def test_inference(num_batches=100, batch_size=64):
    """Test inference loop"""
    print(f"Testing inference ({num_batches} batches, batch_size={batch_size})...")
    model = SimpleModel().cuda()
    model.eval()
    latencies = []
    for i in range(num_batches):
        start = time.time()
        outputs = inference(model, batch_size)
        torch.cuda.synchronize()
        latency = (time.time() - start) * 1000  # ms
        latencies.append(latency)
        if (i + 1) % 10 == 0:
            avg_latency = sum(latencies) / len(latencies)
            print(f"  Batch {i+1}/{num_batches} - Avg latency: {avg_latency:.2f}ms")
    avg_latency = sum(latencies) / len(latencies)
    p95_latency = sorted(latencies)[int(len(latencies) * 0.95)]
    p99_latency = sorted(latencies)[int(len(latencies) * 0.99)]
    print(f"✓ Inference test complete")
    print(f"  Average latency: {avg_latency:.2f}ms")
    print(f"  P95 latency: {p95_latency:.2f}ms")
    print(f"  P99 latency: {p99_latency:.2f}ms")
def main():
    parser = argparse.ArgumentParser(description='PyTorch workload generator for NeuronTrace')
    parser.add_argument('--mode', choices=['all', 'memory', 'kernels', 'training', 'inference'],
                       default='all', help='Test mode')
    parser.add_argument('--steps', type=int, default=100, help='Number of training steps')
    parser.add_argument('--batch-size', type=int, default=32, help='Batch size')
    parser.add_argument('--inference-batches', type=int, default=100, help='Number of inference batches')
    args = parser.parse_args()
    # Check CUDA availability
    if not torch.cuda.is_available():
        print("❌ CUDA is not available!")
        return
    print(f"🚀 NeuronTrace PyTorch Test Workload")
    print(f"   GPU: {torch.cuda.get_device_name(0)}")
    print(f"   CUDA Version: {torch.version.cuda}")
    print(f"   PyTorch Version: {torch.__version__}")
    print()
    if args.mode in ['all', 'memory']:
        test_memory_allocation()
        print()
    if args.mode in ['all', 'kernels']:
        test_kernel_launches()
        print()
    if args.mode in ['all', 'training']:
        test_training(num_steps=args.steps, batch_size=args.batch_size)
        print()
    if args.mode in ['all', 'inference']:
        test_inference(num_batches=args.inference_batches, batch_size=args.batch_size)
        print()
    print("✅ All tests complete!")
    print()
    print("Check NeuronTrace metrics:")
    print("  curl http://localhost:8080/metrics | grep neurontrace_gpu")
    print("  curl http://localhost:8080/metrics | grep neurontrace_ml")
if __name__ == '__main__':
    main()

Step 1: MCP Protocol Monitoring eBPF
bpf/mcp.bpf.c
c -279 lines

// SPDX-License-Identifier: GPL-2.0
// MCP (Model Context Protocol) monitoring with eBPF
#include "core.bpf.h"
char LICENSE[] SEC("license") = "GPL";
// MCP event types
enum mcp_event_type {
    MCP_TOOL_CALL = 1,
    MCP_TOOL_RESPONSE = 2,
    MCP_RESOURCE_READ = 3,
    MCP_RESOURCE_WRITE = 4,
    MCP_PROMPT_REQUEST = 5,
    MCP_SERVER_START = 6,
    MCP_SERVER_STOP = 7,
    MCP_CONNECTION_OPEN = 8,
    MCP_CONNECTION_CLOSE = 9,
};
// MCP access types
enum mcp_access_type {
    MCP_ACCESS_READ = 1,
    MCP_ACCESS_WRITE = 2,
    MCP_ACCESS_EXEC = 3,
    MCP_ACCESS_DELETE = 4,
};
// MCP event structure
struct mcp_event {
    struct event_header hdr;
    u8 mcp_event_type;
    u8 access_type;
    u8 result;           // 0=success, 1=denied, 2=error
    u32 duration_us;
    char tool_name[64];
    char resource_uri[256];
    char server_name[64];
    u32 request_size;
    u32 response_size;
    // Connection info
    u32 client_pid;
    u32 server_port;
    u32 connection_id;
};
// MCP tool call stats
struct tool_stats {
    u64 call_count;
    u64 success_count;
    u64 denied_count;
    u64 error_count;
    u64 total_duration_us;
    u64 total_bytes_read;
    u64 total_bytes_written;
    u32 concurrent_calls;
};
// MCP server stats
struct server_stats {
    u64 total_requests;
    u64 active_connections;
    u64 total_tools_called;
    u64 total_resources_accessed;
    u64 policy_violations;
    u64 start_time;
};
// Resource access tracking
struct resource_access {
    u32 pid;
    char resource_uri[256];
};
struct access_record {
    u64 timestamp;
    u8 access_type;
    u8 result;
    u32 count;
};
// Maps
struct {
    __uint(type, BPF_MAP_TYPE_RINGBUF);
    __uint(max_entries, 512 * 1024);
} mcp_events SEC(".maps");
// Tool stats per tool name
struct {
    __uint(type, BPF_MAP_TYPE_HASH);
    __uint(max_entries, 256);
    __type(key, char[64]);  // Tool name
    __type(value, struct tool_stats);
} tool_stats_map SEC(".maps");
// Server stats per PID
struct {
    __uint(type, BPF_MAP_TYPE_HASH);
    __uint(max_entries, 64);
    __type(key, u32);  // Server PID
    __type(value, struct server_stats);
} server_stats_map SEC(".maps");
// Resource access tracking
struct {
    __uint(type, BPF_MAP_TYPE_HASH);
    __uint(max_entries, MAX_ENTRIES);
    __type(key, struct resource_access);
    __type(value, struct access_record);
} resource_access_map SEC(".maps");
// Rate limiting per tool per PID
struct {
    __uint(type, BPF_MAP_TYPE_HASH);
    __uint(max_entries, 1024);
    __type(key, u64);  // (PID << 32) | tool_hash
    __type(value, u64); // Last call timestamp
} rate_limit_map SEC(".maps");
// Timing for tool calls
struct {
    __uint(type, BPF_MAP_TYPE_HASH);
    __uint(max_entries, MAX_ENTRIES);
    __type(key, u64);  // Unique call ID
    __type(value, u64); // Start timestamp
} tool_call_timing SEC(".maps");
// Helper to emit MCP event
static __always_inline void emit_mcp_event(struct mcp_event *event)
{
    struct mcp_event *e;
    e = bpf_ringbuf_reserve(&mcp_events, sizeof(*e), 0);
    if (!e)
        return;
    __builtin_memcpy(e, event, sizeof(*event));
    bpf_ringbuf_submit(e, 0);
}
// Helper to update tool stats
static __always_inline void update_tool_stats(
    char *tool_name,
    u64 duration_us,
    u8 result,
    u64 bytes_read,
    u64 bytes_written)
{
    struct tool_stats *stats = bpf_map_lookup_elem(&tool_stats_map, tool_name);
    if (!stats) {
        struct tool_stats new_stats = {
            .call_count = 1,
            .total_duration_us = duration_us,
            .total_bytes_read = bytes_read,
            .total_bytes_written = bytes_written,
        };
        if (result == 0) {
            new_stats.success_count = 1;
        } else if (result == 1) {
            new_stats.denied_count = 1;
        } else {
            new_stats.error_count = 1;
        }
        bpf_map_update_elem(&tool_stats_map, tool_name, &new_stats, BPF_ANY);
    } else {
        __sync_fetch_and_add(&stats->call_count, 1);
        __sync_fetch_and_add(&stats->total_duration_us, duration_us);
        __sync_fetch_and_add(&stats->total_bytes_read, bytes_read);
        __sync_fetch_and_add(&stats->total_bytes_written, bytes_written);
        if (result == 0) {
            __sync_fetch_and_add(&stats->success_count, 1);
        } else if (result == 1) {
            __sync_fetch_and_add(&stats->denied_count, 1);
        } else {
            __sync_fetch_and_add(&stats->error_count, 1);
        }
    }
}
// Track MCP server process start
SEC("tracepoint/syscalls/sys_enter_execve")
int trace_mcp_server_start(struct trace_event_raw_sys_enter *ctx)
{
    if (!should_trace_process())
        return 0;
    u32 pid = bpf_get_current_pid_tgid() >> 32;
    char comm[TASK_COMM_LEN];
    bpf_get_current_comm(&comm, sizeof(comm));
    // Check if this is an MCP server process
    // Look for common MCP server patterns: "mcp-server", "mcp_server", "mcpd"
    if (comm[0] == 'm' && comm[1] == 'c' && comm[2] == 'p') {
        struct mcp_event event = {};
        fill_event_header(&event.hdr, EVENT_PROCESS_START);
        event.mcp_event_type = MCP_SERVER_START;
        __builtin_memcpy(event.server_name, comm, sizeof(comm));
        emit_mcp_event(&event);
        // Initialize server stats
        struct server_stats stats = {
            .start_time = bpf_ktime_get_ns(),
        };
        bpf_map_update_elem(&server_stats_map, &pid, &stats, BPF_ANY);
    }
    return 0;
}
// Track file access (MCP resource access)
SEC("tracepoint/syscalls/sys_enter_openat")
int trace_mcp_resource_access(struct trace_event_raw_sys_enter *ctx)
{
    if (!should_trace_process())
        return 0;
    u32 pid = bpf_get_current_pid_tgid() >> 32;
    // Check if this is an MCP server
    struct server_stats *server = bpf_map_lookup_elem(&server_stats_map, &pid);
    if (!server)
        return 0;  // Not an MCP server
    // This is an MCP server accessing a resource
    int dfd = (int)ctx->args[0];
    const char *filename = (const char *)ctx->args[1];
    int flags = (int)ctx->args[2];
    struct mcp_event event = {};
    fill_event_header(&event.hdr, EVENT_FILE_OPEN);
    event.mcp_event_type = MCP_RESOURCE_READ;
    // Read filename
    bpf_probe_read_user_str(event.resource_uri, sizeof(event.resource_uri), filename);
    // Determine access type from flags
    if (flags & 0x0001) {  // O_WRONLY or O_RDWR
        event.access_type = MCP_ACCESS_WRITE;
        event.mcp_event_type = MCP_RESOURCE_WRITE;
    } else {
        event.access_type = MCP_ACCESS_READ;
    }
    emit_mcp_event(&event);
    // Update server stats
    __sync_fetch_and_add(&server->total_resources_accessed, 1);
    return 0;
}
// Track network connections (MCP client connections)
SEC("kprobe/tcp_connect")
int trace_mcp_connection(struct sock *sk)
{
    if (!should_trace_process())
        return 0;
    u32 pid = bpf_get_current_pid_tgid() >> 32;
    // Check if this is an MCP server
    struct server_stats *server = bpf_map_lookup_elem(&server_stats_map, &pid);
    if (!server)
        return 0;
    struct mcp_event event = {};
    fill_event_header(&event.hdr, EVENT_NETWORK_CONNECT);
    event.mcp_event_type = MCP_CONNECTION_OPEN;
    // Read socket info
    u16 family = BPF_CORE_READ(sk, __sk_common.skc_family);
    if (family == AF_INET) {
        event.server_port = BPF_CORE_READ(sk, __sk_common.skc_num);
    }
    emit_mcp_event(&event);
    // Update server stats
    __sync_fetch_and_add(&server->active_connections, 1);
    return 0;
}
// Track send/recv for MCP protocol messages
SEC("kprobe/tcp_sendmsg")
int trace_mcp_send(struct sock *sk, struct msghdr *msg, size_t size)
{
    if (!should_trace_process())
        return 0;
    u32 pid = bpf_get_current_pid_tgid() >> 32;
    struct server_stats *server = bpf_map_lookup_elem(&server_stats_map, &pid);
    if (!server)
        return 0;
    __sync_fetch_and_add(&server->total_requests, 1);
    return 0;
}
// Track Python function calls (for MCP servers written in Python)
// This requires knowing the Python interpreter's function call mechanism
// For now, we'll use a generic approach
// Helper to check rate limits
static __always_inline bool check_rate_limit(u32 pid, char *tool_name, u64 min_interval_ns)
{
    // Simple hash of tool name
    u32 hash = 0;
    for (int i = 0; i < 64 && tool_name[i] != 0; i++) {
        hash = hash * 31 + tool_name[i];
    }
    u64 key = ((u64)pid << 32) | hash;
    u64 now = bpf_ktime_get_ns();
    u64 *last_call = bpf_map_lookup_elem(&rate_limit_map, &key);
    if (!last_call) {
        bpf_map_update_elem(&rate_limit_map, &key, &now, BPF_ANY);
        return true;  // Allow first call
    }
    u64 elapsed = now - *last_call;
    if (elapsed < min_interval_ns) {
        return false;  // Rate limit exceeded
    }
    // Update last call time
    bpf_map_update_elem(&rate_limit_map, &key, &now, BPF_ANY);
    return true;
}




Step 2: MCP Security Policies eBPF
bpf/mcp_security.bpf.c

// SPDX-License-Identifier: GPL-2.0
// MCP security policy enforcement with eBPF
#include "core.bpf.h"
#include "mcp.bpf.c"
char LICENSE[] SEC("license") = "GPL";
// Security policy structure
struct security_policy {
    u8 enabled;
    u8 enforce;           // 0=audit, 1=block
    u8 allow_read;
    u8 allow_write;
    u8 allow_exec;
    u8 allow_delete;
    u32 max_rate_per_min;
    u32 max_file_size_mb;
};
// Path-based policies
struct path_policy {
    char path_prefix[256];
    struct security_policy policy;
};
// Tool-based policies
struct tool_policy {
    char tool_name[64];
    struct security_policy policy;
};
// Maps for security policies
struct {
    __uint(type, BPF_MAP_TYPE_HASH);
    __uint(max_entries, 256);
    __type(key, char[256]);  // Path prefix
    __type(value, struct security_policy);
} path_policies SEC(".maps");
struct {
    __uint(type, BPF_MAP_TYPE_HASH);
    __uint(max_entries, 128);
    __type(key, char[64]);  // Tool name
    __type(value, struct security_policy);
} tool_policies SEC(".maps");
// Default policy
struct {
    __uint(type, BPF_MAP_TYPE_ARRAY);
    __uint(max_entries, 1);
    __type(key, u32);
    __type(value, struct security_policy);
} default_policy SEC(".maps");
// Violation tracking
struct violation_record {
    u64 timestamp;
    u32 pid;
    u8 violation_type;
    char resource[256];
    char tool[64];
};
struct {
    __uint(type, BPF_MAP_TYPE_RINGBUF);
    __uint(max_entries, 256 * 1024);
} security_violations SEC(".maps");
// Helper to check path policy
static __always_inline bool check_path_policy(
    const char *path,
    u8 access_type,
    u32 pid)
{
    // Try exact match first
    struct security_policy *policy = bpf_map_lookup_elem(&path_policies, path);
    if (!policy) {
        // Try prefix matching (simplified - in real impl would iterate)
        u32 key = 0;
        policy = bpf_map_lookup_elem(&default_policy, &key);
        if (!policy) {
            return true;  // No policy, allow by default
        }
    }
    if (!policy->enabled) {
        return true;
    }
    // Check access type
    bool allowed = false;
    switch (access_type) {
    case MCP_ACCESS_READ:
        allowed = policy->allow_read;
        break;
    case MCP_ACCESS_WRITE:
        allowed = policy->allow_write;
        break;
    case MCP_ACCESS_EXEC:
        allowed = policy->allow_exec;
        break;
    case MCP_ACCESS_DELETE:
        allowed = policy->allow_delete;
        break;
    }
    if (!allowed && policy->enforce) {
        // Log violation
        struct violation_record *v;
        v = bpf_ringbuf_reserve(&security_violations, sizeof(*v), 0);
        if (v) {
            v->timestamp = bpf_ktime_get_ns();
            v->pid = pid;
            v->violation_type = access_type;
            bpf_probe_read_kernel_str(v->resource, sizeof(v->resource), path);
            bpf_ringbuf_submit(v, 0);
        }
        return false;  // Block access
    }
    return true;
}
// Helper to check tool policy
static __always_inline bool check_tool_policy(
    char *tool_name,
    u32 pid)
{
    struct security_policy *policy = bpf_map_lookup_elem(&tool_policies, tool_name);
    if (!policy) {
        u32 key = 0;
        policy = bpf_map_lookup_elem(&default_policy, &key);
        if (!policy) {
            return true;
        }
    }
    if (!policy->enabled) {
        return true;
    }
    // Check rate limiting
    if (policy->max_rate_per_min > 0) {
        u64 min_interval_ns = (60ULL * 1000000000ULL) / policy->max_rate_per_min;
        if (!check_rate_limit(pid, tool_name, min_interval_ns)) {
            // Rate limit exceeded
            struct violation_record *v;
            v = bpf_ringbuf_reserve(&security_violations, sizeof(*v), 0);
            if (v) {
                v->timestamp = bpf_ktime_get_ns();
                v->pid = pid;
                v->violation_type = 255;  // Rate limit violation
                __builtin_memcpy(v->tool, tool_name, sizeof(v->tool));
                bpf_ringbuf_submit(v, 0);
            }
            if (policy->enforce) {
                return false;
            }
        }
    }
    return true;
}
// Enhanced file access check with security
SEC("tracepoint/syscalls/sys_enter_openat")
int trace_mcp_resource_access_secure(struct trace_event_raw_sys_enter *ctx)
{
    if (!should_trace_process())
        return 0;
    u32 pid = bpf_get_current_pid_tgid() >> 32;
    struct server_stats *server = bpf_map_lookup_elem(&server_stats_map, &pid);
    if (!server)
        return 0;
    const char *filename = (const char *)ctx->args[1];
    int flags = (int)ctx->args[2];
    char path[256];
    bpf_probe_read_user_str(path, sizeof(path), filename);
    u8 access_type = (flags & 0x0001) ? MCP_ACCESS_WRITE : MCP_ACCESS_READ;
    // Check security policy
    if (!check_path_policy(path, access_type, pid)) {
        // Access denied
        struct mcp_event event = {};
        fill_event_header(&event.hdr, EVENT_FILE_OPEN);
        event.mcp_event_type = MCP_RESOURCE_READ;
        event.access_type = access_type;
        event.result = 1;  // Denied
        __builtin_memcpy(event.resource_uri, path, sizeof(path));
        emit_mcp_event(&event);
        // Update violation count
        __sync_fetch_and_add(&server->policy_violations, 1);
        // Note: We can't actually block the syscall from eBPF
        // This is for monitoring/auditing only
        // Actual blocking would require LSM BPF or seccomp
    }
    return 0;
}
// Pattern detection for suspicious behavior
struct suspicious_pattern {
    u32 rapid_file_access_count;
    u32 large_file_access_count;
    u32 sensitive_path_access_count;
    u64 last_check_time;
};
struct {
    __uint(type, BPF_MAP_TYPE_HASH);
    __uint(max_entries, 256);
    __type(key, u32);  // PID
    __type(value, struct suspicious_pattern);
} pattern_detection SEC(".maps");
static __always_inline void detect_suspicious_patterns(u32 pid)
{
    struct suspicious_pattern *pattern = bpf_map_lookup_elem(&pattern_detection, &pid);
    u64 now = bpf_ktime_get_ns();
    if (!pattern) {
        struct suspicious_pattern new_pattern = {
            .last_check_time = now,
        };
        bpf_map_update_elem(&pattern_detection, &pid, &new_pattern, BPF_ANY);
        return;
    }
    // Check if we should reset counters (every 60 seconds)
    u64 elapsed = now - pattern->last_check_time;
    if (elapsed > 60ULL * 1000000000ULL) {
        pattern->rapid_file_access_count = 0;
        pattern->large_file_access_count = 0;
        pattern->sensitive_path_access_count = 0;
        pattern->last_check_time = now;
    }
    // Increment appropriate counter
    __sync_fetch_and_add(&pattern->rapid_file_access_count, 1);
    // Alert if threshold exceeded
    if (pattern->rapid_file_access_count > 1000) {
        struct violation_record *v;
        v = bpf_ringbuf_reserve(&security_violations, sizeof(*v), 0);
        if (v) {
            v->timestamp = now;
            v->pid = pid;
            v->violation_type = 254;  // Suspicious pattern
            bpf_ringbuf_submit(v, 0);
        }
    }
}

Step 4: MCP Server Detection
pkg/mcp/detector.go
go -237 lines

package mcp
import (
    "bufio"
    "fmt"
    "os"
    "path/filepath"
    "regexp"
    "strings"
    "github.com/yourorg/neurontrace/pkg/types"
)
type MCPDetector struct {
    servers []types.MCPServerInfo
}
func NewMCPDetector() *MCPDetector {
    return &MCPDetector{
        servers: make([]types.MCPServerInfo, 0),
    }
}
func (d *MCPDetector) DetectServers() ([]types.MCPServerInfo, error) {
    // Method 1: Check running processes
    procServers, err := d.detectFromProcesses()
    if err == nil {
        d.servers = append(d.servers, procServers...)
    }
    // Method 2: Check network connections
    netServers, err := d.detectFromNetworkConnections()
    if err == nil {
        d.servers = append(d.servers, netServers...)
    }
    // Method 3: Check environment variables
    envServers, err := d.detectFromEnvironment()
    if err == nil {
        d.servers = append(d.servers, envServers...)
    }
    if len(d.servers) == 0 {
        return nil, fmt.Errorf("no MCP servers detected")
    }
    return d.servers, nil
}
func (d *MCPDetector) detectFromProcesses() ([]types.MCPServerInfo, error) {
    servers := make([]types.MCPServerInfo, 0)
    // Read /proc to find MCP server processes
    procDir := "/proc"
    entries, err := os.ReadDir(procDir)
    if err != nil {
        return nil, err
    }
    mcpPattern := regexp.MustCompile(`mcp[-_]?server|mcpd`)
    for _, entry := range entries {
        if !entry.IsDir() {
            continue
        }
        // Try to parse PID
        var pid uint32
        if _, err := fmt.Sscanf(entry.Name(), "%d", &pid); err != nil {
            continue
        }
        // Read cmdline
        cmdlinePath := filepath.Join(procDir, entry.Name(), "cmdline")
        cmdlineData, err := os.ReadFile(cmdlinePath)
        if err != nil {
            continue
        }
        cmdline := string(cmdlineData)
        // Check if it's an MCP server
        if mcpPattern.MatchString(cmdline) {
            server := types.MCPServerInfo{
                PID:  pid,
                Name: extractServerName(cmdline),
            }
            // Try to get more info
            d.enrichServerInfo(&server)
            servers = append(servers, server)
        }
    }
    return servers, nil
}
func (d *MCPDetector) detectFromNetworkConnections() ([]types.MCPServerInfo, error) {
    servers := make([]types.MCPServerInfo, 0)
    // Read /proc/net/tcp to find listening MCP servers
    tcpFile, err := os.Open("/proc/net/tcp")
    if err != nil {
        return nil, err
    }
    defer tcpFile.Close()
    scanner := bufio.NewScanner(tcpFile)
    scanner.Scan() // Skip header
    for scanner.Scan() {
        line := scanner.Text()
        fields := strings.Fields(line)
        if len(fields) < 10 {
            continue
        }
        // Check if listening (state 0A = LISTEN)
        if fields[3] != "0A" {
            continue
        }
        // Parse local address and port
        localAddr := fields[1]
        parts := strings.Split(localAddr, ":")
        if len(parts) != 2 {
            continue
        }
        var port uint32
        fmt.Sscanf(parts[1], "%X", &port)
        // Common MCP ports: 3000-3999, 8000-8999
        if (port >= 3000 && port <= 3999) || (port >= 8000 && port <= 8999) {
            // Try to find the process
            inode := fields[9]
            pid := d.findPIDByInode(inode)
            if pid > 0 {
                server := types.MCPServerInfo{
                    PID:  pid,
                    Port: port,
                }
                d.enrichServerInfo(&server)
                servers = append(servers, server)
            }
        }
    }
    return servers, nil
}
func (d *MCPDetector) detectFromEnvironment() ([]types.MCPServerInfo, error) {
    servers := make([]types.MCPServerInfo, 0)
    // Check common MCP environment variables
    mcpEnvVars := []string{
        "MCP_SERVER_URL",
        "MCP_SERVER_PORT",
        "MCP_SERVER_NAME",
    }
    for _, envVar := range mcpEnvVars {
        if value := os.Getenv(envVar); value != "" {
            // Parse the value and create server info
            // This is simplified - real implementation would parse URLs, etc.
            server := types.MCPServerInfo{
                Name: value,
            }
            servers = append(servers, server)
        }
    }
    return servers, nil
}
func (d *MCPDetector) enrichServerInfo(server *types.MCPServerInfo) {
    if server.PID == 0 {
        return
    }
    // Read process info
    cmdlinePath := fmt.Sprintf("/proc/%d/cmdline", server.PID)
    cmdlineData, err := os.ReadFile(cmdlinePath)
    if err == nil {
        cmdline := string(cmdlineData)
        if server.Name == "" {
            server.Name = extractServerName(cmdline)
        }
        // Try to detect protocol
        if strings.Contains(cmdline, "stdio") {
            server.Protocol = "stdio"
        } else if strings.Contains(cmdline, "http") {
            server.Protocol = "http"
        } else if strings.Contains(cmdline, "sse") {
            server.Protocol = "sse"
        }
    }
    // Try to read server manifest/config
    // Look for common config file locations
    configPaths := []string{
        fmt.Sprintf("/proc/%d/cwd/mcp.json", server.PID),
        fmt.Sprintf("/proc/%d/cwd/.mcp/config.json", server.PID),
    }
    for _, configPath := range configPaths {
        if info := d.readServerConfig(configPath); info != nil {
            server.Version = info.Version
            server.Tools = info.Tools
            server.Resources = info.Resources
            server.Capabilities = info.Capabilities
            break
        }
    }
}
func (d *MCPDetector) readServerConfig(configPath string) *types.MCPServerInfo {
    // Placeholder - would parse JSON config
    return nil
}
func (d *MCPDetector) findPIDByInode(inode string) uint32 {
    procDir := "/proc"
    entries, err := os.ReadDir(procDir)
    if err != nil {
        return 0
    }
    for _, entry := range entries {
        if !entry.IsDir() {
            continue
        }
        var pid uint32
        if _, err := fmt.Sscanf(entry.Name(), "%d", &pid); err != nil {
            continue
        }
        fdDir := filepath.Join(procDir, entry.Name(), "fd")
        fdEntries, err := os.ReadDir(fdDir)
        if err != nil {
            continue
        }
        for _, fdEntry := range fdEntries {
            linkPath := filepath.Join(fdDir, fdEntry.Name())
            target, err := os.Readlink(linkPath)
            if err != nil {
                continue
            }
            if strings.Contains(target, inode) {
                return pid
            }
        }
    }
    return 0
}
func extractServerName(cmdline string) string {
    // Extract server name from command line
    parts := strings.Split(cmdline, "\x00")
    for _, part := range parts {
        if strings.Contains(part, "mcp") {
            // Extract just the binary name
            return filepath.Base(part)
        }
    }
    return "unknown"
}
// Get tools available on an MCP server
func (d *MCPDetector) GetServerTools(serverPID uint32) ([]types.MCPTool, error) {
    // This would typically query the server's /tools endpoint
    // For now, return empty list
    return []types.MCPTool{}, nil
}
// Get resources available on an MCP server
func (d *MCPDetector) GetServerResources(serverPID uint32) ([]types.MCPResource, error) {
    // This would typically query the server's /resources endpoint
    return []types.MCPResource{}, nil
}




Step 5: MCP Protocol Parser

package mcp
import (
    "encoding/json"
    "fmt"
    "github.com/yourorg/neurontrace/pkg/types"
)
// MCP JSON-RPC message structure
type MCPMessage struct {
    JSONRPC string          `json:"jsonrpc"`
    ID      interface{}     `json:"id,omitempty"`
    Method  string          `json:"method,omitempty"`
    Params  json.RawMessage `json:"params,omitempty"`
    Result  json.RawMessage `json:"result,omitempty"`
    Error   *MCPError       `json:"error,omitempty"`
}
type MCPError struct {
    Code    int    `json:"code"`
    Message string `json:"message"`
    Data    interface{} `json:"data,omitempty"`
}
// Tool call parameters
type ToolCallParams struct {
    Name      string                 `json:"name"`
    Arguments map[string]interface{} `json:"arguments,omitempty"`
}
// Resource read parameters
type ResourceReadParams struct {
    URI string `json:"uri"`
}
type MCPParser struct{}
func NewMCPParser() *MCPParser {
    return &MCPParser{}
}
func (p *MCPParser) ParseMessage(data []byte) (*MCPMessage, error) {
    var msg MCPMessage
    if err := json.Unmarshal(data, &msg); err != nil {
        return nil, fmt.Errorf("failed to parse MCP message: %w", err)
    }
    return &msg, nil
}
func (p *MCPParser) IsToolCall(msg *MCPMessage) bool {
    return msg.Method == "tools/call"
}
func (p *MCPParser) IsResourceRead(msg *MCPMessage) bool {
    return msg.Method == "resources/read"
}
func (p *MCPParser) IsPromptRequest(msg *MCPMessage) bool {
    return msg.Method == "prompts/get"
}
func (p *MCPParser) ExtractToolCall(msg *MCPMessage) (*ToolCallParams, error) {
    if !p.IsToolCall(msg) {
        return nil, fmt.Errorf("not a tool call message")
    }
    var params ToolCallParams
    if err := json.Unmarshal(msg.Params, &params); err != nil {
        return nil, err
    }
    return &params, nil
}
func (p *MCPParser) ExtractResourceRead(msg *MCPMessage) (*ResourceReadParams, error) {
    if !p.IsResourceRead(msg) {
        return nil, fmt.Errorf("not a resource read message")
    }
    var params ResourceReadParams
    if err := json.Unmarshal(msg.Params, &params); err != nil {
        return nil, err
    }
    return &params, nil
}
func (p *MCPParser) CreateMCPEvent(msg *MCPMessage, serverPID uint32) (*types.MCPEvent, error) {
    event := &types.MCPEvent{
        EventHeader: types.EventHeader{
            PID: serverPID,
        },
        RequestSize: uint32(len(msg.Params)),
    }
    switch {
    case p.IsToolCall(msg):
        event.MCPEventType = types.MCPToolCall
        params, err := p.ExtractToolCall(msg)
        if err == nil {
            event.ToolName = params.Name
        }
    case p.IsResourceRead(msg):
        event.MCPEventType = types.MCPResourceRead
        params, err := p.ExtractResourceRead(msg)
        if err == nil {
            event.ResourceURI = params.URI
        }
    case p.IsPromptRequest(msg):
        event.MCPEventType = types.MCPPromptRequest
    }
    if msg.Error != nil {
        event.Result = 2  // Error
    } else if msg.Result != nil {
        event.Result = 0  // Success
        event.ResponseSize = uint32(len(msg.Result))
    }
    return event, nil
}




Step 6: Policy Engine
pkg/mcp/policy.go
go -223 lines

package mcp
import (
    "fmt"
    "os"
    "path/filepath"
    "strings"
    "time"
    "gopkg.in/yaml.v3"
    "github.com/yourorg/neurontrace/pkg/types"
)
type PolicyEngine struct {
    config       *types.PolicyConfig
    violations   []types.PolicyViolation
    lastViolation time.Time
}
func NewPolicyEngine(configPath string) (*PolicyEngine, error) {
    engine := &PolicyEngine{
        violations: make([]types.PolicyViolation, 0),
    }
    if err := engine.LoadConfig(configPath); err != nil {
        return nil, err
    }
    return engine, nil
}
func (e *PolicyEngine) LoadConfig(configPath string) error {
    data, err := os.ReadFile(configPath)
    if err != nil {
        return fmt.Errorf("failed to read policy config: %w", err)
    }
    var config types.PolicyConfig
    if err := yaml.Unmarshal(data, &config); err != nil {
        return fmt.Errorf("failed to parse policy config: %w", err)
    }
    e.config = &config
    return nil
}
func (e *PolicyEngine) CheckToolAccess(toolName string, serverPID uint32) (bool, string) {
    // Check tool-specific policy
    if policy, exists := e.config.ToolPolicies[toolName]; exists {
        if !policy.Enabled {
            return false, "tool disabled"
        }
        // Check rate limiting
        if policy.MaxRatePerMin > 0 {
            // Would check actual rate here
        }
        return true, ""
    }
    // Fall back to default policy
    if !e.config.DefaultPolicy.Enabled {
        return false, "default policy denies access"
    }
    return true, ""
}
func (e *PolicyEngine) CheckResourceAccess(
    resourceURI string,
    accessType types.MCPAccessType,
    toolName string,
    serverPID uint32,
) (bool, string) {
    // Find matching resource policy
    var matchedPolicy *types.ResourcePolicy
    for prefix, policy := range e.config.ResourcePolicies {
        if strings.HasPrefix(resourceURI, prefix) {
            matchedPolicy = &policy
            break
        }
    }
    if matchedPolicy == nil {
        // Use default policy
        return e.checkDefaultResourcePolicy(resourceURI, accessType)
    }
    // Check if tool is allowed
    if len(matchedPolicy.AllowedTools) > 0 {
        allowed := false
        for _, allowedTool := range matchedPolicy.AllowedTools {
            if allowedTool == toolName || allowedTool == "*" {
                allowed = true
                break
            }
        }
        if !allowed {
            return false, fmt.Sprintf("tool %s not allowed for resource", toolName)
        }
    }
    // Check if tool is denied
    for _, deniedTool := range matchedPolicy.DeniedTools {
        if deniedTool == toolName {
            return false, fmt.Sprintf("tool %s explicitly denied", toolName)
        }
    }
    // Check access type
    switch accessType {
    case types.MCPAccessRead:
        if !matchedPolicy.AllowRead {
            return false, "read access denied"
        }
    case types.MCPAccessWrite:
        if !matchedPolicy.AllowWrite {
            return false, "write access denied"
        }
    case types.MCPAccessExec:
        if !matchedPolicy.AllowExec {
            return false, "execute access denied"
        }
    case types.MCPAccessDelete:
        if !matchedPolicy.AllowDelete {
            return false, "delete access denied"
        }
    }
    return true, ""
}
func (e *PolicyEngine) checkDefaultResourcePolicy(
    resourceURI string,
    accessType types.MCPAccessType,
) (bool, string) {
    // Check sensitive paths
    sensitivePaths := []string{
        "/etc/",
        "/root/",
        "/sys/",
        "/proc/",
        "/.ssh/",
        "/.aws/",
        "/.kube/",
    }
    for _, sensitive := range sensitivePaths {
        if strings.Contains(resourceURI, sensitive) {
            return false, fmt.Sprintf("access to sensitive path %s denied", sensitive)
        }
    }
    // Check default policy
    switch accessType {
    case types.MCPAccessRead:
        return e.config.DefaultPolicy.AllowRead, "default policy"
    case types.MCPAccessWrite:
        return e.config.DefaultPolicy.AllowWrite, "default policy"
    case types.MCPAccessExec:
        return e.config.DefaultPolicy.AllowExec, "default policy"
    case types.MCPAccessDelete:
        return e.config.DefaultPolicy.AllowDelete, "default policy"
    }
    return false, "unknown access type"
}
func (e *PolicyEngine) RecordViolation(violation types.PolicyViolation) {
    e.violations = append(e.violations, violation)
    e.lastViolation = time.Now()
}
func (e *PolicyEngine) GetViolations() []types.PolicyViolation {
    return e.violations
}
func (e *PolicyEngine) GetViolationsSince(since time.Time) []types.PolicyViolation {
    result := make([]types.PolicyViolation, 0)
    for _, v := range e.violations {
        if v.Timestamp.After(since) {
            result = append(result, v)
        }
    }
    return result
}
func (e *PolicyEngine) ClearViolations() {
    e.violations = make([]types.PolicyViolation, 0)
}
// Detect suspicious patterns
func (e *PolicyEngine) DetectSuspiciousActivity(
    serverPID uint32,
    recentEvents []types.MCPEvent,
) []string {
    suspicious := make([]string, 0)
    if !e.config.EnableAnomalyDetection {
        return suspicious
    }
    // Count rapid file accesses
    fileAccessCount := 0
    for _, event := range recentEvents {
        if event.MCPEventType == types.MCPResourceRead ||
           event.MCPEventType == types.MCPResourceWrite {
            fileAccessCount++
        }
    }
    if fileAccessCount > int(e.config.SuspiciousThresholds.RapidFileAccessCount) {
        suspicious = append(suspicious, 
            fmt.Sprintf("rapid file access detected: %d accesses", fileAccessCount))
    }
    // Count failed attempts
    failedCount := 0
    for _, event := range recentEvents {
        if event.Result == 1 || event.Result == 2 {
            failedCount++
        }
    }
    if failedCount > int(e.config.SuspiciousThresholds.FailedAccessAttempts) {
        suspicious = append(suspicious,
            fmt.Sprintf("multiple failed access attempts: %d failures", failedCount))
    }
    // Check for sensitive path access
    sensitiveCount := 0
    for _, event := range recentEvents {
        if e.isSensitivePath(event.ResourceURI) {
            sensitiveCount++
        }
    }
    if sensitiveCount > int(e.config.SuspiciousThresholds.SensitivePathAccessCount) {
        suspicious = append(suspicious,
            fmt.Sprintf("suspicious sensitive path access: %d accesses", sensitiveCount))
    }
    return suspicious
}
func (e *PolicyEngine) isSensitivePath(path string) bool {
    sensitivePaths := []string{
        "/etc/passwd",
        "/etc/shadow",
        "/.ssh/",
        "/.aws/",
        "/root/",
    }
    for _, sensitive := range sensitivePaths {
        if strings.Contains(path, sensitive) {
            return true
        }
    }
    return false
}
