Step 8: MCP Agent Handler
pkg/agent/mcp.go
go -320 lines

package agent
import (
    "bytes"
    "encoding/binary"
    "fmt"
    "log"
    "time"
    "github.com/cilium/ebpf/ringbuf"
    "github.com/yourorg/neurontrace/pkg/mcp"
    "github.com/yourorg/neurontrace/pkg/types"
)
// MCP event from eBPF (must match C struct)
type mcpEventRaw struct {
    Header        eventHeaderRaw
    MCPEventType  uint8
    AccessType    uint8
    Result        uint8
    DurationUs    uint32
    ToolName      [64]byte
    ResourceURI   [256]byte
    ServerName    [64]byte
    RequestSize   uint32
    ResponseSize  uint32
    ClientPID     uint32
    ServerPort    uint32
    ConnectionID  uint32
}
func (a *Agent) startMCPMonitoring() error {
    // Detect MCP servers
    detector := mcp.NewMCPDetector()
    servers, err := detector.DetectServers()
    if err != nil {
        log.Printf("⚠ No MCP servers detected: %v", err)
        return nil  // Not an error, just skip MCP monitoring
    }
    log.Printf("✓ Detected %d MCP server(s)", len(servers))
    for _, s := range servers {
        log.Printf("  - %s (PID: %d, Port: %d)", s.Name, s.PID, s.Port)
    }
    // Load policy engine
    policyEngine, err := mcp.NewPolicyEngine(a.config.MCPPolicyPath)
    if err != nil {
        log.Printf("⚠ Failed to load MCP policies: %v", err)
        // Continue with default policies
    }
    a.mcpPolicy = policyEngine
    // Load MCP eBPF programs
    if err := a.loadMCPPrograms(); err != nil {
        return fmt.Errorf("failed to load MCP programs: %w", err)
    }
    // Start event processing
    rb, ok := a.objs.Maps["mcp_events"]
    if !ok {
        return fmt.Errorf("mcp_events map not found")
    }
    reader, err := ringbuf.NewReader(rb)
    if err != nil {
        return fmt.Errorf("failed to create MCP reader: %w", err)
    }
    a.readers = append(a.readers, reader)
    go a.processMCPEvents(reader)
    // Start security violation monitoring
    violationRB, ok := a.objs.Maps["security_violations"]
    if ok {
        violationReader, err := ringbuf.NewReader(violationRB)
        if err == nil {
            a.readers = append(a.readers, violationReader)
            go a.processSecurityViolations(violationReader)
        }
    }
    // Start MCP stats collector
    go a.collectMCPStats()
    log.Println("✓ MCP monitoring started")
    return nil
}
func (a *Agent) loadMCPPrograms() error {
    // MCP programs are already loaded as part of the main collection
    // Just need to ensure they're attached
    log.Println("MCP eBPF programs loaded")
    return nil
}
func (a *Agent) processMCPEvents(reader *ringbuf.Reader) {
    log.Println("MCP event processing loop started")
    recentEvents := make([]types.MCPEvent, 0, 100)
    for {
        select {
        case <-a.ctx.Done():
            return
        default:
            record, err := reader.Read()
            if err != nil {
                continue
            }
            var raw mcpEventRaw
            if err := binary.Read(
                bytes.NewReader(record.RawSample),
                binary.LittleEndian,
                &raw,
            ); err != nil {
                log.Printf("Failed to parse MCP event: %v\n", err)
                continue
            }
            event := a.parseMCPEvent(&raw)
            a.handleMCPEvent(event)
            a.metrics.EventsProcessed.Inc()
            // Store for pattern analysis
            recentEvents = append(recentEvents, *event)
            if len(recentEvents) > 100 {
                recentEvents = recentEvents[1:]
            }
            // Periodic pattern analysis
            if len(recentEvents) >= 50 {
                a.analyzeMCPPatterns(event.PID, recentEvents)
            }
        }
    }
}
func (a *Agent) parseMCPEvent(raw *mcpEventRaw) *types.MCPEvent {
    event := &types.MCPEvent{
        EventHeader:   parseEventHeader(&raw.Header),
        MCPEventType:  types.MCPEventType(raw.MCPEventType),
        AccessType:    types.MCPAccessType(raw.AccessType),
        Result:        raw.Result,
        DurationUs:    raw.DurationUs,
        ToolName:      string(bytes.TrimRight(raw.ToolName[:], "\x00")),
        ResourceURI:   string(bytes.TrimRight(raw.ResourceURI[:], "\x00")),
        ServerName:    string(bytes.TrimRight(raw.ServerName[:], "\x00")),
        RequestSize:   raw.RequestSize,
        ResponseSize:  raw.ResponseSize,
        ClientPID:     raw.ClientPID,
        ServerPort:    raw.ServerPort,
        ConnectionID:  raw.ConnectionID,
    }
    return event
}
func (a *Agent) handleMCPEvent(event *types.MCPEvent) {
    // Update metrics based on event type
    switch event.MCPEventType {
    case types.MCPToolCall:
        a.metrics.MCPToolCalls.WithLabelValues(
            event.ToolName,
            event.ServerName,
        ).Inc()
        if event.Result == 0 {
            a.metrics.MCPToolCallsSuccess.WithLabelValues(
                event.ToolName,
            ).Inc()
        } else if event.Result == 1 {
            a.metrics.MCPToolCallsDenied.WithLabelValues(
                event.ToolName,
            ).Inc()
        } else {
            a.metrics.MCPToolCallsError.WithLabelValues(
                event.ToolName,
            ).Inc()
        }
        a.metrics.MCPToolDuration.WithLabelValues(
            event.ToolName,
        ).Observe(float64(event.DurationUs) / 1000000.0)
    case types.MCPResourceRead, types.MCPResourceWrite:
        accessType := "read"
        if event.MCPEventType == types.MCPResourceWrite {
            accessType = "write"
        }
        a.metrics.MCPResourceAccess.WithLabelValues(
            accessType,
            event.ToolName,
        ).Inc()
        if event.Result == 1 {
            a.metrics.MCPResourceAccessDenied.WithLabelValues(
                accessType,
                event.ResourceURI,
            ).Inc()
        }
    case types.MCPConnectionOpen:
        a.metrics.MCPConnections.WithLabelValues(
            event.ServerName,
        ).Inc()
        a.metrics.MCPActiveConnections.WithLabelValues(
            event.ServerName,
        ).Inc()
    case types.MCPConnectionClose:
        a.metrics.MCPActiveConnections.WithLabelValues(
            event.ServerName,
        ).Dec()
    }
    // Log interesting events
    if a.config.LogLevel == "debug" || event.Result != 0 {
        log.Printf("MCP Event: %s called %s on %s - Result: %d",
            event.ServerName, event.ToolName, event.ResourceURI, event.Result)
    }
}
func (a *Agent) processSecurityViolations(reader *ringbuf.Reader) {
    log.Println("Security violation monitoring started")
    for {
        select {
        case <-a.ctx.Done():
            return
        default:
            record, err := reader.Read()
            if err != nil {
                continue
            }
            var raw struct {
                Timestamp uint64
                PID       uint32
                ViolationType uint8
                Resource  [256]byte
                Tool      [64]byte
            }
            if err := binary.Read(
                bytes.NewReader(record.RawSample),
                binary.LittleEndian,
                &raw,
            ); err != nil {
                continue
            }
            violation := types.SecurityViolation{
                Timestamp:     time.Unix(0, int64(raw.Timestamp)),
                PID:           raw.PID,
                ViolationType: raw.ViolationType,
                Resource:      string(bytes.TrimRight(raw.Resource[:], "\x00")),
                Tool:          string(bytes.TrimRight(raw.Tool[:], "\x00")),
                Severity:      "medium",
                Action:        "audit",
            }
            // Determine severity
            if raw.ViolationType == 254 || raw.ViolationType == 255 {
                violation.Severity = "high"
            }
            // Record violation
            if a.mcpPolicy != nil {
                a.mcpPolicy.RecordViolation(violation)
            }
            // Update metrics
            a.metrics.MCPSecurityViolations.WithLabelValues(
                violation.Tool,
                violation.Severity,
            ).Inc()
            // Log violation
            log.Printf("⚠ Security Violation: PID=%d Tool=%s Resource=%s Type=%d",
                violation.PID, violation.Tool, violation.Resource, violation.ViolationType)
        }
    }
}
func (a *Agent) analyzeMCPPatterns(serverPID uint32, events []types.MCPEvent) {
    if a.mcpPolicy == nil {
        return
    }
    suspicious := a.mcpPolicy.DetectSuspiciousActivity(serverPID, events)
    for _, pattern := range suspicious {
        log.Printf("🔍 Suspicious Activity Detected: %s", pattern)
        a.metrics.MCPSuspiciousActivity.WithLabelValues(
            pattern,
        ).Inc()
    }
}
func (a *Agent) collectMCPStats() {
    ticker := time.NewTicker(10 * time.Second)
    defer ticker.Stop()
    for {
        select {
        case <-a.ctx.Done():
            return
        case <-ticker.C:
            a.updateMCPMapStats()
        }
    }
}
func (a *Agent) updateMCPMapStats() {
    // Read tool stats from eBPF map
    toolStatsMap, ok := a.objs.Maps["tool_stats_map"]
    if !ok {
        return
    }
    var toolName [64]byte
    var stats struct {
        CallCount         uint64
        SuccessCount      uint64
        DeniedCount       uint64
        ErrorCount        uint64
        TotalDurationUs   uint64
        TotalBytesRead    uint64
        TotalBytesWritten uint64
        ConcurrentCalls   uint32
    }
    iter := toolStatsMap.Iterate()
    for iter.Next(&toolName, &stats) {
        tool := string(bytes.TrimRight(toolName[:], "\x00"))
        // Update per-tool metrics
        a.metrics.MCPToolCallsTotal.WithLabelValues(tool).Set(float64(stats.CallCount))
        a.metrics.MCPToolBytesRead.WithLabelValues(tool).Set(float64(stats.TotalBytesRead))
        a.metrics.MCPToolBytesWritten.WithLabelValues(tool).Set(float64(stats.TotalBytesWritten))
        if stats.CallCount > 0 {
            avgDuration := float64(stats.TotalDurationUs) / float64(stats.CallCount) / 1000.0
            a.metrics.MCPToolAvgDuration.WithLabelValues(tool).Set(avgDuration)
        }
    }
    // Read server stats
    serverStatsMap, ok := a.objs.Maps["server_stats_map"]
    if !ok {
        return
    }
    var pid uint32
    var serverStats struct {
        TotalRequests          uint64
        ActiveConnections      uint64
        TotalToolsCalled       uint64
        TotalResourcesAccessed uint64
        PolicyViolations       uint64
        StartTime              uint64
    }
    serverIter := serverStatsMap.Iterate()
    for serverIter.Next(&pid, &serverStats) {
        pidStr := fmt.Sprintf("%d", pid)
        a.metrics.MCPServerRequests.WithLabelValues(pidStr).Set(float64(serverStats.TotalRequests))
        a.metrics.MCPServerConnections.WithLabelValues(pidStr).Set(float64(serverStats.ActiveConnections))
        a.metrics.MCPServerViolations.WithLabelValues(pidStr).Set(float64(serverStats.PolicyViolations))
    }
}

Step 10: MCP Test Server
scripts/test-mcp-server.py

#!/usr/bin/env python3
"""
Test MCP server for NeuronTrace monitoring
Implements a simple MCP server with various tools
"""
import asyncio
import json
import sys
import time
import os
from typing import Any, Dict, List, Optional
from dataclasses import dataclass
import argparse
# Simple MCP server implementation
@dataclass
class MCPTool:
    name: str
    description: str
    input_schema: Dict[str, Any]
@dataclass
class MCPResource:
    uri: str
    name: str
    description: str
    mime_type: str
class SimpleMCPServer:
    def __init__(self, name: str = "test-mcp-server"):
        self.name = name
        self.tools = self._register_tools()
        self.resources = self._register_resources()
        self.request_count = 0
        self.start_time = time.time()
    def _register_tools(self) -> List[MCPTool]:
        return [
            MCPTool(
                name="filesystem",
                description="Read and write files",
                input_schema={
                    "type": "object",
                    "properties": {
                        "path": {"type": "string"},
                        "operation": {"type": "string", "enum": ["read", "write"]},
                        "content": {"type": "string"}
                    },
                    "required": ["path", "operation"]
                }
            ),
            MCPTool(
                name="web_search",
                description="Search the web",
                input_schema={
                    "type": "object",
                    "properties": {
                        "query": {"type": "string"},
                        "max_results": {"type": "integer"}
                    },
                    "required": ["query"]
                }
            ),
            MCPTool(
                name="database",
                description="Query database",
                input_schema={
                    "type": "object",
                    "properties": {
                        "query": {"type": "string"},
                        "database": {"type": "string"}
                    },
                    "required": ["query"]
                }
            ),
        ]
    def _register_resources(self) -> List[MCPResource]:
        return [
            MCPResource(
                uri="file:///tmp/test.txt",
                name="test.txt",
                description="Test file",
                mime_type="text/plain"
            ),
            MCPResource(
                uri="file:///home/user/documents",
                name="documents",
                description="User documents",
                mime_type="inode/directory"
            ),
        ]
    async def handle_request(self, request: Dict[str, Any]) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        """Handle MCP JSON-RPC request"""
        self.request_count += 1
        method = request.get("method")
        params = request.get("params", {})
        request_id = request.get("id")
        print(f"📨 Request #{self.request_count}: {method}")
        if method == "initialize":
            return self._handle_initialize(request_id)
        elif method == "tools/list":
            return self._handle_tools_list(request_id)
        elif method == "tools/call":
            return await self._handle_tool_call(request_id, params)
        elif method == "resources/list":
            return self._handle_resources_list(request_id)
        elif method == "resources/read":
            return await self._handle_resource_read(request_id, params)
        else:
            return self._error_response(request_id, -32601, f"Method not found: {method}")
    def _handle_initialize(self, request_id: Any) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        return {
            "jsonrpc": "2.0",
            "id": request_id,
            "result": {
                "protocolVersion": "2024-11-05",
                "serverInfo": {
                    "name": self.name,
                    "version": "0.1.0"
                },
                "capabilities": {
                    "tools": {},
                    "resources": {}
                }
            }
        }
    def _handle_tools_list(self, request_id: Any) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        return {
            "jsonrpc": "2.0",
            "id": request_id,
            "result": {
                "tools": [
                    {
                        "name": tool.name,
                        "description": tool.description,
                        "inputSchema": tool.input_schema
                    }
                    for tool in self.tools
                ]
            }
        }
    async def _handle_tool_call(self, request_id: Any, params: Dict[str, Any]) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        tool_name = params.get("name")
        arguments = params.get("arguments", {})
        print(f"  🔧 Tool: {tool_name}")
        print(f"  📋 Args: {arguments}")
        # Simulate tool execution
        await asyncio.sleep(0.1)  # Simulate work
        if tool_name == "filesystem":
            return await self._execute_filesystem(request_id, arguments)
        elif tool_name == "web_search":
            return await self._execute_web_search(request_id, arguments)
        elif tool_name == "database":
            return await self._execute_database(request_id, arguments)
        else:
            return self._error_response(request_id, -32602, f"Unknown tool: {tool_name}")
    async def _execute_filesystem(self, request_id: Any, args: Dict[str, Any]) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        path = args.get("path")
        operation = args.get("operation")
        if operation == "read":
            # Simulate file read
            try:
                if os.path.exists(path):
                    with open(path, 'r') as f:
                        content = f.read()
                else:
                    content = f"File not found: {path}"
                return {
                    "jsonrpc": "2.0",
                    "id": request_id,
                    "result": {
                        "content": [
                            {
                                "type": "text",
                                "text": content
                            }
                        ]
                    }
                }
            except Exception as e:
                return self._error_response(request_id, -32000, str(e))
        elif operation == "write":
            content = args.get("content", "")
            try:
                with open(path, 'w') as f:
                    f.write(content)
                return {
                    "jsonrpc": "2.0",
                    "id": request_id,
                    "result": {
                        "content": [
                            {
                                "type": "text",
                                "text": f"Written {len(content)} bytes to {path}"
                            }
                        ]
                    }
                }
            except Exception as e:
                return self._error_response(request_id, -32000, str(e))
    async def _execute_web_search(self, request_id: Any, args: Dict[str, Any]) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        query = args.get("query")
        max_results = args.get("max_results", 5)
        # Simulate web search
        await asyncio.sleep(0.2)
        results = [
            f"Result {i+1} for '{query}'"
            for i in range(max_results)
        ]
        return {
            "jsonrpc": "2.0",
            "id": request_id,
            "result": {
                "content": [
                    {
                        "type": "text",
                        "text": "\n".join(results)
                    }
                ]
            }
        }
    async def _execute_database(self, request_id: Any, args: Dict[str, Any]) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        query = args.get("query")
        database = args.get("database", "default")
        # Simulate database query
        await asyncio.sleep(0.15)
        return {
            "jsonrpc": "2.0",
            "id": request_id,
            "result": {
                "content": [
                    {
                        "type": "text",
                        "text": f"Query executed on {database}: {query}\nReturned 42 rows"
                    }
                ]
            }
        }
    def _handle_resources_list(self, request_id: Any) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        return {
            "jsonrpc": "2.0",
            "id": request_id,
            "result": {
                "resources": [
                    {
                        "uri": resource.uri,
                        "name": resource.name,
                        "description": resource.description,
                        "mimeType": resource.mime_type
                    }
                    for resource in self.resources
                ]
            }
        }
    async def _handle_resource_read(self, request_id: Any, params: Dict[str, Any]) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        uri = params.get("uri")
        # Find resource
        resource = next((r for r in self.resources if r.uri == uri), None)
        if not resource:
            return self._error_response(request_id, -32602, f"Resource not found: {uri}")
        # Simulate reading resource
        await asyncio.sleep(0.1)
        return {
            "jsonrpc": "2.0",
            "id": request_id,
            "result": {
                "contents": [
                    {
                        "uri": resource.uri,
                        "mimeType": resource.mime_type,
                        "text": f"Content of {resource.name}"
                    }
                ]
            }
        }
    def _error_response(self, request_id: Any, code: int, message: str) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        return {
            "jsonrpc": "2.0",
            "id": request_id,
            "error": {
                "code": code,
                "message": message
            }
        }
    async def run_stdio(self):
        """Run server using stdio transport"""
        print(f"🚀 {self.name} started (stdio mode)", file=sys.stderr)
        print(f"   PID: {os.getpid()}", file=sys.stderr)
        print(f"   Registered {len(self.tools)} tools", file=sys.stderr)
        print(f"   Registered {len(self.resources)} resources", file=sys.stderr)
        print("", file=sys.stderr)
        while True:
            try:
                # Read JSON-RPC request from stdin
                line = sys.stdin.readline()
                if not line:
                    break
                request = json.loads(line)
                response = await self.handle_request(request)
                # Write response to stdout
                print(json.dumps(response), flush=True)
            except json.JSONDecodeError as e:
                print(f"❌ JSON decode error: {e}", file=sys.stderr)
            except Exception as e:
                print(f"❌ Error: {e}", file=sys.stderr)
    def print_stats(self):
        """Print server statistics"""
        uptime = time.time() - self.start_time
        print(f"\n📊 Server Statistics:", file=sys.stderr)
        print(f"   Uptime: {uptime:.2f}s", file=sys.stderr)
        print(f"   Total requests: {self.request_count}", file=sys.stderr)
        print(f"   Requests/sec: {self.request_count/uptime:.2f}", file=sys.stderr)
async def main():
    parser = argparse.ArgumentParser(description='Test MCP server for NeuronTrace')
    parser.add_argument('--name', default='test-mcp-server', help='Server name')
    parser.add_argument('--transport', choices=['stdio', 'http'], default='stdio', help='Transport type')
    args = parser.parse_args()
    server = SimpleMCPServer(name=args.name)
    try:
        if args.transport == 'stdio':
            await server.run_stdio()
        else:
            print("HTTP transport not yet implemented", file=sys.stderr)
            sys.exit(1)
    except KeyboardInterrupt:
        server.print_stats()
        print("\n👋 Server stopped", file=sys.stderr)
if __name__ == '__main__':
    asyncio.run(main())




Step 11: MCP Test Client
scripts/test-mcp-client.py
python -235 lines

#!/usr/bin/env python3
"""
Test MCP client for NeuronTrace monitoring
Generates various MCP requests for testing
"""
import asyncio
import json
import sys
import subprocess
import time
import argparse
from typing import Any, Dict, Optional
class MCPClient:
    def __init__(self, server_command: str):
        self.server_command = server_command
        self.process: Optional[subprocess.Popen] = None
        self.request_id = 0
    async def start(self):
        """Start MCP server process"""
        self.process = subprocess.Popen(
            self.server_command,
            shell=True,
            stdin=subprocess.PIPE,
            stdout=subprocess.PIPE,
            stderr=subprocess.PIPE,
            text=True,
            bufsize=1
        )
        # Wait a bit for server to start
        await asyncio.sleep(0.5)
        # Initialize
        response = await self.send_request("initialize", {
            "protocolVersion": "2024-11-05",
            "clientInfo": {
                "name": "test-client",
                "version": "0.1.0"
            }
        })
        print(f"✓ Connected to server: {response['result']['serverInfo']['name']}")
    async def send_request(self, method: str, params: Optional[Dict[str, Any]] = None) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        """Send JSON-RPC request to server"""
        self.request_id += 1
        request = {
            "jsonrpc": "2.0",
            "id": self.request_id,
            "method": method
        }
        if params:
            request["params"] = params
        # Send request
        self.process.stdin.write(json.dumps(request) + "\n")
        self.process.stdin.flush()
        # Read response
        response_line = self.process.stdout.readline()
        response = json.loads(response_line)
        return response
    async def list_tools(self):
        """List available tools"""
        response = await self.send_request("tools/list")
        tools = response['result']['tools']
        print(f"\n📦 Available tools ({len(tools)}):")
        for tool in tools:
            print(f"  - {tool['name']}: {tool['description']}")
        return tools
    async def call_tool(self, name: str, arguments: Dict[str, Any]):
        """Call a tool"""
        start = time.time()
        response = await self.send_request("tools/call", {
            "name": name,
            "arguments": arguments
        })
        duration = (time.time() - start) * 1000
        if "error" in response:
            print(f"❌ Tool call failed: {response['error']['message']}")
            return None
        print(f"✓ Tool '{name}' completed in {duration:.2f}ms")
        return response['result']
    async def list_resources(self):
        """List available resources"""
        response = await self.send_request("resources/list")
        resources = response['result']['resources']
        print(f"\n📁 Available resources ({len(resources)}):")
        for resource in resources:
            print(f"  - {resource['uri']}: {resource['name']}")
        return resources
    async def read_resource(self, uri: str):
        """Read a resource"""
        start = time.time()
        response = await self.send_request("resources/read", {
            "uri": uri
        })
        duration = (time.time() - start) * 1000
        if "error" in response:
            print(f"❌ Resource read failed: {response['error']['message']}")
            return None
        print(f"✓ Resource read completed in {duration:.2f}ms")
        return response['result']
    async def stop(self):
        """Stop server process"""
        if self.process:
            self.process.terminate()
            self.process.wait()
async def run_test_workload(client: MCPClient, args):
    """Run various test scenarios"""
    print("\n" + "="*60)
    print("🧪 Starting MCP Test Workload")
    print("="*60)
    # Test 1: List tools
    print("\n[Test 1] Listing tools...")
    await client.list_tools()
    # Test 2: Filesystem operations
    if args.test_filesystem:
        print("\n[Test 2] Testing filesystem tool...")
        # Create test file
        test_file = "/tmp/neurontrace_test.txt"
        # Write
        await client.call_tool("filesystem", {
            "path": test_file,
            "operation": "write",
            "content": "Hello from NeuronTrace test!"
        })
        # Read
        await client.call_tool("filesystem", {
            "path": test_file,
            "operation": "read"
        })
        # Try to access restricted path (should trigger security violation)
        await client.call_tool("filesystem", {
            "path": "/etc/passwd",
            "operation": "read"
        })
    # Test 3: Web search
    if args.test_search:
        print("\n[Test 3] Testing web_search tool...")
        queries = [
            "machine learning",
            "eBPF monitoring",
            "AI observability"
        ]
        for query in queries:
            await client.call_tool("web_search", {
                "query": query,
                "max_results": 3
            })
            await asyncio.sleep(0.5)
    # Test 4: Database queries
    if args.test_database:
        print("\n[Test 4] Testing database tool...")
        queries = [
            "SELECT * FROM users LIMIT 10",
            "SELECT COUNT(*) FROM events",
            "SELECT * FROM metrics WHERE timestamp > NOW() - INTERVAL '1 hour'"
        ]
        for query in queries:
            await client.call_tool("database", {
                "query": query,
                "database": "test_db"
            })
            await asyncio.sleep(0.3)
    # Test 5: Resource access
    if args.test_resources:
        print("\n[Test 5] Testing resource access...")
        resources = await client.list_resources()
        for resource in resources[:3]:
            await client.read_resource(resource['uri'])
            await asyncio.sleep(0.2)
    # Test 6: Rapid requests (stress test)
    if args.stress_test:
        print(f"\n[Test 6] Stress test ({args.stress_requests} requests)...")
        start = time.time()
        for i in range(args.stress_requests):
            await client.call_tool("filesystem", {
                "path": f"/tmp/stress_test_{i}.txt",
                "operation": "read"
            })
            if (i + 1) % 10 == 0:
                elapsed = time.time() - start
                rate = (i + 1) / elapsed
                print(f"  Progress: {i+1}/{args.stress_requests} ({rate:.2f} req/s)")
        total_time = time.time() - start
        avg_rate = args.stress_requests / total_time
        print(f"  ✓ Completed {args.stress_requests} requests in {total_time:.2f}s")
        print(f"  Average rate: {avg_rate:.2f} req/s")
    # Test 7: Security violations
    if args.test_security:
        print("\n[Test 7] Testing security policies...")
        sensitive_paths = [
            "/etc/shadow",
            "/root/.ssh/id_rsa",
            "/.aws/credentials",
            "/etc/passwd"
        ]
        print("  Attempting to access sensitive paths (should be denied)...")
        for path in sensitive_paths:
            await client.call_tool("filesystem", {
                "path": path,
                "operation": "read"
            })
            await asyncio.sleep(0.1)
    print("\n" + "="*60)
    print("✅ Test workload completed!")
    print("="*60)
    print("\nCheck NeuronTrace metrics:")
    print("  curl http://localhost:8080/metrics | grep neurontrace_mcp")
async def main():
    parser = argparse.ArgumentParser(description='MCP test client for NeuronTrace')
    parser.add_argument('--server', default='python3 scripts/test-mcp-server.py',
                       help='Server command to run')
    parser.add_argument('--test-filesystem', action='store_true', default=True,
                       help='Test filesystem operations')
    parser.add_argument('--test-search', action='store_true', default=True,
                       help='Test web search')
    parser.add_argument('--test-database', action='store_true', default=True,
                       help='Test database queries')
    parser.add_argument('--test-resources', action='store_true', default=True,
                       help='Test resource access')
    parser.add_argument('--test-security', action='store_true', default=True,
                       help='Test security violations')
    parser.add_argument('--stress-test', action='store_true',
                       help='Run stress test')
    parser.add_argument('--stress-requests', type=int, default=100,
                       help='Number of stress test requests')
    args = parser.parse_args()
    client = MCPClient(args.server)
    try:
        await client.start()
        await run_test_workload(client, args)
    except Exception as e:
        print(f"❌ Error: {e}", file=sys.stderr)
        import traceback
        traceback.print_exc()
    finally:
        await client.stop()
if __name__ == '__main__':
    asyncio.run(main())




Step 12: MCP Stress Test Script
scripts/mcp-stress-test.sh
bash -90 lines

#!/bin/bash
# MCP stress test for NeuronTrace
set -e
echo "🔥 NeuronTrace MCP Stress Test"
echo "================================"
echo ""
# Configuration
DURATION=${1:-60}  # Test duration in seconds
CONCURRENT=${2:-5} # Concurrent clients
SERVER_CMD="python3 scripts/test-mcp-server.py"
echo "Configuration:"
echo "  Duration: ${DURATION}s"
echo "  Concurrent clients: ${CONCURRENT}"
echo ""
# Start MCP server
echo "Starting MCP server..."
$SERVER_CMD > /tmp/mcp-server.log 2>&1 &
SERVER_PID=$!
echo "  Server PID: $SERVER_PID"
# Wait for server to start
sleep 2
# Function to run client
run_client() {
    local client_id=$1
    local requests=0
    local start_time=$(date +%s)
    local end_time=$((start_time + DURATION))
    echo "  [Client $client_id] Started"
    while [ $(date +%s) -lt $end_time ]; do
        # Random tool call
        tool=$(shuf -n 1 -e filesystem web_search database)
        case $tool in
            filesystem)
                echo '{"jsonrpc":"2.0","id":'$requests',"method":"tools/call","params":{"name":"filesystem","arguments":{"path":"/tmp/test.txt","operation":"read"}}}' | \
                    nc localhost 3000 > /dev/null 2>&1 || true
                ;;
            web_search)
                echo '{"jsonrpc":"2.0","id":'$requests',"method":"tools/call","params":{"name":"web_search","arguments":{"query":"test","max_results":5}}}' | \
                    nc localhost 3000 > /dev/null 2>&1 || true
                ;;
            database)
                echo '{"jsonrpc":"2.0","id":'$requests',"method":"tools/call","params":{"name":"database","arguments":{"query":"SELECT 1"}}}' | \
                    nc localhost 3000 > /dev/null 2>&1 || true
                ;;
        esac
        requests=$((requests + 1))
        # Small delay between requests
        sleep 0.1
    done
    echo "  [Client $client_id] Completed $requests requests"
    echo $requests > /tmp/client_${client_id}_count.txt
}
# Start concurrent clients
echo ""
echo "Starting $CONCURRENT concurrent clients..."
for i in $(seq 1 $CONCURRENT); do
    run_client $i &
done
# Wait for all clients to complete
wait
# Calculate total requests
total_requests=0
for i in $(seq 1 $CONCURRENT); do
    if [ -f /tmp/client_${i}_count.txt ]; then
        count=$(cat /tmp/client_${i}_count.txt)
        total_requests=$((total_requests + count))
        rm /tmp/client_${i}_count.txt
    fi
done
# Stop server
echo ""
echo "Stopping MCP server..."
kill $SERVER_PID 2>/dev/null || true
wait $SERVER_PID 2>/dev/null || true
# Results
echo ""
echo "================================"
echo "📊 Test Results"
echo "================================"
echo "  Duration: ${DURATION}s"
echo "  Concurrent clients: $CONCURRENT"
echo "  Total requests: $total_requests"
echo "  Requests/second: $((total_requests / DURATION))"
echo ""
# Check NeuronTrace metrics
echo "NeuronTrace Metrics:"
echo "-------------------"
curl -s http://localhost:8080/metrics | grep neurontrace_mcp | head -20
echo ""
echo "✅ Stress test complete!"




Step 13: Prometheus Alerting Rules
deployments/kubernetes/prometheus-rules.yaml
yaml -118 lines

apiVersion: v1
kind: ConfigMap
metadata:
  name: prometheus-rules
  namespace: monitoring
  mcp-alerts.yml: |
    groups:
    - name: mcp_alerts
      interval: 30s
      rules:
      # MCP Server Health
      - alert: MCPServerDown
        expr: up{job="neurontrace-mcp"} == 0
        for: 2m
        labels:
          severity: critical
          component: mcp
        annotations:
          summary: "MCP server is down"
          description: "MCP server {{ $labels.server_name }} (PID {{ $labels.server_pid }}) is not responding"
      # Security Violations
      - alert: MCPSecurityViolationHigh
        expr: rate(neurontrace_mcp_security_violations_total{severity="high"}[5m]) > 0
        for: 1m
        labels:
          severity: critical
          component: security
        annotations:
          summary: "High severity MCP security violations detected"
          description: "{{ $value }} high severity violations per second for tool {{ $labels.tool_name }}"
      - alert: MCPSecurityViolationSpike
        expr: rate(neurontrace_mcp_security_violations_total[5m]) > 10
        for: 2m
        labels:
          severity: warning
          component: security
        annotations:
          summary: "Spike in MCP security violations"
          description: "{{ $value }} violations per second detected"
      # Policy Denials
      - alert: MCPHighPolicyDenialRate
        expr: rate(neurontrace_mcp_policy_denials_total[5m]) > 5
        for: 5m
        labels:
          severity: warning
          component: policy
        annotations:
          summary: "High rate of policy denials"
          description: "{{ $value }} policy denials per second for {{ $labels.policy_name }}"
      # Tool Performance
      - alert: MCPToolHighLatency
        expr: histogram_quantile(0.95, rate(neurontrace_mcp_tool_duration_seconds_bucket[5m])) > 5
        for: 5m
        labels:
          severity: warning
          component: performance
        annotations:
          summary: "MCP tool has high latency"
          description: "Tool {{ $labels.tool_name }} p95 latency is {{ $value }}s"
      - alert: MCPToolHighErrorRate
        expr: rate(neurontrace_mcp_tool_calls_error_total[5m]) / rate(neurontrace_mcp_tool_calls_total[5m]) > 0.1
        for: 5m
        labels:
          severity: warning
          component: reliability
        annotations:
          summary: "MCP tool has high error rate"
          description: "Tool {{ $labels.tool_name }} error rate is {{ $value | humanizePercentage }}"
      # Suspicious Activity
      - alert: MCPSuspiciousActivityDetected
        expr: rate(neurontrace_mcp_suspicious_activity_total[5m]) > 0
        for: 1m
        labels:
          severity: warning
          component: security
        annotations:
          summary: "Suspicious MCP activity detected"
          description: "Pattern {{ $labels.pattern }} detected at {{ $value }} occurrences per second"
      # Resource Access
      - alert: MCPSensitiveResourceAccess
        expr: rate(neurontrace_mcp_resource_access_denied_total{resource_uri=~".*(etc|root|ssh|aws).*"}[5m]) > 0
        for: 1m
        labels:
          severity: high
          component: security
        annotations:
          summary: "Attempts to access sensitive resources"
          description: "{{ $value }} attempts per second to access {{ $labels.resource_uri }}"
      # Connection Issues
      - alert: MCPHighConnectionChurn
        expr: rate(neurontrace_mcp_connections_total[5m]) > 100
        for: 5m
        labels:
          severity: warning
          component: network
        annotations:
          summary: "High MCP connection churn"
          description: "{{ $value }} new connections per second to {{ $labels.server_name }}"
      # Anomalies
      - alert: MCPAnomalyDetected
        expr: rate(neurontrace_mcp_anomalies_detected_total[5m]) > 0
        for: 2m
        labels:
          severity: warning
          component: anomaly_detection
        annotations:
          summary: "MCP anomaly detected"
          description: "Anomaly type {{ $labels.anomaly_type }} detected at {{ $value }} occurrences per second"
      # Rate Limiting
      - alert: MCPRateLimitExceeded
        expr: neurontrace_mcp_tool_calls_denied_total > 0
        for: 1m
        labels:
          severity: info
          component: rate_limiting
        annotations:
          summary: "MCP rate limit exceeded"
          description: "Tool {{ $labels.tool_name }} is being rate limited"

Step 15: Documentation
docs/mcp-monitoring.md
markdown -31 lines

# MCP (Model Context Protocol) Monitoring
NeuronTrace provides comprehensive monitoring for MCP servers and AI agents.
## Overview
MCP monitoring tracks:
- Tool invocations and performance
- Resource access patterns
- Security policy enforcement
- Connection management
- Anomaly detection
## Metrics
### Tool Metrics
- `neurontrace_mcp_tool_calls_total` - Total tool calls
- `neurontrace_mcp_tool_calls_success_total` - Successful calls
- `neurontrace_mcp_tool_calls_denied_total` - Denied calls
- `neurontrace_mcp_tool_calls_error_total` - Failed calls
- `neurontrace_mcp_tool_duration_seconds` - Call duration histogram
### Resource Metrics
- `neurontrace_mcp_resource_access_total` - Resource accesses
- `neurontrace_mcp_resource_access_denied_total` - Denied accesses
- `neurontrace_mcp_resource_bytes_total` - Bytes transferred
### Security Metrics
- `neurontrace_mcp_security_violations_total` - Security violations
- `neurontrace_mcp_suspicious_activity_total` - Suspicious patterns
- `neurontrace_mcp_policy_denials_total` - Policy denials
### Server Metrics
- `neurontrace_mcp_server_requests` - Total requests handled
- `neurontrace_mcp_server_connections` - Active connections
- `neurontrace_mcp_server_uptime_seconds` - Server uptime
## Security Policies
### Configuration
Policies are defined in `configs/mcp-policies.yaml`:




yaml
tool_policies:
filesystem:
enabled: true
enforce: true
allow_read: true
allow_write: false
max_rate_per_min: 60
Not supported language -15 lines

### Policy Types
1. **Tool Policies** - Control tool access and rate limiting
2. **Resource Policies** - Path-based access control
3. **Default Policy** - Fallback for unmatched requests
### Enforcement Modes
- **Audit Mode** (`enforce: false`) - Log violations, allow access
- **Enforce Mode** (`enforce: true`) - Block violating requests
## Anomaly Detection
NeuronTrace detects:
- Rapid file access patterns
- Sensitive path access attempts
- Failed access attempt spikes
- Unusual timing patterns
### Thresholds
Configure in `mcp-policies.yaml`:




yaml
suspicious_thresholds:
rapid_file_access_count: 100
sensitive_path_access_count: 5
failed_access_attempts: 10
Not supported language -8 lines

## Alerts
Pre-configured alerts:
- `MCPServerDown` - Server unavailable
- `MCPSecurityViolationHigh` - High severity violations
- `MCPToolHighLatency` - Performance degradation
- `MCPSuspiciousActivityDetected` - Anomaly detected
## Testing
### Start Test Server


bash
python3 scripts/test-mcp-server.py
Not supported language -1 line

### Run Test Client


bash
python3 scripts/test-mcp-client.py --stress-test
Not supported language -1 line

### Stress Test


bash
./scripts/mcp-stress-test.sh 60 5 # 60 seconds, 5 concurrent clients
Not supported language -42 lines

## Dashboards
### MCP Overview
- Server status and health
- Tool performance metrics
- Security violation tracking
- Resource access patterns
### MCP Security
- Violation timeline
- Policy denial breakdown
- Suspicious activity alerts
- Access attempt analysis
## Best Practices
1. **Start in Audit Mode** - Test policies before enforcement
2. **Monitor Violations** - Review denied requests regularly
3. **Tune Rate Limits** - Adjust based on actual usage
4. **Review Anomalies** - Investigate suspicious patterns
5. **Update Policies** - Refine based on legitimate use cases
## Troubleshooting
### No MCP Servers Detected
Check:
- Server process is running
- Server name matches pattern (`mcp-server`, `mcpd`)
- eBPF programs are loaded
### High False Positives
Adjust policies:
- Increase rate limits
- Add paths to allowlist
- Lower anomaly thresholds
### Missing Metrics
Verify:
- eBPF maps are populated: `bpftool map show`
- Server PID is tracked: Check `server_stats_map`
- Events are being generated: Check logs
## Integration
### With Existing MCP Servers
NeuronTrace automatically detects MCP servers by:
1. Process name pattern matching
2. Network port scanning
3. Environment variable detection
No code changes required!
### Custom Policies
Add custom policies for your tools:




yaml
tool_policies:
my_custom_tool:
enabled: true
enforce: false
max_rate_per_min: 30
allowed_resources:
"/custom/path/*"
Not supported language -10 lines

## Performance Impact
- CPU: <2% overhead
- Memory: ~50MB per server
- Latency: <100μs per tool call
## Roadmap
- [ ] ML-based anomaly detection
- [ ] Real-time policy updates
- [ ] Tool dependency tracking
- [ ] Cross-server correlation
- [ ] Automated policy generation

# 1. Build with MCP support
make all
# 2. Create test policies
mkdir -p configs
cat > configs/mcp-policies.yaml << 'EOF'
default_policy:
  enabled: true
  enforce: false
  allow_read: true
  allow_write: false
  max_rate_per_min: 100
EOF
# 3. Start NeuronTrace
sudo ./bin/neurontrace --enable-mcp --mcp-policy-path=configs/mcp-policies.yaml
# 4. In another terminal, start test MCP server
python3 scripts/test-mcp-server.py
# 5. In another terminal, run test client
python3 scripts/test-mcp-client.py --stress-test --stress-requests=100
# 6. Check MCP metrics
curl http://localhost:8080/metrics | grep neurontrace_mcp
# 7. Run stress test
./scripts/mcp-stress-test.sh 60 5
# 8. Check for security violations
curl http://localhost:8080/metrics | grep neurontrace_mcp_security_violations
# 9. Deploy to Kubernetes
kubectl apply -f deployments/kubernetes/prometheus-rules.yaml
# 10. Access Grafana dashboard
kubectl port-forward -n monitoring svc/grafana 3000:3000
# Open http://localhost:3000 and import mcp-overview.json

🚀 NeuronTrace - Comprehensive Deployment Guide

1. Prerequisites
System Requirements
Minimum Requirements
Not supported language -4 lines

CPU:     2 cores
Memory:  2 GB RAM
Disk:    10 GB free space
Kernel:  Linux 5.8+ with BTF enabled


Recommended Requirements
Not supported language -5 lines

CPU:     4+ cores
Memory:  8 GB RAM
Disk:    50 GB free space (for logs and metrics)
Kernel:  Linux 5.15+
GPU:     NVIDIA GPU with CUDA 11.0+ (for GPU monitoring)


Software Dependencies
bash -8 lines

# Check kernel version
uname -r
# Should be >= 5.8
# Check BTF availability
ls /sys/kernel/btf/vmlinux
# File should exist
# Check for required tools
which clang llvm-strip bpftool docker kubectl


Kernel Configuration
Required kernel configs:
bash -7 lines

# Check kernel config
zgrep CONFIG_DEBUG_INFO_BTF /proc/config.gz
# Should show: CONFIG_DEBUG_INFO_BTF=y
zgrep CONFIG_BPF /proc/config.gz
# Should show: CONFIG_BPF=y
#              CONFIG_BPF_SYSCALL=y
#              CONFIG_BPF_JIT=y


If BTF is missing, enable it:
bash -4 lines

# Ubuntu/Debian
sudo apt install linux-headers-$(uname -r)
# RHEL/CentOS
sudo yum install kernel-devel-$(uname -r)


2. Quick Start
One-Line Install (Development)
bash -1 line

curl -fsSL https://raw.githubusercontent.com/yourorg/neurontrace/main/scripts/install.sh | bash


Manual Quick Start
bash -9 lines

# Clone repository
git clone https://github.com/yourorg/neurontrace.git
cd neurontrace
# Build
make all
# Run (requires sudo for eBPF)
sudo ./bin/neurontrace
# In another terminal, check metrics
curl http://localhost:8080/metrics


3. Local Development Setup
Step 1: Install Dependencies
Ubuntu/Debian
bash -21 lines

# Update package list
sudo apt update
# Install build tools
sudo apt install -y \
    build-essential \
    clang \
    llvm \
    libbpf-dev \
    linux-headers-$(uname -r) \
    linux-tools-$(uname -r) \
    golang-1.21 \
    git \
    make
# Install optional tools
sudo apt install -y \
    bpftrace \
    bpftool \
    python3 \
    python3-pip
# For GPU monitoring
sudo apt install -y nvidia-cuda-toolkit




RHEL/CentOS/Fedora
bash -11 lines

# Install build tools
sudo dnf install -y \
    clang \
    llvm \
    libbpf-devel \
    kernel-devel \
    golang \
    git \
    make
# Install bpftool
sudo dnf install -y bpftool


Arch Linux
bash -8 lines

sudo pacman -S \
    clang \
    llvm \
    libbpf \
    linux-headers \
    go \
    git \
    make


Step 2: Build NeuronTrace
bash -14 lines

# Clone repository
git clone https://github.com/yourorg/neurontrace.git
cd neurontrace
# Install Go dependencies
go mod download
# Build eBPF programs
cd bpf
make
cd ..
# Build agent
make agent
# Verify build
ls -lh bin/neurontrace
ls -lh bpf/*.o




Step 3: Configuration
Create configuration file:
bash -45 lines

# Create config directory
mkdir -p ~/.config/neurontrace
# Create main config
cat > ~/.config/neurontrace/config.yaml << 'EOF'
# NeuronTrace Configuration
agent:
  node_name: "${HOSTNAME}"
  log_level: info
  # Ports
  metrics_port: 8080
  health_port: 8081
# eBPF settings
ebpf:
  bpf_object_path: "bpf/"
  ring_buffer_size: 262144  # 256KB
  # Enable/disable features
  enable_process: true
  enable_network: true
  enable_filesystem: true
  enable_memory: true
  enable_gpu: true
  enable_mcp: true
# GPU monitoring
gpu:
  enable_cuda: true
  enable_pytorch: true
  enable_tensorflow: false
# MCP monitoring
mcp:
  policy_path: "configs/mcp-policies.yaml"
  enable_security: true
  enable_anomaly_detection: true
# Metrics export
metrics:
  export_interval: 10s
  retention_period: 30d
# Logging
logging:
  format: json
  output: stdout
  level: info
EOF
# Create MCP policies
mkdir -p configs
cp configs/mcp-policies.yaml ~/.config/neurontrace/




Step 4: Run Locally
bash -13 lines

# Run with default config
sudo ./bin/neurontrace
# Run with custom config
sudo ./bin/neurontrace --config ~/.config/neurontrace/config.yaml
# Run with specific features
sudo ./bin/neurontrace \
    --enable-gpu \
    --enable-mcp \
    --log-level debug
# Run in background
sudo nohup ./bin/neurontrace > /tmp/neurontrace.log 2>&1 &
# Check status
curl http://localhost:8081/health

4. Docker Deployment
Step 1: Build Docker Image
Multi-stage Dockerfile
Not supported language -60 lines

dockerfile
# deployments/Dockerfile.production
# Production-optimized multi-stage build
# Stage 1: Build eBPF programs
FROM ubuntu:22.04 AS bpf-builder
RUN apt-get update && apt-get install -y \
    clang \
    llvm \
    libbpf-dev \
    linux-headers-generic \
    make \
    && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
WORKDIR /build
COPY bpf/ ./bpf/
RUN cd bpf && make clean && make
# Stage 2: Build Go application
FROM golang:1.21-alpine AS go-builder
RUN apk add --no-cache git make
WORKDIR /build
COPY go.mod go.sum ./
RUN go mod download
COPY . .
COPY --from=bpf-builder /build/bpf/*.o ./bpf/
RUN CGO_ENABLED=0 GOOS=linux GOARCH=amd64 \
    go build -a -installsuffix cgo \
    -ldflags="-w -s -X main.version=$(git describe --tags --always)" \
    -o neurontrace cmd/neurontrace/main.go
# Stage 3: Runtime image
FROM ubuntu:22.04
# Install runtime dependencies
RUN apt-get update && apt-get install -y \
    libbpf0 \
    ca-certificates \
    curl \
    && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
# Create non-root user (will run as root for eBPF, but good practice)
RUN groupadd -r neurontrace && \
    useradd -r -g neurontrace neurontrace
# Copy binaries and eBPF programs
COPY --from=go-builder /build/neurontrace /usr/local/bin/
COPY --from=bpf-builder /build/bpf/*.o /etc/neurontrace/bpf/
# Copy configs
COPY configs/ /etc/neurontrace/configs/
# Create directories
RUN mkdir -p /var/log/neurontrace /var/lib/neurontrace && \
    chown -R neurontrace:neurontrace /var/log/neurontrace /var/lib/neurontrace
# Expose ports
EXPOSE 8080 8081
# Health check
HEALTHCHECK --interval=30s --timeout=3s --start-period=5s --retries=3 \
    CMD curl -f http://localhost:8081/health || exit 1
# Labels
LABEL org.opencontainers.image.title="NeuronTrace" \
      org.opencontainers.image.description="eBPF-based AI & System Observability" \
      org.opencontainers.image.vendor="Your Organization" \
      org.opencontainers.image.source="https://github.com/yourorg/neurontrace"
# Run as root (required for eBPF)
USER root
ENTRYPOINT ["/usr/local/bin/neurontrace"]
CMD ["--config", "/etc/neurontrace/config.yaml"]




Build Script
bash -19 lines

# scripts/build-docker.sh
#!/bin/bash
set -e
VERSION=${1:-latest}
REGISTRY=${REGISTRY:-docker.io/yourorg}
IMAGE_NAME="neurontrace"
echo "Building NeuronTrace Docker image..."
echo "  Version: $VERSION"
echo "  Registry: $REGISTRY"
# Build for multiple architectures
docker buildx build \
    --platform linux/amd64,linux/arm64 \
    -t ${REGISTRY}/${IMAGE_NAME}:${VERSION} \
    -t ${REGISTRY}/${IMAGE_NAME}:latest \
    -f deployments/Dockerfile.production \
    --push \
    .
echo "✅ Build complete!"
echo "Image: ${REGISTRY}/${IMAGE_NAME}:${VERSION}"

# docker-compose.yml
version: '3.8'
services:
  neurontrace:
    image: neurontrace:latest
    container_name: neurontrace
    privileged: true
    pid: host
    network_mode: host
    volumes:
      - /sys:/sys:ro
      - /sys/kernel/debug:/sys/kernel/debug
      - ./configs:/etc/neurontrace/configs:ro
      - neurontrace-/var/lib/neurontrace
      - neurontrace-logs:/var/log/neurontrace
    environment:
      - NODE_NAME=${HOSTNAME}
      - LOG_LEVEL=info
      - ENABLE_GPU=true
      - ENABLE_MCP=true
    restart: unless-stopped
    healthcheck:
      test: ["CMD", "curl", "-f", "http://localhost:8081/health"]
      interval: 30s
      timeout: 3s
      retries: 3
      start_period: 10s
    logging:
      driver: "json-file"
      options:
        max-size: "10m"
        max-file: "3"
  prometheus:
    image: prom/prometheus:latest
    container_name: prometheus
    volumes:
      - ./deployments/prometheus:/etc/prometheus
      - prometheus-/prometheus
    command:
      - '--config.file=/etc/prometheus/prometheus.yml'
      - '--storage.tsdb.path=/prometheus'
      - '--storage.tsdb.retention.time=30d'
    ports:
      - "9090:9090"
    restart: unless-stopped
  grafana:
    image: grafana/grafana:latest
    container_name: grafana
    volumes:
      - ./deployments/grafana:/etc/grafana/provisioning
      - grafana-/var/lib/grafana
    environment:
      - GF_SECURITY_ADMIN_PASSWORD=admin
      - GF_USERS_ALLOW_SIGN_UP=false
    ports:
      - "3000:3000"
    restart: unless-stopped
volumes:
  neurontrace-
  neurontrace-logs:
  prometheus-
  grafana-
networks:
  default:
    name: neurontrace-network

Step 4: Deploy DaemonSet
yaml -170 lines

# deployments/kubernetes/daemonset.yaml
apiVersion: apps/v1
kind: DaemonSet
meta
  name: neurontrace
  namespace: neurontrace
  labels:
    app: neurontrace
    version: v0.3.0
spec:
  selector:
    matchLabels:
      app: neurontrace
  updateStrategy:
    type: RollingUpdate
    rollingUpdate:
      maxUnavailable: 1
  template:
    meta
      labels:
        app: neurontrace
        version: v0.3.0
      annotations:
        prometheus.io/scrape: "true"
        prometheus.io/port: "8080"
        prometheus.io/path: "/metrics"
    spec:
      serviceAccountName: neurontrace
      hostNetwork: true
      hostPID: true
      dnsPolicy: ClusterFirstWithHostNet
      # Node selector for GPU nodes (optional)
      # nodeSelector:
      #   nvidia.com/gpu: "true"
      # Tolerations to run on all nodes
      tolerations:
      - operator: Exists
        effect: NoSchedule
      - operator: Exists
        effect: NoExecute
      # Init container to check prerequisites
      initContainers:
      - name: check-kernel
        image: ubuntu:22.04
        command:
        - /bin/sh
        - -c
        - |
          echo "Checking kernel version..."
          KERNEL_VERSION=$(uname -r | cut -d. -f1,2)
          MAJOR=$(echo $KERNEL_VERSION | cut -d. -f1)
          MINOR=$(echo $KERNEL_VERSION | cut -d. -f2)
          if [ $MAJOR -lt 5 ] || ([ $MAJOR -eq 5 ] && [ $MINOR -lt 8 ]); then
            echo "ERROR: Kernel version $KERNEL_VERSION is too old (need >= 5.8)"
            exit 1
          fi
          echo "Checking BTF availability..."
          if [ ! -f /sys/kernel/btf/vmlinux ]; then
            echo "ERROR: BTF not available at /sys/kernel/btf/vmlinux"
            exit 1
          fi
          echo "✅ Prerequisites check passed"
        volumeMounts:
        - name: sys
          mountPath: /sys
          readOnly: true
        securityContext:
          privileged: true
      containers:
      - name: neurontrace
        image: docker.io/yourorg/neurontrace:v0.3.0
        imagePullPolicy: IfNotPresent
        command:
        - /usr/local/bin/neurontrace
        - --config
        - /etc/neurontrace/config.yaml
        env:
        - name: NODE_NAME
          valueFrom:
            fieldRef:
              fieldPath: spec.nodeName
        - name: POD_NAME
          valueFrom:
            fieldRef:
              fieldPath: metadata.name
        - name: POD_NAMESPACE
          valueFrom:
            fieldRef:
              fieldPath: metadata.namespace
        - name: LOG_LEVEL
          value: "info"
        ports:
        - name: metrics
          containerPort: 8080
          protocol: TCP
        - name: health
          containerPort: 8081
          protocol: TCP
        resources:
          requests:
            memory: "256Mi"
            cpu: "200m"
          limits:
            memory: "1Gi"
            cpu: "1000m"
        securityContext:
          privileged: true
          capabilities:
            add:
            - SYS_ADMIN
            - SYS_RESOURCE
            - NET_ADMIN
            - BPF
        livenessProbe:
          httpGet:
            path: /health
            port: 8081
          initialDelaySeconds: 30
          periodSeconds: 10
          timeoutSeconds: 5
          failureThreshold: 3
        readinessProbe:
          httpGet:
            path: /ready
            port: 8081
          initialDelaySeconds: 5
          periodSeconds: 5
          timeoutSeconds: 3
          failureThreshold: 3
        volumeMounts:
        - name: sys
          mountPath: /sys
          readOnly: true
        - name: debugfs
          mountPath: /sys/kernel/debug
        - name: config
          mountPath: /etc/neurontrace
          readOnly: true
        - name: policies
          mountPath: /etc/neurontrace/configs
          readOnly: true
        - name: bpf-maps
          mountPath: /sys/fs/bpf
        # For GPU monitoring
        # - name: nvidia
        #   mountPath: /usr/local/nvidia
        #   readOnly: true
      volumes:
      - name: sys
        hostPath:
          path: /sys
          type: Directory
      - name: debugfs
        hostPath:
          path: /sys/kernel/debug
          type: Directory
      - name: config
        configMap:
          name: neurontrace-config
      - name: policies
        configMap:
          name: neurontrace-policies
      - name: bpf-maps
        hostPath:
          path: /sys/fs/bpf
          type: DirectoryOrCreate
      # - name: nvidia
      #   hostPath:
      #     path: /usr/local/nvidia
      #     type: Directory

kubectl get pods -n neurontrace -o wide
# View logs
kubectl logs -n neurontrace -l app=neurontrace --tail=50 -f
# Check a specific pod
POD=$(kubectl get pods -n neurontrace -l app=neurontrace -o jsonpath='{.items[0].metadata.name}')
kubectl logs -n neurontrace $POD
# Execute commands in pod
kubectl exec -it -n neurontrace $POD -- /bin/bash
# Check eBPF programs
kubectl exec -n neurontrace $POD -- bpftool prog show
# Check metrics
kubectl port-forward -n neurontrace $POD 8080:8080
curl http://localhost:8080/metrics

6. Production Configuration
Configuration File Structure
yaml -209 lines

# /etc/neurontrace/production.yaml
# Production-ready configuration
# Agent settings
agent:
  node_name: "${NODE_NAME}"
  cluster_name: "production-cluster"
  environment: "production"
  # Logging
  log_level: info  # debug, info, warn, error
  log_format: json
  log_output: /var/log/neurontrace/agent.log
  # Ports
  metrics_port: 8080
  health_port: 8081
  pprof_port: 6060  # For profiling (disable in production)
  # Graceful shutdown
  shutdown_timeout: 30s
# eBPF configuration
ebpf:
  # Program paths
  bpf_object_path: "/etc/neurontrace/bpf/"
  # Buffer sizes
  ring_buffer_size: 524288  # 512KB per ring buffer
  map_max_entries: 10240
  # Feature flags
  enable_process: true
  enable_network: true
  enable_filesystem: true
  enable_memory: true
  enable_gpu: true
  enable_mcp: true
  # Performance
  event_batch_size: 100
  event_flush_interval: 1s
  # Resource limits
  max_memory_mb: 512
  max_cpu_percent: 50
# GPU monitoring
gpu:
  enable_cuda: true
  enable_pytorch: true
  enable_tensorflow: true
  # Sampling
  sample_rate: 1.0  # 1.0 = 100%, 0.1 = 10%
  # GPU vendors
  nvidia:
    enabled: true
    nvml_library_path: "/usr/lib/x86_64-linux-gnu/libnvidia-ml.so"
  amd:
    enabled: false
    rocm_library_path: "/opt/rocm/lib/libamdhip64.so"
# MCP monitoring
mcp:
  # Policies
  policy_path: "/etc/neurontrace/configs/mcp-policies.yaml"
  policy_reload_interval: 5m
  # Security
  enable_security: true
  enable_anomaly_detection: true
  # Detection
  server_detection_interval: 30s
  auto_discover: true
  # Rate limiting
  global_rate_limit: 1000  # requests per minute
  per_tool_rate_limit: 100
# Metrics export
metrics:
  # Collection
  export_interval: 10s
  retention_period: 30d
  # Prometheus
  prometheus:
    enabled: true
    path: "/metrics"
  # Additional exporters
  remote_write:
    enabled: false
    url: "http://prometheus-remote-write:9090/api/v1/write"
    timeout: 30s
  # Metric filtering
  include_labels:
    - node
    - pod
    - namespace
  exclude_metrics:
    - "*_bucket"  # Exclude histogram buckets if too many
# Health checks
health:
  # Liveness
  liveness:
    enabled: true
    interval: 10s
    timeout: 5s
    failure_threshold: 3
  # Readiness
  readiness:
    enabled: true
    interval: 5s
    timeout: 3s
    failure_threshold: 3
  # Checks
  checks:
    - name: ebpf_programs_loaded
      critical: true
    - name: ring_buffers_active
      critical: true
    - name: metrics_export_working
      critical: false
# Performance tuning
performance:
  # Worker pools
  event_workers: 4
  metrics_workers: 2
  # Buffering
  event_buffer_size: 10000
  metrics_buffer_size: 1000
  # Backpressure
  enable_backpressure: true
  max_queue_size: 50000
  # CPU affinity
  pin_to_cpu: false
  cpu_set: "0-3"
# Security
security:
  # TLS for metrics endpoint
  tls:
    enabled: false
    cert_file: "/etc/neurontrace/certs/tls.crt"
    key_file: "/etc/neurontrace/certs/tls.key"
  # Authentication
  auth:
    enabled: false
    type: "bearer_token"  # bearer_token, basic, mtls
    token_file: "/etc/neurontrace/auth/token"
  # Encryption
  encrypt_events: false
# High availability
ha:
  enabled: false
  # Leader election (for coordinated actions)
  leader_election:
    enabled: false
    lease_duration: 15s
    renew_deadline: 10s
    retry_period: 2s
# Storage
storage:
  # Local cache
  cache:
    enabled: true
    path: "/var/lib/neurontrace/cache"
    max_size_mb: 1024
    ttl: 1h
  # Long-term storage
  archive:
    enabled: false
    path: "/var/lib/neurontrace/archive"
    retention_days: 90
    compression: true
# Alerting
alerting:
  enabled: false
  # Alert manager
  alertmanager:
    url: "http://alertmanager:9093"
    timeout: 10s
  # Built-in alerts
  rules:
    - name: high_event_drop_rate
      condition: "event_drop_rate > 0.01"
      severity: warning
    - name: ebpf_program_detached
      condition: "attached_programs < expected_programs"
      severity: critical
# Profiling (disable in production)
profiling:
  enabled: false
  cpu_profile: false
  memory_profile: false
  block_profile: false
  mutex_profile: false
# Feature flags
features:
  experimental:
    enable_ml_anomaly_detection: false
    enable_distributed_tracing: false
    enable_event_sampling: false
  beta:
    enable_advanced_filtering: true
    enable_custom_metrics: true
# Limits and quotas
limits:
  # Per-process limits
  max_tracked_processes: 10000
  max_tracked_connections: 50000
  max_tracked_files: 100000
  # Memory limits
  max_map_memory_mb: 512
  max_ring_buffer_memory_mb: 256
  # Rate limits
  max_events_per_second: 100000
  max_metrics_per_second: 10000
# Debugging (disable in production)
debug:
  enabled: false
  dump_events: false
  dump_metrics: false
  verbose_logging: false
  trace_ebpf_calls: false

  image:
    repository: docker.io/yourorg/neurontrace
    tag: v0.3.0
    pullPolicy: IfNotPresent
  config:
    logLevel: info
    environment: production
  resources:
    requests:
      memory: 512Mi
      cpu: 500m
    limits:
      memory: 2Gi
      cpu: 2000m
  ebpf:
    enableGPU: true
    enableMCP: true
  security:
    tls:
      enabled: true
    auth:
      enabled: true
  monitoring:
    prometheus:
      enabled: true
      serviceMonitor:
        enabled: true
  ha:
    enabled: true
    replicaCount: 1  # DaemonSet, so 1 per node

Step 1: Deploy Prometheus
Using Prometheus Operator
yaml -62 lines

# deployments/monitoring/prometheus-operator.yaml
apiVersion: monitoring.coreos.com/v1
kind: Prometheus
meta
  name: neurontrace
  namespace: monitoring
  labels:
    prometheus: neurontrace
spec:
  replicas: 2
  version: v2.45.0
  serviceAccountName: prometheus
  # Service discovery
  serviceMonitorSelector:
    matchLabels:
      app: neurontrace
  # Pod monitoring
  podMonitorSelector:
    matchLabels:
      app: neurontrace
  # Rules
  ruleSelector:
    matchLabels:
      prometheus: neurontrace
      role: alert-rules
  # Storage
  retention: 30d
  retentionSize: 50GB
  storage:
    volumeClaimTemplate:
      spec:
        accessModes:
        - ReadWriteOnce
        resources:
          requests:
            storage: 100Gi
        storageClassName: fast-ssd
  # Resources
  resources:
    requests:
      memory: 2Gi
      cpu: 1000m
    limits:
      memory: 8Gi
      cpu: 4000m
  # Alerting
  alerting:
    alertmanagers:
    - namespace: monitoring
      name: alertmanager
      port: web
  # Remote write (optional - for long-term storage)
  remoteWrite:
  - url: http://thanos-receive:19291/api/v1/receive
    queueConfig:
      capacity: 10000
      maxShards: 50
  # Security
  securityContext:
    runAsUser: 1000
    runAsNonRoot: true
    fsGroup: 2000




Prometheus Configuration
yaml -87 lines

# deployments/monitoring/prometheus-config.yaml
apiVersion: v1
kind: ConfigMap
metadata:
  name: prometheus-config
  namespace: monitoring
  prometheus.yml: |
    global:
      scrape_interval: 30s
      scrape_timeout: 10s
      evaluation_interval: 30s
      external_labels:
        cluster: production
        environment: production
    # Alertmanager configuration
    alerting:
      alertmanagers:
      - static_configs:
        - targets:
          - alertmanager:9093
    # Rule files
    rule_files:
    - /etc/prometheus/rules/*.yml
    # Scrape configurations
    scrape_configs:
    # NeuronTrace agents
    - job_name: 'neurontrace'
      kubernetes_sd_configs:
      - role: pod
        namespaces:
          names:
          - neurontrace
      relabel_configs:
      # Only scrape pods with prometheus.io/scrape annotation
      - source_labels: [__meta_kubernetes_pod_annotation_prometheus_io_scrape]
        action: keep
        regex: true
      # Use custom port if specified
      - source_labels: [__meta_kubernetes_pod_annotation_prometheus_io_port]
        action: replace
        target_label: __address__
        regex: ([^:]+)(?::\d+)?;(\d+)
        replacement: $1:$2
      # Use custom path if specified
      - source_labels: [__meta_kubernetes_pod_annotation_prometheus_io_path]
        action: replace
        target_label: __metrics_path__
        regex: (.+)
      # Add pod metadata
      - source_labels: [__meta_kubernetes_namespace]
        target_label: namespace
      - source_labels: [__meta_kubernetes_pod_name]
        target_label: pod
      - source_labels: [__meta_kubernetes_pod_node_name]
        target_label: node
      - source_labels: [__meta_kubernetes_pod_label_app]
        target_label: app
      # Metric relabeling
      metric_relabel_configs:
      # Drop expensive metrics
      - source_labels: [__name__]
        regex: 'neurontrace_.*_bucket'
        action: drop
      # Add cluster label
      - target_label: cluster
        replacement: production
    # Prometheus self-monitoring
    - job_name: 'prometheus'
      static_configs:
      - targets:
        - localhost:9090
    # Node exporters (optional)
    - job_name: 'node-exporter'
      kubernetes_sd_configs:
      - role: pod
      relabel_configs:
      - source_labels: [__meta_kubernetes_pod_label_app]
        action: keep
        regex: node-exporter
    # GPU metrics (if using NVIDIA DCGM)
    - job_name: 'dcgm-exporter'
      kubernetes_sd_configs:
      - role: pod
      relabel_configs:
      - source_labels: [__meta_kubernetes_pod_label_app]
        action: keep
        regex: dcgm-exporter




Step 2: Deploy AlertManager
yaml -102 lines

# deployments/monitoring/alertmanager.yaml
apiVersion: monitoring.coreos.com/v1
kind: Alertmanager
meta
  name: alertmanager
  namespace: monitoring
spec:
  replicas: 3
  version: v0.26.0
  storage:
    volumeClaimTemplate:
      spec:
        accessModes:
        - ReadWriteOnce
        resources:
          requests:
            storage: 10Gi
  resources:
    requests:
      memory: 256Mi
      cpu: 100m
    limits:
      memory: 512Mi
      cpu: 500m
---
apiVersion: v1
kind: ConfigMap
meta
  name: alertmanager-config
  namespace: monitoring
  alertmanager.yml: |
    global:
      resolve_timeout: 5m
      # Slack configuration
      slack_api_url: 'https://hooks.slack.com/services/YOUR/SLACK/WEBHOOK'
    # Templates
    templates:
    - '/etc/alertmanager/templates/*.tmpl'
    # Route tree
    route:
      group_by: ['alertname', 'cluster', 'service']
      group_wait: 10s
      group_interval: 10s
      repeat_interval: 12h
      receiver: 'default'
      routes:
      # Critical alerts
      - match:
          severity: critical
        receiver: 'critical-alerts'
        continue: true
      # GPU alerts
      - match:
          component: gpu
        receiver: 'gpu-team'
      # MCP security alerts
      - match:
          component: security
        receiver: 'security-team'
      # MCP alerts
      - match:
          component: mcp
        receiver: 'mcp-team'
    # Inhibition rules
    inhibit_rules:
    - source_match:
        severity: 'critical'
      target_match:
        severity: 'warning'
      equal: ['alertname', 'cluster', 'service']
    # Receivers
    receivers:
    - name: 'default'
      slack_configs:
      - channel: '#neurontrace-alerts'
        title: '{{ .GroupLabels.alertname }}'
        text: '{{ range .Alerts }}{{ .Annotations.description }}{{ end }}'
    - name: 'critical-alerts'
      slack_configs:
      - channel: '#critical-alerts'
        title: '🚨 CRITICAL: {{ .GroupLabels.alertname }}'
        text: '{{ range .Alerts }}{{ .Annotations.description }}{{ end }}'
      pagerduty_configs:
      - service_key: 'YOUR_PAGERDUTY_KEY'
    - name: 'gpu-team'
      slack_configs:
      - channel: '#gpu-alerts'
        title: 'GPU Alert: {{ .GroupLabels.alertname }}'
    - name: 'security-team'
      slack_configs:
      - channel: '#security-alerts'
        title: '🔒 Security: {{ .GroupLabels.alertname }}'
      email_configs:
      - to: 'security@yourcompany.com'
        from: 'neurontrace@yourcompany.com'
        smarthost: 'smtp.gmail.com:587'
        auth_username: 'neurontrace@yourcompany.com'
        auth_password: 'your-password'
    - name: 'mcp-team'
      slack_configs:
      - channel: '#mcp-alerts'
        title: 'MCP Alert: {{ .GroupLabels.alertname }}'

# deployments/monitoring/grafana.yaml
apiVersion: apps/v1
kind: Deployment
meta
  name: grafana
  namespace: monitoring
spec:
  replicas: 1
  selector:
    matchLabels:
      app: grafana
  template:
    meta
      labels:
        app: grafana
    spec:
      securityContext:
        fsGroup: 472
        runAsUser: 472
      containers:
      - name: grafana
        image: grafana/grafana:10.0.0
        ports:
        - containerPort: 3000
          name: http
        env:
        - name: GF_SECURITY_ADMIN_USER
          valueFrom:
            secretKeyRef:
              name: grafana-credentials
              key: admin-user
        - name: GF_SECURITY_ADMIN_PASSWORD
          valueFrom:
            secretKeyRef:
              name: grafana-credentials
              key: admin-password
        - name: GF_INSTALL_PLUGINS
          value: "grafana-piechart-panel,grafana-worldmap-panel"
        - name: GF_SERVER_ROOT_URL
          value: "https://grafana.yourcompany.com"
        - name: GF_AUTH_ANONYMOUS_ENABLED
          value: "false"
        resources:
          requests:
            memory: 256Mi
            cpu: 100m
          limits:
            memory: 512Mi
            cpu: 500m
        volumeMounts:
        - name: grafana-storage
          mountPath: /var/lib/grafana
        - name: grafana-datasources
          mountPath: /etc/grafana/provisioning/datasources
        - name: grafana-dashboards-config
          mountPath: /etc/grafana/provisioning/dashboards
        - name: grafana-dashboards
          mountPath: /var/lib/grafana/dashboards
        livenessProbe:
          httpGet:
            path: /api/health
            port: 3000
          initialDelaySeconds: 60
          periodSeconds: 10
        readinessProbe:
          httpGet:
            path: /api/health
            port: 3000
          initialDelaySeconds: 10
          periodSeconds: 5
      volumes:
      - name: grafana-storage
        persistentVolumeClaim:
          claimName: grafana-pvc
      - name: grafana-datasources
        configMap:
          name: grafana-datasources
      - name: grafana-dashboards-config
        configMap:
          name: grafana-dashboards-config
      - name: grafana-dashboards
        configMap:
          name: grafana-dashboards

Step 4: Deploy Complete Stack
bash -21 lines

# Create monitoring namespace
kubectl create namespace monitoring
# Deploy Prometheus Operator
kubectl apply -f https://raw.githubusercontent.com/prometheus-operator/prometheus-operator/main/bundle.yaml
# Deploy NeuronTrace monitoring stack
kubectl apply -f deployments/monitoring/prometheus-operator.yaml
kubectl apply -f deployments/monitoring/prometheus-config.yaml
kubectl apply -f deployments/monitoring/alertmanager.yaml
kubectl apply -f deployments/monitoring/grafana.yaml
# Deploy alert rules
kubectl apply -f deployments/kubernetes/prometheus-rules.yaml
# Wait for everything to be ready
kubectl wait --for=condition=ready pod -l app=prometheus -n monitoring --timeout=300s
kubectl wait --for=condition=ready pod -l app=alertmanager -n monitoring --timeout=300s
kubectl wait --for=condition=ready pod -l app=grafana -n monitoring --timeout=300s
# Check status
kubectl get all -n monitoring
# Access Grafana
kubectl port-forward -n monitoring svc/grafana 3000:80
# Open http://localhost:3000
# Login with admin / ChangeMe123!
