Network Security
Network Policies
yaml -59 lines

# deployments/kubernetes/network-policy.yaml
apiVersion: networking.k8s.io/v1
kind: NetworkPolicy
meta
  name: neurontrace-network-policy
  namespace: neurontrace
spec:
  podSelector:
    matchLabels:
      app: neurontrace
  policyTypes:
  - Ingress
  - Egress
  # Ingress rules
  ingress:
  # Allow Prometheus scraping
  - from:
    - namespaceSelector:
        matchLabels:
          name: monitoring
      podSelector:
        matchLabels:
          app: prometheus
    ports:
    - protocol: TCP
      port: 8080
  # Allow health checks from kubelet
  - from:
    - namespaceSelector: {}
    ports:
    - protocol: TCP
      port: 8081
  # Egress rules
  egress:
  # Allow DNS
  - to:
    - namespaceSelector:
        matchLabels:
          name: kube-system
      podSelector:
        matchLabels:
          k8s-app: kube-dns
    ports:
    - protocol: UDP
      port: 53
  # Allow Prometheus remote write
  - to:
    - namespaceSelector:
        matchLabels:
          name: monitoring
    ports:
    - protocol: TCP
      port: 9090
  # Allow API server access
  - to:
    - namespaceSelector: {}
    ports:
    - protocol: TCP
      port: 443




Pod Security
Pod Security Policy
yaml -67 lines

# deployments/kubernetes/pod-security-policy.yaml
apiVersion: policy/v1beta1
kind: PodSecurityPolicy
meta
  name: neurontrace-psp
  annotations:
    seccomp.security.alpha.kubernetes.io/allowedProfileNames: 'runtime/default'
    apparmor.security.beta.kubernetes.io/allowedProfileNames: 'runtime/default'
spec:
  privileged: true  # Required for eBPF
  allowPrivilegeEscalation: true
  # Required capabilities for eBPF
  allowedCapabilities:
  - SYS_ADMIN
  - SYS_RESOURCE
  - NET_ADMIN
  - BPF
  # Host namespaces
  hostNetwork: true
  hostPID: true
  hostIPC: false
  # Volumes
  volumes:
  - 'configMap'
  - 'secret'
  - 'hostPath'
  - 'emptyDir'
  allowedHostPaths:
  - pathPrefix: "/sys"
    readOnly: true
  - pathPrefix: "/sys/kernel/debug"
    readOnly: false
  - pathPrefix: "/sys/fs/bpf"
    readOnly: false
  # Run as root (required for eBPF)
  runAsUser:
    rule: 'RunAsAny'
  seLinux:
    rule: 'RunAsAny'
  supplementalGroups:
    rule: 'RunAsAny'
  fsGroup:
    rule: 'RunAsAny'
---
apiVersion: rbac.authorization.k8s.io/v1
kind: ClusterRole
meta
  name: neurontrace-psp
rules:
- apiGroups: ['policy']
  resources: ['podsecuritypolicies']
  verbs: ['use']
  resourceNames:
  - neurontrace-psp
---
apiVersion: rbac.authorization.k8s.io/v1
kind: ClusterRoleBinding
meta
  name: neurontrace-psp
roleRef:
  kind: ClusterRole
  name: neurontrace-psp
  apiGroup: rbac.authorization.k8s.io
subjects:
- kind: ServiceAccount
  name: neurontrace
  namespace: neurontrace




Secrets Management
Using Sealed Secrets
bash -13 lines

# Install Sealed Secrets controller
kubectl apply -f https://github.com/bitnami-labs/sealed-secrets/releases/download/v0.24.0/controller.yaml
# Install kubeseal CLI
wget https://github.com/bitnami-labs/sealed-secrets/releases/download/v0.24.0/kubeseal-linux-amd64
sudo install -m 755 kubeseal-linux-amd64 /usr/local/bin/kubeseal
# Create secret
kubectl create secret generic neurontrace-secrets \
  --from-literal=auth-token='your-secret-token' \
  --dry-run=client -o yaml > secret.yaml
# Seal the secret
kubeseal -f secret.yaml -w sealed-secret.yaml
# Apply sealed secret
kubectl apply -f sealed-secret.yaml

# Read-only access to pods (for metadata)
- apiGroups: [""]
  resources: ["pods"]
  verbs: ["get", "list", "watch"]
# ConfigMap access (for dynamic configuration)
- apiGroups: [""]
  resources: ["configmaps"]
  verbs: ["get", "list", "watch"]
  resourceNames: ["neurontrace-config"]

        resources: ["configmaps"]

9. Performance Tuning
System-Level Optimizations
Kernel Parameters
bash -27 lines

# /etc/sysctl.d/99-neurontrace.conf
# Kernel tuning for eBPF and high-performance monitoring
# eBPF settings
kernel.unprivileged_bpf_disabled=1
kernel.bpf_stats_enabled=1
# Increase map memory limits
kernel.bpf.map_memory_limit=1073741824  # 1GB
# Network performance
net.core.rmem_max=134217728
net.core.wmem_max=134217728
net.core.rmem_default=16777216
net.core.wmem_default=16777216
net.ipv4.tcp_rmem=4096 87380 134217728
net.ipv4.tcp_wmem=4096 65536 134217728
# File descriptor limits
fs.file-max=2097152
fs.nr_open=2097152
# Inotify limits (for file monitoring)
fs.inotify.max_user_watches=524288
fs.inotify.max_user_instances=512
# Memory management
vm.swappiness=10
vm.dirty_ratio=15
vm.dirty_background_ratio=5
# CPU scheduling
kernel.sched_migration_cost_ns=5000000
kernel.sched_autogroup_enabled=0




Apply settings:
bash -5 lines

# Load settings
sudo sysctl -p /etc/sysctl.d/99-neurontrace.conf
# Verify
sysctl kernel.bpf_stats_enabled
sysctl fs.file-max

eBPF Optimizations
Map Sizing
yaml -18 lines

# Optimal map sizes based on workload
ebpf:
  maps:
    # Process tracking
    process_map:
      max_entries: 10240  # ~10K processes
    # Network connections
    connection_map:
      max_entries: 50000  # ~50K connections
    # File descriptors
    fd_map:
      max_entries: 100000  # ~100K file descriptors
    # GPU tracking
    gpu_map:
      max_entries: 1024  # Per-process GPU stats
    # MCP tools
    tool_stats_map:
      max_entries: 256  # Tool statistics




Ring Buffer Tuning
yaml -12 lines

# Ring buffer configuration
ebpf:
  ring_buffers:
    # Size per buffer (power of 2)
    process_events: 524288    # 512KB
    network_events: 1048576   # 1MB
    file_events: 524288       # 512KB
    gpu_events: 1048576       # 1MB (GPU events can be large)
    mcp_events: 524288        # 512KB
    # Polling configuration
    poll_timeout_ms: 100
    batch_size: 100




Program Optimization
c -42 lines

// Performance optimizations in eBPF code
// 1. Use __always_inline for hot paths
static __always_inline u64 get_timestamp(void)
{
    return bpf_ktime_get_ns();
}
// 2. Minimize map lookups
static __always_inline void update_stats_optimized(u32 pid)
{
    // Lookup once, update multiple fields
    struct stats *s = bpf_map_lookup_elem(&stats_map, &pid);
    if (s) {
        __sync_fetch_and_add(&s->count, 1);
        __sync_fetch_and_add(&s->bytes, size);
        s->last_update = bpf_ktime_get_ns();
    }
}
// 3. Use per-CPU maps for high-frequency counters
struct {
    __uint(type, BPF_MAP_TYPE_PERCPU_ARRAY);
    __uint(max_entries, 1);
    __type(key, u32);
    __type(value, u64);
} counters SEC(".maps");
// 4. Early filtering to reduce processing
SEC("kprobe/tcp_sendmsg")
int trace_tcp_send(struct pt_regs *ctx)
{
    // Filter early
    u32 pid = bpf_get_current_pid_tgid() >> 32;
    if (pid < 1000)  // Skip system processes
        return 0;
    // Only process if we're tracking this PID
    if (!bpf_map_lookup_elem(&tracked_pids, &pid))
        return 0;
    // Continue processing...
}
// 5. Use bounded loops
#pragma unroll
for (int i = 0; i < 8; i++) {
    // Loop body
}

Memory Management
go -65 lines

// pkg/agent/performance.go
package agent
import (
    "runtime"
    "runtime/debug"
    "time"
)
type PerformanceManager struct {
    gcInterval time.Duration
    memLimit   uint64
}
func NewPerformanceManager(memLimitMB uint64) *PerformanceManager {
    return &PerformanceManager{
        gcInterval: 5 * time.Minute,
        memLimit:   memLimitMB * 1024 * 1024,
    }
}
func (pm *PerformanceManager) Start() {
    // Set memory limit
    debug.SetMemoryLimit(int64(pm.memLimit))
    // Tune GC
    debug.SetGCPercent(50)  // More aggressive GC
    // Periodic GC and memory stats
    ticker := time.NewTicker(pm.gcInterval)
    go func() {
        for range ticker.C {
            pm.collectStats()
            pm.maybeForceGC()
        }
    }()
}
func (pm *PerformanceManager) collectStats() {
    var m runtime.MemStats
    runtime.ReadMemStats(&m)
    // Log memory stats
    log.Printf("Memory: Alloc=%dMB, TotalAlloc=%dMB, Sys=%dMB, NumGC=%d",
        m.Alloc/1024/1024,
        m.TotalAlloc/1024/1024,
        m.Sys/1024/1024,
        m.NumGC)
}
func (pm *PerformanceManager) maybeForceGC() {
    var m runtime.MemStats
    runtime.ReadMemStats(&m)
    // Force GC if using > 80% of limit
    if m.Alloc > uint64(float64(pm.memLimit)*0.8) {
        log.Println("Forcing GC due to high memory usage")
        runtime.GC()
        debug.FreeOSMemory()
    }
}
// Object pooling for frequently allocated objects
var eventPool = sync.Pool{
    New: func() interface{} {
        return &Event{}
    },
}
func getEvent() *Event {
    return eventPool.Get().(*Event)
}
func putEvent(e *Event) {
    // Reset event
    *e = Event{}
    eventPool.Put(e)
}

Metric Filtering
go -23 lines

// Filter metrics before export
type MetricFilter struct {
    allowlist []string
    denylist  []string
}
func (mf *MetricFilter) ShouldExport(metric string) bool {
    // Check denylist first
    for _, pattern := range mf.denylist {
        if matched, _ := filepath.Match(pattern, metric); matched {
            return false
        }
    }
    // Check allowlist
    if len(mf.allowlist) == 0 {
        return true
    }
    for _, pattern := range mf.allowlist {
        if matched, _ := filepath.Match(pattern, metric); matched {
            return true
        }
    }
    return false
}

Benchmarking
bash -84 lines

# scripts/benchmark.sh
#!/bin/bash
set -e
echo "🔥 NeuronTrace Performance Benchmark"
echo "===================================="
echo ""
# Configuration
DURATION=${1:-60}
WORKLOAD=${2:-mixed}
echo "Running benchmark for ${DURATION}s with ${WORKLOAD} workload..."
echo ""
# Start monitoring
kubectl port-forward -n neurontrace svc/neurontrace 8080:8080 &
PF_PID=$!
sleep 2
# Baseline metrics
echo "📊 Baseline Metrics:"
curl -s http://localhost:8080/metrics | grep -E "(events_processed|events_dropped|cpu_seconds)" | head -5
echo ""
# Start workload
case $WORKLOAD in
    process)
        echo "Starting process workload..."
        ./scripts/test-workload.sh process $DURATION &
        ;;
    network)
        echo "Starting network workload..."
        ./scripts/test-workload.sh network $DURATION &
        ;;
    gpu)
        echo "Starting GPU workload..."
        python3 scripts/test-pytorch.py --steps 1000 &
        ;;
    mcp)
        echo "Starting MCP workload..."
        python3 scripts/test-mcp-client.py --stress-test --stress-requests 1000 &
        ;;
    mixed)
        echo "Starting mixed workload..."
        ./scripts/test-workload.sh process $DURATION &
        ./scripts/test-workload.sh network $DURATION &
        python3 scripts/test-mcp-client.py --stress-test --stress-requests 500 &
        ;;
esac
WORKLOAD_PID=$!
# Monitor performance
START_TIME=$(date +%s)
END_TIME=$((START_TIME + DURATION))
while [ $(date +%s) -lt $END_TIME ]; do
    ELAPSED=$(($(date +%s) - START_TIME))
    # Get current metrics
    EVENTS_PROCESSED=$(curl -s http://localhost:8080/metrics | grep "neurontrace_events_processed_total" | grep -v "#" | awk '{print $2}')
    EVENTS_DROPPED=$(curl -s http://localhost:8080/metrics | grep "neurontrace_events_dropped_total" | grep -v "#" | awk '{print $2}')
    CPU_USAGE=$(curl -s http://localhost:8080/metrics | grep "process_cpu_seconds_total" | grep -v "#" | awk '{print $2}')
    MEM_USAGE=$(curl -s http://localhost:8080/metrics | grep "process_resident_memory_bytes" | grep -v "#" | awk '{print $2}')
    echo "[${ELAPSED}s] Events: ${EVENTS_PROCESSED}, Dropped: ${EVENTS_DROPPED}, CPU: ${CPU_USAGE}s, Mem: $((MEM_USAGE/1024/1024))MB"
    sleep 5
done
# Stop workload
kill $WORKLOAD_PID 2>/dev/null || true
wait $WORKLOAD_PID 2>/dev/null || true
# Final metrics
echo ""
echo "📊 Final Metrics:"
curl -s http://localhost:8080/metrics | grep -E "(events_processed|events_dropped|cpu_seconds)" | head -5
echo ""
# Calculate statistics
FINAL_EVENTS=$(curl -s http://localhost:8080/metrics | grep "neurontrace_events_processed_total" | grep -v "#" | awk '{print $2}')
FINAL_DROPPED=$(curl -s http://localhost:8080/metrics | grep "neurontrace_events_dropped_total" | grep -v "#" | awk '{print $2}')
EVENTS_PER_SEC=$((FINAL_EVENTS / DURATION))
DROP_RATE=$(echo "scale=4; $FINAL_DROPPED / $FINAL_EVENTS * 100" | bc)
echo "Results:"
echo "  Total events processed: $FINAL_EVENTS"
echo "  Events per second: $EVENTS_PER_SEC"
echo "  Events dropped: $FINAL_DROPPED"
echo "  Drop rate: ${DROP_RATE}%"
echo ""
# Cleanup
kill $PF_PID 2>/dev/null || true
if (( $(echo "$DROP_RATE > 1.0" | bc -l) )); then
    echo "⚠️  WARNING: Drop rate is high (${DROP_RATE}%). Consider tuning."
else
    echo "✅ Performance is within acceptable limits."
fi




10. Troubleshooting
Common Issues and Solutions
Issue 1: Agent Won't Start
bash -18 lines

# Check kernel version
uname -r
# Must be >= 5.8
# Check BTF availability
ls -l /sys/kernel/btf/vmlinux
# File must exist
# Check eBPF support
zgrep CONFIG_BPF /proc/config.gz
# Should show CONFIG_BPF=y
# Check permissions
sudo -v
# Agent needs root/CAP_BPF
# Check logs
kubectl logs -n neurontrace -l app=neurontrace --tail=100
# Common errors and fixes:
# "failed to load BPF programs" -> Check kernel version and BTF
# "permission denied" -> Run with sudo or add CAP_BPF
# "map creation failed" -> Increase map memory limits

# scripts/debug.sh
#!/bin/bash
set -e
NAMESPACE=${1:-neurontrace}
POD=${2:-}
if [ -z "$POD" ]; then
    POD=$(kubectl get pods -n $NAMESPACE -l app=neurontrace -o jsonpath='{.items[0].metadata.name}')
fi
echo "🔍 NeuronTrace Debug Information"
echo "================================"
echo "Namespace: $NAMESPACE"
echo "Pod: $POD"
echo ""
# Pod status
echo "📦 Pod Status:"
kubectl get pod -n $NAMESPACE $POD
echo ""
# Events
echo "📋 Recent Events:"
kubectl get events -n $NAMESPACE --field-selector involvedObject.name=$POD --sort-by='.lastTimestamp' | tail -10
echo ""
# Logs
echo "📝 Recent Logs:"
kubectl logs -n $NAMESPACE $POD --tail=20
echo ""
# eBPF programs
echo "🔧 eBPF Programs:"
kubectl exec -n $NAMESPACE $POD -- bpftool prog show | grep neurontrace || echo "No programs found"
echo ""
# eBPF maps
echo "🗺️  eBPF Maps:"
kubectl exec -n $NAMESPACE $POD -- bpftool map show | grep neurontrace || echo "No maps found"
echo ""
# Metrics sample
echo "📊 Metrics Sample:"
kubectl exec -n $NAMESPACE $POD -- curl -s http://localhost:8080/metrics | head -20
echo ""
# Health check
echo "💚 Health Check:"
kubectl exec -n $NAMESPACE $POD -- curl -s http://localhost:8081/health
echo ""
# Resource usage
echo "💻 Resource Usage:"
kubectl top pod -n $NAMESPACE $POD
echo ""
# Network connectivity
echo "🌐 Network Connectivity:"
kubectl exec -n $NAMESPACE $POD -- curl -s -o /dev/null -w "Metrics endpoint: %{http_code}\n" http://localhost:8080/metrics
kubectl exec -n $NAMESPACE $POD -- curl -s -o /dev/null -w "Health endpoint: %{http_code}\n" http://localhost:8081/health
echo ""
echo "✅ Debug information collected"

Diagnostic Checklist
markdown -38 lines

# NeuronTrace Diagnostic Checklist
## System Requirements
- [ ] Kernel version >= 5.8
- [ ] BTF available at /sys/kernel/btf/vmlinux
- [ ] CONFIG_BPF=y in kernel config
- [ ] Sufficient memory (>= 2GB)
- [ ] Sufficient CPU (>= 2 cores)
## Agent Status
- [ ] Pod is Running
- [ ] No CrashLoopBackOff
- [ ] No OOMKilled events
- [ ] Health check passing
- [ ] Readiness check passing
## eBPF Status
- [ ] Programs loaded (bpftool prog show)
- [ ] Maps created (bpftool map show)
- [ ] Probes attached
- [ ] No verification errors in logs
## Metrics
- [ ] Metrics endpoint responding (port 8080)
- [ ] Metrics being scraped by Prometheus
- [ ] No gaps in metric timeseries
- [ ] Event counters incrementing
## Performance
- [ ] CPU usage < 50%
- [ ] Memory usage < 80% of limit
- [ ] Event drop rate < 1%
- [ ] Ring buffer not full
## Network
- [ ] Can reach Prometheus
- [ ] Can reach API server
- [ ] DNS resolution working
- [ ] No network policies blocking traffic
## Security
- [ ] Appropriate RBAC permissions
- [ ] Pod security policy applied
- [ ] Secrets mounted correctly
- [ ] TLS configured (if enabled)




11. Upgrade Procedures
Pre-Upgrade Checklist
bash -41 lines

# scripts/pre-upgrade-check.sh
#!/bin/bash
set -e
echo "🔍 Pre-Upgrade Checklist"
echo "======================="
echo ""
# Check current version
CURRENT_VERSION=$(kubectl get daemonset -n neurontrace neurontrace -o jsonpath='{.spec.template.spec.containers[0].image}' | cut -d: -f2)
echo "Current version: $CURRENT_VERSION"
echo "Target version: ${1:-latest}"
echo ""
# Check cluster health
echo "Checking cluster health..."
kubectl get nodes
kubectl get pods -n neurontrace
echo ""
# Backup current configuration
echo "Backing up current configuration..."
mkdir -p backups/$(date +%Y%m%d)
kubectl get daemonset -n neurontrace neurontrace -o yaml > backups/$(date +%Y%m%d)/daemonset.yaml
kubectl get configmap -n neurontrace -o yaml > backups/$(date +%Y%m%d)/configmaps.yaml
kubectl get secret -n neurontrace -o yaml > backups/$(date +%Y%m%d)/secrets.yaml
echo "✅ Configuration backed up"
echo ""
# Check for breaking changes
echo "Checking release notes for breaking changes..."
# Add logic to check release notes
echo ""
# Verify resources
echo "Checking resource availability..."
kubectl top nodes
echo ""
# Check Prometheus
echo "Checking Prometheus connectivity..."
kubectl port-forward -n monitoring svc/prometheus 9090:9090 &
PF_PID=$!
sleep 2
curl -s http://localhost:9090/-/healthy || echo "⚠️  Prometheus not healthy"
kill $PF_PID
echo ""
echo "✅ Pre-upgrade checks complete"




Upgrade Strategy
Rolling Update (Recommended)
bash -17 lines

# scripts/rolling-upgrade.sh
#!/bin/bash
set -e
NEW_VERSION=${1:-latest}
echo "🚀 Rolling Upgrade to $NEW_VERSION"
echo "================================="
echo ""
# Update image
kubectl set image daemonset/neurontrace \
    -n neurontrace \
    neurontrace=docker.io/yourorg/neurontrace:$NEW_VERSION
# Watch rollout
kubectl rollout status daemonset/neurontrace -n neurontrace
# Verify new version
kubectl get pods -n neurontrace -o jsonpath='{.items[*].spec.containers[*].image}' | tr ' ' '\n' | sort -u
echo ""
echo "✅ Upgrade complete"

bash -16 lines

# Blue-Green upgrade process
# 1. Deploy green
kubectl apply -f deployments/kubernetes/daemonset-green.yaml
# 2. Wait for green to be ready
kubectl wait --for=condition=ready pod -l version=green -n neurontrace --timeout=300s
# 3. Verify green is working
kubectl logs -n neurontrace -l version=green --tail=50
# 4. Switch traffic (update service selector)
kubectl patch service neurontrace -n neurontrace -p '{"spec":{"selector":{"version":"green"}}}'
# 5. Monitor for issues
sleep 300
# 6. If successful, delete blue
kubectl delete daemonset neurontrace-blue -n neurontrace
# 7. If issues, rollback
# kubectl patch service neurontrace -n neurontrace -p '{"spec":{"selector":{"version":"blue"}}}'
# kubectl delete daemonset neurontrace-green -n neurontrace




Rollback Procedure
bash -17 lines

# scripts/rollback.sh
#!/bin/bash
set -e
echo "🔙 Rolling Back NeuronTrace"
echo "=========================="
echo ""
# Get previous version from history
PREVIOUS_VERSION=$(kubectl rollout history daemonset/neurontrace -n neurontrace | tail -2 | head -1 | awk '{print $1}')
echo "Rolling back to revision: $PREVIOUS_VERSION"
# Rollback
kubectl rollout undo daemonset/neurontrace -n neurontrace --to-revision=$PREVIOUS_VERSION
# Wait for rollback
kubectl rollout status daemonset/neurontrace -n neurontrace
# Verify
kubectl get pods -n neurontrace -o wide
echo ""
echo "✅ Rollback complete"




Post-Upgrade Verification

# scripts/post-upgrade-verify.sh
#!/bin/bash
set -e
echo "✅ Post-Upgrade Verification"
echo "============================"
echo ""
# Check pod status
echo "Checking pod status..."
kubectl get pods -n neurontrace
echo ""
# Check logs for errors
echo "Checking for errors in logs..."
ERROR_COUNT=$(kubectl logs -n neurontrace -l app=neurontrace --tail=100 | grep -c ERROR || true)
echo "Errors found: $ERROR_COUNT"
if [ $ERROR_COUNT -gt 10 ]; then
    echo "⚠️  High error count detected"
fi
echo ""
# Check metrics
echo "Checking metrics..."
POD=$(kubectl get pods -n neurontrace -l app=neurontrace -o jsonpath='{.items[0].metadata.name}')
kubectl port-forward -n neurontrace $POD 8080:8080 &
PF_PID=$!
sleep 2
METRICS_COUNT=$(curl -s http://localhost:8080/metrics | grep -c "neurontrace_" || true)
echo "Metrics exported: $METRICS_COUNT"
if [ $METRICS_COUNT -lt 10 ]; then
    echo "⚠️  Low metric count detected"
fi
kill $PF_PID
echo ""
# Check eBPF programs
echo "Checking eBPF programs..."
PROG_COUNT=$(kubectl exec -n neurontrace $POD -- bpftool prog show | grep -c neurontrace || true)
echo "eBPF programs loaded: $PROG_COUNT"
echo ""
# Check Prometheus scraping
echo "Checking Prometheus scraping..."
kubectl port-forward -n monitoring svc/prometheus 9090:9090 &
PF_PID=$!
sleep 2
SCRAPE_STATUS=$(curl -s 'http://localhost:9090/api/v1/targets' | jq -r '.data.activeTargets[] | select(.labels.job=="neurontrace") | .health' | head -1)
echo "Prometheus scrape status: $SCRAPE_STATUS"
kill $PF_PID
echo ""
# Generate test workload
echo "Generating test workload..."
kubectl run test-workload --image=busybox --restart=Never -- /bin/sh -c "for i in \$(seq 1 10); do ls /tmp; sleep 1; done"
sleep 15
kubectl delete pod test-workload
# Check if events were captured
sleep 5
kubectl port-forward -n neurontrace $POD 8080:8080 &
PF_PID=$!
sleep 2
EVENTS_PROCESSED=$(curl -s http://localhost:8080/metrics | grep "neurontrace_events_processed_total" | grep -v "#" | awk '{print $2}')
echo "Events processed: $EVENTS_PROCESSED"
kill $PF_PID
echo ""
if [ "$EVENTS_PROCESSED" -gt 0 ]; then
    echo "✅ Upgrade verification successful"
else
    echo "⚠️  No events processed - may need investigation"
fi




12. Disaster Recovery

What to Backup
bash -34 lines

# scripts/backup.sh
#!/bin/bash
set -e
BACKUP_DIR="backups/$(date +%Y%m%d_%H%M%S)"
mkdir -p $BACKUP_DIR
echo "📦 Creating NeuronTrace Backup"
echo "=============================="
echo "Backup directory: $BACKUP_DIR"
echo ""
# 1. Kubernetes resources
echo "Backing up Kubernetes resources..."
kubectl get daemonset -n neurontrace -o yaml > $BACKUP_DIR/daemonset.yaml
kubectl get configmap -n neurontrace -o yaml > $BACKUP_DIR/configmaps.yaml
kubectl get secret -n neurontrace -o yaml > $BACKUP_DIR/secrets.yaml
kubectl get service -n neurontrace -o yaml > $BACKUP_DIR/services.yaml
kubectl get servicemonitor -n neurontrace -o yaml > $BACKUP_DIR/servicemonitor.yaml 2>/dev/null || true
# 2. Prometheus configuration
echo "Backing up Prometheus configuration..."
kubectl get configmap -n monitoring prometheus-config -o yaml > $BACKUP_DIR/prometheus-config.yaml
kubectl get prometheusrule -n monitoring -o yaml > $BACKUP_DIR/prometheus-rules.yaml 2>/dev/null || true
# 3. Grafana dashboards
echo "Backing up Grafana dashboards..."
kubectl get configmap -n monitoring -l grafana_dashboard=1 -o yaml > $BACKUP_DIR/grafana-dashboards.yaml
# 4. Prometheus data (optional - can be large)
# echo "Backing up Prometheus data..."
# kubectl exec -n monitoring prometheus-0 -- tar czf /tmp/prometheus-data.tar.gz /prometheus
# kubectl cp monitoring/prometheus-0:/tmp/prometheus-data.tar.gz $BACKUP_DIR/prometheus-data.tar.gz
# 5. Create archive
echo "Creating archive..."
tar czf $BACKUP_DIR.tar.gz $BACKUP_DIR
rm -rf $BACKUP_DIR
echo ""
echo "✅ Backup complete: $BACKUP_DIR.tar.gz"
echo "Size: $(du -h $BACKUP_DIR.tar.gz | cut -f1)"




Automated Backups
yaml -69 lines

# deployments/kubernetes/backup-cronjob.yaml
apiVersion: batch/v1
kind: CronJob
meta
  name: neurontrace-backup
  namespace: neurontrace
spec:
  schedule: "0 2 * * *"  # Daily at 2 AM
  successfulJobsHistoryLimit: 7
  failedJobsHistoryLimit: 3
  jobTemplate:
    spec:
      template:
        spec:
          serviceAccountName: neurontrace-backup
          containers:
          - name: backup
            image: bitnami/kubectl:latest
            command:
            - /bin/bash
            - -c
            - |
              #!/bin/bash
              set -e
              BACKUP_DIR="/backups/$(date +%Y%m%d_%H%M%S)"
              mkdir -p $BACKUP_DIR
              # Backup resources
              kubectl get daemonset -n neurontrace -o yaml > $BACKUP_DIR/daemonset.yaml
              kubectl get configmap -n neurontrace -o yaml > $BACKUP_DIR/configmaps.yaml
              kubectl get secret -n neurontrace -o yaml > $BACKUP_DIR/secrets.yaml
              # Upload to S3 (optional)
              # aws s3 cp $BACKUP_DIR s3://your-bucket/neurontrace-backups/ --recursive
              echo "Backup complete: $BACKUP_DIR"
            volumeMounts:
            - name: backup-storage
              mountPath: /backups
          volumes:
          - name: backup-storage
            persistentVolumeClaim:
              claimName: backup-pvc
          restartPolicy: OnFailure
---
apiVersion: v1
kind: ServiceAccount
meta
  name: neurontrace-backup
  namespace: neurontrace
---
apiVersion: rbac.authorization.k8s.io/v1
kind: ClusterRole
meta
  name: neurontrace-backup
rules:
- apiGroups: ["", "apps", "monitoring.coreos.com"]
  resources: ["*"]
  verbs: ["get", "list"]
---
apiVersion: rbac.authorization.k8s.io/v1
kind: ClusterRoleBinding
meta
  name: neurontrace-backup
roleRef:
  apiGroup: rbac.authorization.k8s.io
  kind: ClusterRole
  name: neurontrace-backup
subjects:
- kind: ServiceAccount
  name: neurontrace-backup
  namespace: neurontrace




Restore Procedure
bash -54 lines

# scripts/restore.sh
#!/bin/bash
set -e
BACKUP_FILE=${1:-}
if [ -z "$BACKUP_FILE" ]; then
    echo "Usage: $0 <backup-file.tar.gz>"
    exit 1
fi
echo "🔄 Restoring NeuronTrace from Backup"
echo "===================================="
echo "Backup file: $BACKUP_FILE"
echo ""
# Extract backup
RESTORE_DIR=$(mktemp -d)
tar xzf $BACKUP_FILE -C $RESTORE_DIR
BACKUP_DIR=$(find $RESTORE_DIR -mindepth 1 -maxdepth 1 -type d)
echo "Extracted to: $BACKUP_DIR"
echo ""
# Confirm restore
read -p "This will replace current configuration. Continue? (yes/no) " -n 3 -r
echo
if [[ ! $REPLY =~ ^yes$ ]]; then
    echo "Restore cancelled"
    rm -rf $RESTORE_DIR
    exit 1
fi
# Stop current deployment
echo "Stopping current deployment..."
kubectl scale daemonset neurontrace -n neurontrace --replicas=0
sleep 10
# Restore resources
echo "Restoring Kubernetes resources..."
kubectl apply -f $BACKUP_DIR/daemonset.yaml
kubectl apply -f $BACKUP_DIR/configmaps.yaml
kubectl apply -f $BACKUP_DIR/secrets.yaml
kubectl apply -f $BACKUP_DIR/services.yaml
kubectl apply -f $BACKUP_DIR/servicemonitor.yaml 2>/dev/null || true
# Restore Prometheus config
echo "Restoring Prometheus configuration..."
kubectl apply -f $BACKUP_DIR/prometheus-config.yaml
kubectl apply -f $BACKUP_DIR/prometheus-rules.yaml 2>/dev/null || true
# Restore Grafana dashboards
echo "Restoring Grafana dashboards..."
kubectl apply -f $BACKUP_DIR/grafana-dashboards.yaml
# Wait for pods to be ready
echo "Waiting for pods to be ready..."
kubectl wait --for=condition=ready pod -l app=neurontrace -n neurontrace --timeout=300s
# Verify
echo "Verifying restore..."
kubectl get pods -n neurontrace
# Cleanup
rm -rf $RESTORE_DIR
echo ""
echo "✅ Restore complete"




Disaster Recovery Plan
markdown -56 lines

# NeuronTrace Disaster Recovery Plan
## Scenarios
### Scenario 1: Single Node Failure
**Impact**: Monitoring lost on one node
**Recovery Time**: 5 minutes (automatic)
**Procedure**:
1. DaemonSet automatically schedules new pod on healthy node
2. No manual intervention required
3. Verify with: `kubectl get pods -n neurontrace -o wide`
### Scenario 2: Configuration Corruption
**Impact**: Agent misconfiguration
**Recovery Time**: 10 minutes
**Procedure**:
1. Restore from backup: `./scripts/restore.sh backups/latest.tar.gz`
2. Verify configuration: `kubectl get configmap -n neurontrace`
3. Restart pods: `kubectl rollout restart daemonset/neurontrace -n neurontrace`
### Scenario 3: Complete Namespace Deletion
**Impact**: All NeuronTrace resources lost
**Recovery Time**: 30 minutes
**Procedure**:
1. Recreate namespace: `kubectl create namespace neurontrace`
2. Restore from backup: `./scripts/restore.sh backups/latest.tar.gz`
3. Verify all components: `./scripts/post-upgrade-verify.sh`
### Scenario 4: Prometheus Data Loss
**Impact**: Historical metrics lost
**Recovery Time**: Variable (depends on backup size)
**Procedure**:
1. Stop Prometheus: `kubectl scale statefulset prometheus -n monitoring --replicas=0`
2. Restore data: `kubectl cp backups/prometheus-data.tar.gz monitoring/prometheus-0:/prometheus/`
3. Start Prometheus: `kubectl scale statefulset prometheus -n monitoring --replicas=1`
### Scenario 5: Cluster Failure
**Impact**: Complete monitoring outage
**Recovery Time**: 1-2 hours
**Procedure**:
1. Provision new cluster
2. Install NeuronTrace: `./scripts/install.sh`
3. Restore configuration: `./scripts/restore.sh backups/latest.tar.gz`
4. Restore Prometheus data (if available)
5. Verify all components
## Recovery Time Objectives (RTO)
| Component | RTO | RPO |
|-----------|-----|-----|
| Single Node | 5 min | 0 |
| Configuration | 10 min | 24 hours |
| Namespace | 30 min | 24 hours |
| Prometheus Data | 2 hours | 24 hours |
| Full Cluster | 4 hours | 24 hours |
## Backup Schedule
- **Daily**: Full configuration backup (2 AM)
- **Weekly**: Prometheus data snapshot (Sunday 2 AM)
- **Monthly**: Complete system backup (1st of month)
- **Retention**: 30 days daily, 12 weeks weekly, 12 months monthly
## Testing Schedule
- **Monthly**: Configuration restore test
- **Quarterly**: Full disaster recovery drill
- **Annually**: Complete cluster recovery test




Health Monitoring
yaml -55 lines

# deployments/kubernetes/health-monitor.yaml
apiVersion: v1
kind: ConfigMap
meta
  name: health-monitor-script
  namespace: neurontrace
  monitor.sh: |
    #!/bin/bash
    while true; do
        # Check pod health
        UNHEALTHY=$(kubectl get pods -n neurontrace -o json | jq -r '.items[] | select(.status.phase != "Running") | .metadata.name')
        if [ -n "$UNHEALTHY" ]; then
            echo "⚠️  Unhealthy pods detected: $UNHEALTHY"
            # Send alert
            curl -X POST https://your-webhook-url \
                -H 'Content-Type: application/json' \
                -d "{\"text\":\"NeuronTrace unhealthy pods: $UNHEALTHY\"}"
        fi
        # Check metrics
        POD=$(kubectl get pods -n neurontrace -l app=neurontrace -o jsonpath='{.items[0].metadata.name}')
        EVENTS_DROPPED=$(kubectl exec -n neurontrace $POD -- curl -s http://localhost:8080/metrics | grep "neurontrace_events_dropped_total" | awk '{print $2}')
        if [ "$EVENTS_DROPPED" -gt 1000 ]; then
            echo "⚠️  High event drop rate: $EVENTS_DROPPED"
        fi
        sleep 60
    done
---
apiVersion: apps/v1
kind: Deployment
meta
  name: health-monitor
  namespace: neurontrace
spec:
  replicas: 1
  selector:
    matchLabels:
      app: health-monitor
  template:
    meta
      labels:
        app: health-monitor
    spec:
      serviceAccountName: neurontrace
      containers:
      - name: monitor
        image: bitnami/kubectl:latest
        command: ["/bin/bash", "/scripts/monitor.sh"]
        volumeMounts:
        - name: script
          mountPath: /scripts
      volumes:
      - name: script
        configMap:
          name: health-monitor-script
          defaultMode: 0755

2. Prometheus Setup
Step 1: Deploy Prometheus Operator
bash -14 lines

# Add Prometheus Operator Helm repo
helm repo add prometheus-community https://prometheus-community.github.io/helm-charts
helm repo update
# Create monitoring namespace
kubectl create namespace monitoring
# Install Prometheus Operator
helm install prometheus-operator prometheus-community/kube-prometheus-stack \
  --namespace monitoring \
  --set prometheus.prometheusSpec.retention=30d \
  --set prometheus.prometheusSpec.storageSpec.volumeClaimTemplate.spec.resources.requests.storage=100Gi \
  --set prometheus.prometheusSpec.resources.requests.memory=4Gi \
  --set prometheus.prometheusSpec.resources.limits.memory=8Gi \
  --set alertmanager.alertmanagerSpec.storage.volumeClaimTemplate.spec.resources.requests.storage=10Gi \
  --set grafana.adminPassword=admin123




Step 2: Custom Prometheus Configuration
yaml -104 lines

# deployments/monitoring/prometheus-values.yaml
prometheus:
  prometheusSpec:
    # Retention
    retention: 30d
    retentionSize: 50GB
    # Resources
    resources:
      requests:
        memory: 4Gi
        cpu: 2000m
      limits:
        memory: 8Gi
        cpu: 4000m
    # Storage
    storageSpec:
      volumeClaimTemplate:
        spec:
          storageClassName: fast-ssd
          accessModes: ["ReadWriteOnce"]
          resources:
            requests:
              storage: 100Gi
    # External labels
    externalLabels:
      cluster: production
      environment: prod
      region: us-west-2
    # Remote write (for long-term storage)
    remoteWrite:
    - url: http://thanos-receive:19291/api/v1/receive
      queueConfig:
        capacity: 10000
        maxShards: 50
        minShards: 1
        maxSamplesPerSend: 5000
        batchSendDeadline: 5s
        minBackoff: 30ms
        maxBackoff: 100ms
      writeRelabelConfigs:
      - sourceLabels: [__name__]
        regex: 'neurontrace_.*'
        action: keep
    # Service monitors
    serviceMonitorSelector:
      matchLabels:
        prometheus: neurontrace
    # Pod monitors
    podMonitorSelector:
      matchLabels:
        prometheus: neurontrace
    # Rule selector
    ruleSelector:
      matchLabels:
        prometheus: neurontrace
    # Additional scrape configs
    additionalScrapeConfigs:
    - job_name: 'neurontrace-agents'
      scrape_interval: 30s
      scrape_timeout: 10s
      kubernetes_sd_configs:
      - role: pod
        namespaces:
          names:
          - neurontrace
      relabel_configs:
      # Keep only pods with prometheus.io/scrape=true
      - source_labels: [__meta_kubernetes_pod_annotation_prometheus_io_scrape]
        action: keep
        regex: true
      # Use custom port
      - source_labels: [__meta_kubernetes_pod_annotation_prometheus_io_port]
        action: replace
        target_label: __address__
        regex: ([^:]+)(?::\d+)?;(\d+)
        replacement: $1:$2
      # Use custom path
      - source_labels: [__meta_kubernetes_pod_annotation_prometheus_io_path]
        action: replace
        target_label: __metrics_path__
        regex: (.+)
      # Add metadata
      - source_labels: [__meta_kubernetes_namespace]
        target_label: namespace
      - source_labels: [__meta_kubernetes_pod_name]
        target_label: pod
      - source_labels: [__meta_kubernetes_pod_node_name]
        target_label: node
      - source_labels: [__meta_kubernetes_pod_label_app]
        target_label: app
      - source_labels: [__meta_kubernetes_pod_label_version]
        target_label: version
      metric_relabel_configs:
      # Drop high-cardinality metrics
      - source_labels: [__name__]
        regex: 'neurontrace_.*_bucket'
        action: drop
      # Add cluster label
      - target_label: cluster
        replacement: production
# Update Prometheus with custom values
helm upgrade prometheus-operator prometheus-community/kube-prometheus-stack \
  --namespace monitoring \
  --values deployments/monitoring/prometheus-values.yaml




Step 3: Recording Rules
yaml -113 lines

# deployments/monitoring/recording-rules.yaml
apiVersion: monitoring.coreos.com/v1
kind: PrometheusRule
meta
  name: neurontrace-recording-rules
  namespace: monitoring
  labels:
    prometheus: neurontrace
    role: recording-rules
spec:
  groups:
  # Process metrics aggregations
  - name: neurontrace_process_aggregations
    interval: 30s
    rules:
    # Total process starts per node
    - record: node:neurontrace_process_starts:rate5m
      expr: sum by (node) (rate(neurontrace_process_starts_total[5m]))
    # Process starts by application
    - record: app:neurontrace_process_starts:rate5m
      expr: sum by (comm) (rate(neurontrace_process_starts_total[5m]))
    # Top 10 processes
    - record: neurontrace_process_top10:rate5m
      expr: topk(10, sum by (comm) (rate(neurontrace_process_starts_total[5m])))
  # Network metrics aggregations
  - name: neurontrace_network_aggregations
    interval: 30s
    rules:
    # Total network bandwidth per node
    - record: node:neurontrace_network_bytes:rate5m
      expr: |
        sum by (node) (
          rate(neurontrace_network_bytes_sent_total[5m]) +
          rate(neurontrace_network_bytes_received_total[5m])
        )
    # Connection rate
    - record: neurontrace_network_connections:rate5m
      expr: sum(rate(neurontrace_network_connections_total[5m]))
    # Network errors
    - record: neurontrace_network_errors:rate5m
      expr: sum(rate(neurontrace_network_errors_total[5m]))
  # GPU metrics aggregations
  - name: neurontrace_gpu_aggregations
    interval: 30s
    rules:
    # Average GPU utilization
    - record: gpu:neurontrace_utilization:avg
      expr: avg by (device_id, device_name) (neurontrace_gpu_utilization_percent)
    # Total GPU memory used
    - record: gpu:neurontrace_memory_used:sum
      expr: sum by (device_id) (neurontrace_gpu_memory_used_bytes)
    # GPU memory utilization percentage
    - record: gpu:neurontrace_memory_utilization:percent
      expr: |
        (
          neurontrace_gpu_memory_used_bytes /
          neurontrace_gpu_memory_total_bytes
        ) * 100
    # Kernel launch rate
    - record: gpu:neurontrace_kernel_launches:rate5m
      expr: sum by (device_id) (rate(neurontrace_gpu_kernel_launches_total[5m]))
    # Average kernel duration
    - record: gpu:neurontrace_kernel_duration:avg
      expr: |
        sum by (device_id) (rate(neurontrace_gpu_kernel_duration_seconds_sum[5m])) /
        sum by (device_id) (rate(neurontrace_gpu_kernel_duration_seconds_count[5m]))
  # MCP metrics aggregations
  - name: neurontrace_mcp_aggregations
    interval: 30s
    rules:
    # Tool call rate
    - record: mcp:neurontrace_tool_calls:rate5m
      expr: sum by (tool_name) (rate(neurontrace_mcp_tool_calls_total[5m]))
    # Tool success rate
    - record: mcp:neurontrace_tool_success_rate:ratio
      expr: |
        sum by (tool_name) (rate(neurontrace_mcp_tool_calls_success_total[5m])) /
        sum by (tool_name) (rate(neurontrace_mcp_tool_calls_total[5m]))
    # Tool error rate
    - record: mcp:neurontrace_tool_error_rate:ratio
      expr: |
        sum by (tool_name) (rate(neurontrace_mcp_tool_calls_error_total[5m])) /
        sum by (tool_name) (rate(neurontrace_mcp_tool_calls_total[5m]))
    # Average tool duration
    - record: mcp:neurontrace_tool_duration:avg
      expr: |
        sum by (tool_name) (rate(neurontrace_mcp_tool_duration_seconds_sum[5m])) /
        sum by (tool_name) (rate(neurontrace_mcp_tool_duration_seconds_count[5m]))
    # Security violations rate
    - record: mcp:neurontrace_violations:rate5m
      expr: sum by (severity) (rate(neurontrace_mcp_security_violations_total[5m]))
  # Agent health aggregations
  - name: neurontrace_agent_health
    interval: 30s
    rules:
    # Event processing rate
    - record: agent:neurontrace_events:rate5m
      expr: sum by (node) (rate(neurontrace_events_processed_total[5m]))
    # Event drop rate
    - record: agent:neurontrace_event_drops:rate5m
      expr: sum by (node) (rate(neurontrace_events_dropped_total[5m]))
    # Agent uptime
    - record: agent:neurontrace_uptime:seconds
      expr: neurontrace_agent_uptime_seconds
    # Memory usage
    - record: agent:neurontrace_memory:bytes
      expr: process_resident_memory_bytes{job="neurontrace"}
    # CPU usage
    - record: agent:neurontrace_cpu:rate5m
      expr: rate(process_cpu_seconds_total{job="neurontrace"}[5m])
---
# Apply recording rules
kubectl apply -f deployments/monitoring/recording-rules.yaml

# deployments/monitoring/grafana-datasources.yaml
apiVersion: v1
kind: ConfigMap
meta
  name: grafana-datasources
  namespace: monitoring
  labels:
    grafana_datasource: "1"
  prometheus.yaml: |
    apiVersion: 1
    datasources:
    - name: Prometheus
      type: prometheus
      access: proxy
      url: http://prometheus-operator-prometheus:9090
      isDefault: true
      editable: false
      jsonData:
        timeInterval: 30s
        queryTimeout: 60s
        httpMethod: POST
        # Enable exemplars
        exemplarTraceIdDestinations:
        - name: trace_id
          datasourceUid: tempo
      # Optional: Basic auth
      # basicAuth: true
      # basicAuthUser: admin
      # secureJsonData:
      #   basicAuthPassword: password
---
# Apply datasource config
kubectl apply -f deployments/monitoring/grafana-datasources.yaml
# Restart Grafana to pick up changes
kubectl rollout restart deployment -n monitoring prometheus-operator-grafana

# deployments/monitoring/alertmanager-config.yaml
apiVersion: v1
kind: Secret
meta
  name: alertmanager-config
  namespace: monitoring
type: Opaque
stringData:
  alertmanager.yaml: |
    global:
      resolve_timeout: 5m
      # Slack webhook
      slack_api_url: 'https://hooks.slack.com/services/YOUR/SLACK/WEBHOOK'
      # PagerDuty
      pagerduty_url: 'https://events.pagerduty.com/v2/enqueue'
      # SMTP settings
      smtp_from: 'neurontrace-alerts@yourcompany.com'
      smtp_smarthost: 'smtp.gmail.com:587'
      smtp_auth_username: 'neurontrace-alerts@yourcompany.com'
      smtp_auth_password: 'your-app-password'
      smtp_require_tls: true
    # Templates
    templates:
    - '/etc/alertmanager/templates/*.tmpl'
    # Route tree
    route:
      receiver: 'default'
      group_by: ['alertname', 'cluster', 'service', 'severity']
      group_wait: 10s
      group_interval: 5m
      repeat_interval: 4h
      routes:
      # Critical alerts - immediate notification
      - match:
          severity: critical
        receiver: 'critical-alerts'
        group_wait: 0s
        repeat_interval: 1h
        continue: true
      # High severity - page on-call
      - match:
          severity: high
        receiver: 'high-priority'
        group_wait: 30s
        repeat_interval: 2h
      # Warning - team channel
      - match:
          severity: warning
        receiver: 'team-alerts'
        group_wait: 1m
        repeat_interval: 12h
      # GPU-specific alerts
      - match:
          component: gpu
        receiver: 'gpu-team'
        routes:
        - match:
            severity: critical
          receiver: 'gpu-critical'
      # MCP security alerts
      - match:
          component: security
        receiver: 'security-team'
        routes:
        - match:
            severity: critical
          receiver: 'security-critical'
      # MCP alerts
      - match:
          component: mcp
        receiver: 'mcp-team'
      # Performance alerts
      - match:
          component: performance
        receiver: 'performance-team'
      # Maintenance silencing
      - match:
          alertname: Watchdog
        receiver: 'null'
    # Inhibition rules (suppress alerts)
    inhibit_rules:
    # Suppress warnings if critical alert is firing
    - source_match:
        severity: 'critical'
      target_match:
        severity: 'warning'
      equal: ['alertname', 'cluster', 'service']
    # Suppress high if critical
    - source_match:
        severity: 'critical'
      target_match:
        severity: 'high'
      equal: ['alertname', 'cluster', 'service']
    # Suppress node alerts if node is down
    - source_match:
        alertname: 'NodeDown'
      target_match_re:
        alertname: 'Node.*'
      equal: ['node']
    # Suppress MCP tool alerts if MCP server is down
    - source_match:
        alertname: 'MCPServerDown'
      target_match_re:
        alertname: 'MCPTool.*'
      equal: ['server_name']
    # Receivers
    receivers:
    # Default receiver
    - name: 'default'
      slack_configs:
      - channel: '#neurontrace-alerts'
        title: '{{ .GroupLabels.alertname }}'
        text: |
          {{ range .Alerts }}
          *Alert:* {{ .Labels.alertname }}
          *Severity:* {{ .Labels.severity }}
          *Summary:* {{ .Annotations.summary }}
          *Description:* {{ .Annotations.description }}
          {{ end }}
        send_resolved: true
    # Critical alerts - multiple channels
    - name: 'critical-alerts'
      slack_configs:
      - channel: '#critical-alerts'
        title: '🚨 CRITICAL: {{ .GroupLabels.alertname }}'
        text: |
          {{ range .Alerts }}
          *Alert:* {{ .Labels.alertname }}
          *Cluster:* {{ .Labels.cluster }}
          *Node:* {{ .Labels.node }}
          *Summary:* {{ .Annotations.summary }}
          *Description:* {{ .Annotations.description }}
          *Runbook:* {{ .Annotations.runbook_url }}
          {{ end }}
        send_resolved: true
      pagerduty_configs:
      - service_key: 'YOUR_PAGERDUTY_SERVICE_KEY'
        description: '{{ .GroupLabels.alertname }}: {{ .Annotations.summary }}'
        details:
          firing: '{{ .Alerts.Firing | len }}'
          resolved: '{{ .Alerts.Resolved | len }}'
      email_configs:
      - to: 'oncall@yourcompany.com'
        headers:
          Subject: '[CRITICAL] {{ .GroupLabels.alertname }}'
        html: |
          <h2>Critical Alert</h2>
          {{ range .Alerts }}
          <p><strong>{{ .Labels.alertname }}</strong></p>
          <p>{{ .Annotations.description }}</p>
          {{ end }}
    # High priority
    - name: 'high-priority'
      slack_configs:
      - channel: '#high-priority-alerts'
        title: '⚠️ HIGH: {{ .GroupLabels.alertname }}'
      pagerduty_configs:
      - service_key: 'YOUR_PAGERDUTY_SERVICE_KEY'
        severity: 'warning'
    # Team alerts
    - name: 'team-alerts'
      slack_configs:
      - channel: '#neurontrace-team'
        title: 'ℹ️ {{ .GroupLabels.alertname }}'
    # GPU team
    - name: 'gpu-team'
      slack_configs:
      - channel: '#gpu-alerts'
        title: '🖥️ GPU Alert: {{ .GroupLabels.alertname }}'
        text: |
          {{ range .Alerts }}
          *Device:* {{ .Labels.device_name }} ({{ .Labels.device_id }})
          *Issue:* {{ .Annotations.description }}
          {{ end }}
    - name: 'gpu-critical'
      slack_configs:
      - channel: '#gpu-critical'
        title: '🚨 GPU CRITICAL: {{ .GroupLabels.alertname }}'
      email_configs:
      - to: 'gpu-team@yourcompany.com'
    # Security team
    - name: 'security-team'
      slack_configs:
      - channel: '#security-alerts'
        title: '🔒 Security: {{ .GroupLabels.alertname }}'
        text: |
          {{ range .Alerts }}
          *Tool:* {{ .Labels.tool_name }}
          *Violation:* {{ .Annotations.description }}
          *Severity:* {{ .Labels.severity }}
          {{ end }}
      email_configs:
      - to: 'security@yourcompany.com'
        headers:
          Subject: '[SECURITY] {{ .GroupLabels.alertname }}'
    - name: 'security-critical'
      slack_configs:
      - channel: '#security-critical'
      pagerduty_configs:
      - service_key: 'YOUR_SECURITY_PAGERDUTY_KEY'
      email_configs:
      - to: 'security-oncall@yourcompany.com'
    # MCP team
    - name: 'mcp-team'
      slack_configs:
      - channel: '#mcp-alerts'
        title: '🔌 MCP: {{ .GroupLabels.alertname }}'
    # Performance team
    - name: 'performance-team'
      slack_configs:
      - channel: '#performance-alerts'
        title: '⚡ Performance: {{ .GroupLabels.alertname }}'
    # Null receiver (for silencing)
    - name: 'null'
---
# Apply AlertManager config
kubectl apply -f deployments/monitoring/alertmanager-config.yaml

# deployments/monitoring/alertmanager-templates.yaml
apiVersion: v1
kind: ConfigMap
meta
  name: alertmanager-templates
  namespace: monitoring
  default.tmpl: |
    {{ define "slack.default.title" }}
    [{{ .Status | toUpper }}{{ if eq .Status "firing" }}:{{ .Alerts.Firing | len }}{{ end }}] {{ .GroupLabels.SortedPairs.Values | join " " }}
    {{ end }}
    {{ define "slack.default.text" }}
    {{ range .Alerts }}
    *Alert:* {{ .Labels.alertname }}
    *Severity:* {{ .Labels.severity }}
    *Summary:* {{ .Annotations.summary }}
    *Description:* {{ .Annotations.description }}
    {{ if .Labels.node }}*Node:* {{ .Labels.node }}{{ end }}
    {{ if .Labels.pod }}*Pod:* {{ .Labels.pod }}{{ end }}
    {{ if .Annotations.runbook_url }}*Runbook:* {{ .Annotations.runbook_url }}{{ end }}
    {{ end }}
    {{ end }}
    {{ define "slack.default.color" }}
    {{ if eq .Status "firing" }}
      {{ if eq .CommonLabels.severity "critical" }}danger{{ else if eq .CommonLabels.severity "warning" }}warning{{ else }}good{{ end }}
    {{ else }}good{{ end }}
    {{ end }}
---

5. Alert Rules
Comprehensive Alert Rules
yaml -265 lines

# deployments/monitoring/alert-rules.yaml
apiVersion: monitoring.coreos.com/v1
kind: PrometheusRule
meta
  name: neurontrace-alert-rules
  namespace: monitoring
  labels:
    prometheus: neurontrace
    role: alert-rules
spec:
  groups:
  # ============================================
  # Agent Health Alerts
  # ============================================
  - name: neurontrace_agent_health
    interval: 30s
    rules:
    - alert: NeuronTraceAgentDown
      expr: up{job="neurontrace"} == 0
      for: 2m
      labels:
        severity: critical
        component: agent
      annotations:
        summary: "NeuronTrace agent is down"
        description: "Agent on node {{ $labels.node }} has been down for more than 2 minutes"
        runbook_url: "https://docs.neurontrace.io/runbooks/agent-down"
    - alert: NeuronTraceHighEventDropRate
      expr: |
        rate(neurontrace_events_dropped_total[5m]) /
        rate(neurontrace_events_processed_total[5m]) > 0.01
      for: 5m
      labels:
        severity: warning
        component: agent
      annotations:
        summary: "High event drop rate detected"
        description: "Agent on {{ $labels.node }} is dropping {{ $value | humanizePercentage }} of events"
        runbook_url: "https://docs.neurontrace.io/runbooks/high-drop-rate"
    - alert: NeuronTraceHighMemoryUsage
      expr: |
        process_resident_memory_bytes{job="neurontrace"} /
        (1024 * 1024 * 1024) > 1.5
      for: 10m
      labels:
        severity: warning
        component: agent
      annotations:
        summary: "Agent memory usage is high"
        description: "Agent on {{ $labels.node }} is using {{ $value }}GB of memory"
    - alert: NeuronTraceHighCPUUsage
      expr: rate(process_cpu_seconds_total{job="neurontrace"}[5m]) > 0.8
      for: 10m
      labels:
        severity: warning
        component: agent
      annotations:
        summary: "Agent CPU usage is high"
        description: "Agent on {{ $labels.node }} is using {{ $value | humanizePercentage }} CPU"
    - alert: NeuronTraceEBPFProgramDetached
      expr: neurontrace_map_entries{map_name="stats"} == 0
      for: 1m
      labels:
        severity: critical
        component: ebpf
      annotations:
        summary: "eBPF program detached"
        description: "eBPF program on {{ $labels.node }} appears to be detached"
  # ============================================
  # GPU Alerts
  # ============================================
  - name: neurontrace_gpu_alerts
    interval: 30s
    rules:
    - alert: GPUHighUtilization
      expr: neurontrace_gpu_utilization_percent > 95
      for: 10m
      labels:
        severity: warning
        component: gpu
      annotations:
        summary: "GPU utilization is very high"
        description: "GPU {{ $labels.device_name }} ({{ $labels.device_id }}) on {{ $labels.node }} is at {{ $value }}% utilization"
    - alert: GPUHighMemoryUsage
      expr: |
        (neurontrace_gpu_memory_used_bytes / neurontrace_gpu_memory_total_bytes) * 100 > 90
      for: 5m
      labels:
        severity: warning
        component: gpu
      annotations:
        summary: "GPU memory usage is high"
        description: "GPU {{ $labels.device_id }} on {{ $labels.node }} is using {{ $value }}% of memory"
    - alert: GPUMemoryLeak
      expr: |
        deriv(neurontrace_gpu_memory_used_bytes[30m]) > 1e8
      for: 30m
      labels:
        severity: high
        component: gpu
      annotations:
        summary: "Possible GPU memory leak detected"
        description: "GPU {{ $labels.device_id }} memory usage increasing at {{ $value | humanize }}B/s"
    - alert: GPUHighTemperature
      expr: neurontrace_gpu_temperature_celsius > 85
      for: 5m
      labels:
        severity: high
        component: gpu
      annotations:
        summary: "GPU temperature is high"
        description: "GPU {{ $labels.device_id }} temperature is {{ $value }}°C"
    - alert: GPUKernelLaunchFailures
      expr: rate(neurontrace_gpu_kernel_launch_failures_total[5m]) > 0
      for: 2m
      labels:
        severity: high
        component: gpu
      annotations:
        summary: "GPU kernel launches failing"
        description: "GPU {{ $labels.device_id }} has {{ $value }} kernel launch failures per second"
  # ============================================
  # MCP Alerts
  # ============================================
  - name: neurontrace_mcp_alerts
    interval: 30s
    rules:
    - alert: MCPServerDown
      expr: neurontrace_mcp_server_uptime_seconds == 0
      for: 1m
      labels:
        severity: critical
        component: mcp
      annotations:
        summary: "MCP server is down"
        description: "MCP server {{ $labels.server_name }} (PID {{ $labels.server_pid }}) is not responding"
    - alert: MCPHighErrorRate
      expr: |
        rate(neurontrace_mcp_tool_calls_error_total[5m]) /
        rate(neurontrace_mcp_tool_calls_total[5m]) > 0.1
      for: 5m
      labels:
        severity: warning
        component: mcp
      annotations:
        summary: "MCP tool has high error rate"
        description: "Tool {{ $labels.tool_name }} has {{ $value | humanizePercentage }} error rate"
    - alert: MCPHighLatency
      expr: |
        histogram_quantile(0.95,
          rate(neurontrace_mcp_tool_duration_seconds_bucket[5m])
        ) > 5
      for: 5m
      labels:
        severity: warning
        component: mcp
      annotations:
        summary: "MCP tool has high latency"
        description: "Tool {{ $labels.tool_name }} p95 latency is {{ $value }}s"
    - alert: MCPSecurityViolation
      expr: rate(neurontrace_mcp_security_violations_total{severity="high"}[5m]) > 0
      for: 1m
      labels:
        severity: high
        component: security
      annotations:
        summary: "High severity MCP security violation"
        description: "{{ $value }} high severity violations per second for tool {{ $labels.tool_name }}"
    - alert: MCPSuspiciousActivity
      expr: rate(neurontrace_mcp_suspicious_activity_total[5m]) > 0
      for: 2m
      labels:
        severity: warning
        component: security
      annotations:
        summary: "Suspicious MCP activity detected"
        description: "Pattern {{ $labels.pattern }} detected at {{ $value }} occurrences/s"
    - alert: MCPRateLimitExceeded
      expr: rate(neurontrace_mcp_tool_calls_denied_total[5m]) > 1
      for: 5m
      labels:
        severity: info
        component: mcp
      annotations:
        summary: "MCP rate limit exceeded"
        description: "Tool {{ $labels.tool_name }} is being rate limited"
  # ============================================
  # Performance Alerts
  # ============================================
  - name: neurontrace_performance_alerts
    interval: 30s
    rules:
    - alert: HighNetworkLatency
      expr: |
        histogram_quantile(0.95,
          rate(neurontrace_network_latency_seconds_bucket[5m])
        ) > 0.1
      for: 10m
      labels:
        severity: warning
        component: performance
      annotations:
        summary: "High network latency detected"
        description: "Network p95 latency is {{ $value }}s on {{ $labels.node }}"
    - alert: HighFileIOLatency
      expr: |
        histogram_quantile(0.95,
          rate(neurontrace_file_operation_duration_seconds_bucket[5m])
        ) > 0.5
      for: 10m
      labels:
        severity: warning
        component: performance
      annotations:
        summary: "High file I/O latency"
        description: "File operations p95 latency is {{ $value }}s on {{ $labels.node }}"
    - alert: HighPageFaultRate
      expr: rate(neurontrace_page_faults_total[5m]) > 1000
      for: 5m
      labels:
        severity: warning
        component: performance
      annotations:
        summary: "High page fault rate"
        description: "{{ $value }} page faults per second on {{ $labels.node }}"
  # ============================================
  # ML/AI Alerts
  # ============================================
  - name: neurontrace_ml_alerts
    interval: 30s
    rules:
    - alert: MLModelHighLatency
      expr: |
        histogram_quantile(0.95,
          rate(neurontrace_ml_forward_duration_seconds_bucket[5m])
        ) > 1
      for: 10m
      labels:
        severity: warning
        component: ml
      annotations:
        summary: "ML model has high inference latency"
        description: "Model {{ $labels.model }} p95 latency is {{ $value }}s"
    - alert: MLModelLowThroughput
      expr: neurontrace_ml_throughput_samples_per_second < 10
      for: 10m
      labels:
        severity: warning
        component: ml
      annotations:
        summary: "ML model has low throughput"
        description: "Model {{ $labels.model }} throughput is {{ $value }} samples/s"
    - alert: MLTrainingStalled
      expr: |
        rate(neurontrace_ml_optimizer_steps_total[5m]) == 0
      for: 10m
      labels:
        severity: high
        component: ml
      annotations:
        summary: "ML training appears stalled"
        description: "No optimizer steps for model {{ $labels.model }} in 10 minutes"
---
# Apply alert rules
kubectl apply -f deployments/monitoring/alert-rules.yaml

Step 2: Configure Slack in AlertManager
yaml -48 lines

# deployments/monitoring/alertmanager-slack-config.yaml
apiVersion: v1
kind: Secret
meta
  name: alertmanager-slack-config
  namespace: monitoring
type: Opaque
stringData:
  slack-webhook-url: "https://hooks.slack.com/services/YOUR/WEBHOOK/URL"
  alertmanager.yaml: |
    global:
      slack_api_url_file: /etc/alertmanager/secrets/slack-webhook-url
    receivers:
    - name: 'slack-notifications'
      slack_configs:
      - channel: '#neurontrace-alerts'
        username: 'NeuronTrace AlertManager'
        icon_emoji: ':chart_with_upwards_trend:'
        title: '{{ template "slack.default.title" . }}'
        text: '{{ template "slack.default.text" . }}'
        color: '{{ template "slack.default.color" . }}'
        # Actions
        actions:
        - type: button
          text: 'View in Grafana'
          url: 'https://grafana.yourcompany.com/d/neurontrace-overview'
        - type: button
          text: 'View in Prometheus'
          url: 'https://prometheus.yourcompany.com/alerts'
        - type: button
          text: 'Silence'
          url: '{{ template "slack.default.silenceURL" . }}'
        # Fields
        fields:
        - title: 'Environment'
          value: '{{ .CommonLabels.environment }}'
          short: true
        - title: 'Cluster'
          value: '{{ .CommonLabels.cluster }}'
          short: true
        - title: 'Severity'
          value: '{{ .CommonLabels.severity }}'
          short: true
        - title: 'Firing'
          value: '{{ .Alerts.Firing | len }}'
          short: true
---
kubectl apply -f deployments/monitoring/alertmanager-slack-config.yaml

# deployments/monitoring/slack-templates.yaml
apiVersion: v1
kind: ConfigMap
meta
  name: alertmanager-slack-templates
  namespace: monitoring
  slack.tmpl: |
    {{ define "slack.default.title" }}
    {{ if eq .Status "firing" }}🔥{{ else }}✅{{ end }} [{{ .Status | toUpper }}] {{ .GroupLabels.alertname }}
    {{ end }}
    {{ define "slack.default.text" }}
    {{ if eq .Status "firing" }}
    *Alerts Firing:*
    {{ range .Alerts.Firing }}
    • *{{ .Labels.alertname }}*
      {{ if .Labels.severity }}Severity: `{{ .Labels.severity }}`{{ end }}
      {{ if .Labels.node }}Node: `{{ .Labels.node }}`{{ end }}
      {{ if .Labels.pod }}Pod: `{{ .Labels.pod }}`{{ end }}
      {{ .Annotations.description }}
      {{ if .Annotations.runbook_url }}<{{ .Annotations.runbook_url }}|Runbook>{{ end }}
    {{ end }}
    {{ else }}
    *Alerts Resolved:*
    {{ range .Alerts.Resolved }}
    • {{ .Labels.alertname }} ({{ .Labels.severity }})
    {{ end }}
    {{ end }}
    {{ end }}
    {{ define "slack.default.color" }}
    {{ if eq .Status "firing" }}
      {{ if eq .CommonLabels.severity "critical" }}danger
      {{ else if eq .CommonLabels.severity "high" }}warning
      {{ else if eq .CommonLabels.severity "warning" }}#FFA500
      {{ else }}good{{ end }}
    {{ else }}good{{ end }}
    {{ end }}
    {{ define "slack.default.silenceURL" }}
    {{ .ExternalURL }}/#/silences/new?filter=%7B
    {{- range .CommonLabels.SortedPairs -}}
      {{- if ne .Name "alertname" -}}
        {{- .Name }}%3D"{{- .Value -}}"%2C%20
      {{- end -}}
    {{- end -}}
    alertname%3D"{{ .CommonLabels.alertname }}"%7D
    {{ end }}
---
kubectl apply -f deployments/monitoring/slack-templates.yaml

# deployments/monitoring/email-config.yaml
apiVersion: v1
kind: Secret
meta
  name: smtp-config
  namespace: monitoring
type: Opaque
stringData:
  smtp-password: "your-smtp-password"
  email.yaml: |
    global:
      smtp_from: 'neurontrace-alerts@yourcompany.com'
      smtp_smarthost: 'smtp.gmail.com:587'
      smtp_auth_username: 'neurontrace-alerts@yourcompany.com'
      smtp_auth_password_file: /etc/alertmanager/secrets/smtp-password
      smtp_require_tls: true
    receivers:
    - name: 'email-notifications'
      email_configs:
      - to: 'team@yourcompany.com'
        headers:
          Subject: '[{{ .Status | toUpper }}] {{ .GroupLabels.alertname }}'
        html: |
          <!DOCTYPE html>
          <html>
          <head>
            <style>
              body { font-family: Arial, sans-serif; }
              .alert { padding: 15px; margin: 10px 0; border-radius: 5px; }
              .critical { background-color: #f8d7da; border: 1px solid #f5c6cb; }
              .warning { background-color: #fff3cd; border: 1px solid #ffeeba; }
              .info { background-color: #d1ecf1; border: 1px solid #bee5eb; }
              .resolved { background-color: #d4edda; border: 1px solid #c3e6cb; }
              .label { font-weight: bold; }
            </style>
          </head>
          <body>
            <h2>NeuronTrace Alert Notification</h2>
            {{ if eq .Status "firing" }}
            <p><strong>Status:</strong> 🔥 FIRING</p>
            {{ range .Alerts.Firing }}
            <div class="alert {{ .Labels.severity }}">
              <p class="label">{{ .Labels.alertname }}</p>
              <p><strong>Severity:</strong> {{ .Labels.severity }}</p>
              {{ if .Labels.node }}<p><strong>Node:</strong> {{ .Labels.node }}</p>{{ end }}
              {{ if .Labels.pod }}<p><strong>Pod:</strong> {{ .Labels.pod }}</p>{{ end }}
              <p><strong>Summary:</strong> {{ .Annotations.summary }}</p>
              <p><strong>Description:</strong> {{ .Annotations.description }}</p>
              {{ if .Annotations.runbook_url }}
              <p><a href="{{ .Annotations.runbook_url }}">View Runbook</a></p>
              {{ end }}
            </div>
            {{ end }}
            {{ else }}
            <div class="alert resolved">
              <p><strong>Status:</strong> ✅ RESOLVED</p>
              {{ range .Alerts.Resolved }}
              <p>{{ .Labels.alertname }} ({{ .Labels.severity }})</p>
              {{ end }}
            </div>
            {{ end }}
            <hr>
            <p><small>
              <a href="https://grafana.yourcompany.com">View in Grafana</a> |
              <a href="https://prometheus.yourcompany.com">View in Prometheus</a>
            </small></p>
          </body>
          </html>

Webhook Integration
yaml -86 lines

# deployments/monitoring/webhook-config.yaml
apiVersion: v1
kind: ConfigMap
meta
  name: webhook-config
  namespace: monitoring
  webhook.yaml: |
    receivers:
    - name: 'webhook-receiver'
      webhook_configs:
      - url: 'https://your-webhook-endpoint.com/alerts'
        send_resolved: true
        http_config:
          bearer_token: 'your-bearer-token'
          # Or use basic auth
          # basic_auth:
          #   username: 'user'
          #   password: 'pass'
        # Custom payload
        # The webhook will receive JSON with alert data
---
# Example webhook server to receive alerts
# deployments/monitoring/webhook-server.yaml
apiVersion: apps/v1
kind: Deployment
meta
  name: alert-webhook-server
  namespace: monitoring
spec:
  replicas: 2
  selector:
    matchLabels:
      app: alert-webhook
  template:
    meta
      labels:
        app: alert-webhook
    spec:
      containers:
      - name: webhook
        image: python:3.9-slim
        command:
        - python
        - -c
        - |
          from http.server import HTTPServer, BaseHTTPRequestHandler
          import json
          import logging
          logging.basicConfig(level=logging.INFO)
          class AlertWebhook(BaseHTTPRequestHandler):
              def do_POST(self):
                  content_length = int(self.headers['Content-Length'])
                  body = self.rfile.read(content_length)
                  try:
                      alert_data = json.loads(body)
                      logging.info(f"Received alert: {json.dumps(alert_data, indent=2)}")
                      # Process alert (send to external system, etc.)
                      # Your custom logic here
                      self.send_response(200)
                      self.end_headers()
                      self.wfile.write(b'OK')
                  except Exception as e:
                      logging.error(f"Error processing alert: {e}")
                      self.send_response(500)
                      self.end_headers()
          server = HTTPServer(('0.0.0.0', 8080), AlertWebhook)
          logging.info("Webhook server started on port 8080")
          server.serve_forever()
        ports:
        - containerPort: 8080
          name: http
---
apiVersion: v1
kind: Service
meta
  name: alert-webhook
  namespace: monitoring
spec:
  selector:
    app: alert-webhook
  ports:
  - port: 80
    targetPort: 8080
---
kubectl apply -f deployments/monitoring/webhook-config.yaml
kubectl apply -f deployments/monitoring/webhook-server.yaml




Microsoft Teams Integration

# deployments/monitoring/teams-config.yaml
apiVersion: v1
kind: Secret
meta
  name: teams-config
  namespace: monitoring
type: Opaque
stringData:
  teams-webhook-url: "https://outlook.office.com/webhook/YOUR/TEAMS/WEBHOOK"
  # Use webhook receiver with custom template
  teams.yaml: |
    receivers:
    - name: 'teams-notifications'
      webhook_configs:
      - url_file: /etc/alertmanager/secrets/teams-webhook-url
        send_resolved: true
        # Teams-compatible JSON payload
        http_config:
          headers:
            Content-Type: 'application/json'
---
kubectl apply -f deployments/monitoring/teams-config.yaml

Deploy All Dashboards
bash -11 lines

# Create ConfigMap with all dashboards
kubectl create configmap grafana-dashboards \
  --from-file=deployments/grafana/dashboards/ \
  -n monitoring \
  --dry-run=client -o yaml | kubectl apply -f -
# Label for auto-import
kubectl label configmap grafana-dashboards \
  -n monitoring \
  grafana_dashboard=1
# Restart Grafana to load dashboards
kubectl rollout restart deployment -n monitoring prometheus-operator-grafana

6:01 PM
Loki is a log aggregation system that allows you to store and query logs from your applications and infrastructure. It's designed to be cost-effective, horizontally scalable, and highly available, making it a great option for managing logs. Loki is also inspired by Prometheus and is often used with Grafana for easy exploration and visualization of logs.
